# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [QR-Recursive Compression of Volume Integral Equations for Electromagnetic Scattering by Large Metasurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10586)
*Vincenzo Mottola,Antonello Tamburrino,Luca Bergamaschi,Andrea G. Chiariello,Emanuele Corsaro,Carlo Forestiere,Guglielmo Rubinacci,Salvatore Ventre*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合QR分解压缩方案与体积积分方程方法的新型数值计算框架，用于快速高效地模拟大规模超表面（metasurfaces）的电磁散射问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超表面由大量相互作用的亚波长散射体组成，具有多尺度（multiscale）特性，这使得数值求解变得极具挑战性。需要开发高效的计算方法以应对实际应用中包含数千个粒子的超表面建模需求。

Method: 提出了一种基于QR分解的定制化压缩方案，与体积积分方程（volume integral equation）方法相结合。该方法利用阵列的几何结构设计了适当的预处理器（preconditioner），构建了一个快速准确的迭代求解器（iterative solver）。

Result: 数值算例证明了该方法在高效建模由数千个粒子组成的超表面方面的有效性，实现了快速且准确的电磁散射计算。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种结合QR分解压缩与体积积分方程的迭代方法，为解决大规模超表面电磁散射的多尺度计算难题提供了有效的数值解决方案。

Abstract: In this paper, a novel QR decomposition-based compression scheme is combined with a volume integral equations method for the fast and efficient numerical computation of the scattering of electromagnetic fields from large scale metasurfaces, via an iterative approach.
  The underlying problem is of a multiscale nature. Indeed, these metasurfaces are made of a large collection of interacting sub-wavelength scatterers, thus making the numerical computation of the solution very challenging.
  More specifically, the paper proposes a tailored version of a QR decomposition-based compression for a volume integral equation, together with a proper preconditioner that exploits the geometrical structure of the array, in order to achieve a fast and accurate iterative solver, in view of realistic applications. Numerical examples prove the effectiveness of the method in efficiently modeling metasurfaces made by thousands of particles.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.supr-con'></div>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Persistent short-range charge correlations revealed by ultrafast melting of electronic order in YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{6+x}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10486)
*C. Seo,L. Shen,A. N. Petsch,S. Wandel,V. Esposito,J. D. Koralek,G. L. Dakovski,M-F. Lin,S. P. Moeller,W. F. Schlotter,A. H. Reid,M. P. Minitti,R. Liang,D. Bonn,W. Hardy,A. Damascelli,C. Giannetti,E. H. da Silva Neto,J. J. Turner,F. Boschini,G. Coslovich*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用时间分辨共振X射线散射技术，揭示了YBa₂Cu₃O₆.₆₇中电荷密度波（CDW）的光诱导动力学，发现长程和短程CDW共存且对光激发具有不同响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDW）在铜氧化物超导体的复杂相图中普遍存在，同时表现出短程和长程关联。理解这些关联的动力学特性对于揭示量子材料中的电子有序机制至关重要。

Method: 采用时间分辨共振X射线散射（time-resolved resonant X-ray scattering）技术，研究YBa₂Cu₃O₆.₆₇中CDW的光诱导动力学，通过不同激发通量下的响应来区分共存的有序相。

Result: 发现激发阈值（Φ_C ≈ 65 μJ/cm²）以上时，长程CDW消失，仅保留短程关联的CDW峰。超快光激发在≈0.2 ps内揭示残余短程CDW关联，而长程CDW相干性在≈0.6 ps内恢复，但峰强度仍部分抑制。

Conclusion: 长程关联的崩溃由电子过程驱动，而短程关联具有不同的时间尺度和对光激发的刚性。该方法确立了超快X射线散射作为解耦量子材料中共存密度波和关联的有效工具。

Abstract: Charge density waves (CDW) are ubiquitous in the complex phase diagram of cuprate superconductors and exhibit both short- and long-range correlations. Using time-resolved resonant X-ray scattering, we investigate the photo-induced dynamics of CDW in YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{6.67}$. We discover an excitation threshold ($Φ$$_\mathrm{C}$ $\approx$ 65 $μ$J/cm$^2$) above which long-range CDW disappear, revealing a persistent CDW peak with short-range correlation length. Ultrafast photo-excitation promptly uncovers this residual short-range CDW correlations, appearing within $\approx$ 0.2 ps. Long-range CDW coherence recovers within $\approx$ 0.6 ps, while the peak intensity remains partially suppressed. We rationalize the dichotomic behavior in the fluence and temporal dependencies as the signature of two coexisting CDW peaks, arising from short- and long-range correlations, which we disentangle through their distinct response to photo-excitation. We provide evidence that the collapse of long-range correlations is driven by an electronic process, while short-range correlations are characterized by distinct timescales and stiffness against photo-excitation. This approach establishes ultrafast X-ray scattering as an effective tool for disentangling coexisting density waves and correlations in quantum materials.

</details>


### [3] [Pauli-limited upper critical field and anisotropic depairing effect of La2.82Sr0.18Ni2O7 superconducting thin film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10717)
*Ke Wang,Maosen Wang,Wei Wei,Bo Hao,Mengqin Liu,Qiaochao Xiang,Xin Zhou,Qiang Hou,Yue Sun,Zengwei Zhu,Sheng Li,Yuefeng Nie,Zhixiang Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过高场输运测量，揭示了La2.82Sr0.18Ni2O7外延薄膜的上临界场和超导各向异性特征。研究发现，在低温下，面内上临界场受到自旋顺磁对破缺的强烈抑制并接近泡利极限，而面外上临界场基本不受影响，导致各向异性比降低，证实了薄膜中的超导性是本质上的三维体相超导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐外延薄膜的上临界场和超导各向异性特性，特别是理解自旋顺磁效应如何影响高场超导相图。通过分析La2.82Sr0.18Ni2O7薄膜的超导行为，可以揭示其从二维特征向三维体相超导的转变过程。

Method: 采用外延生长的La2.82Sr0.18Ni2O7薄膜样品，其超导转变温度Tc=31.6 K。通过高场输运测量分析上临界场特性，并测量相干长度随温度的变化。特别关注面内(ab)和面外(c)方向的上临界场行为，以及自旋顺磁对破缺效应的影响。

Result: 研究发现薄膜在Tc附近表现出厚度限制的二维特征，但随着冷却，面外相干长度减小至低于6 nm样品厚度（对应3个晶胞），表明向三维体相超导的转变。上临界场各向异性比γ~1.34较小，与体相Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐相当。低温下Hc2(ab)受自旋顺磁对破缺强烈抑制并接近泡利极限（Hc2(Pauli)=58 T），而Hc2(c)基本不受影响。

Conclusion: 各向异性的泡利限制解释了上临界场各向异性的降低，支持了薄膜中超导性是本质上三维体相超导的结论。研究强调了自旋顺磁效应在塑造Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐高场超导相图中的重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate the upper critical field and superconducting anisotropy of epitaxial La2.82Sr0.18Ni2O7 thin films, which show a sharp superconducting transition at Tc=31.6 K. Near Tc, superconductivity exhibits thickness-limited two-dimensional characteristics. Upon cooling, the out-of-plane coherence length decreases below the sample thickness of 6 nm, corresponding to a 3-unit-cell film, indicating a crossover to intrinsic three-dimensional bulk superconductivity. High-field transport measurements reveal large upper critical fields with a small anisotropy ratio gama~1.34, comparable to bulk Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates. At low temperatures, the in-plane (ab) upper critical field Hc2(ab) is strongly suppressed by spin-paramagnetic pair breaking and approaches the Pauli limit (Hc2(Pauli)=58 T), while Hc2(c) remains largely unaffected. This anisotropic Pauli limitation accounts for the reduced upper critical field anisotropy and supports the conclusion that superconductivity in these films is fundamentally three-dimensional bulk like. Our results highlight the essential role of spin-paramagnetic effects in shaping the high-field superconducting phase diagram of Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates.

</details>


### [4] [Gap structure and phase diagram of twisted bilayer cuprates from a microscopic perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10865)
*Siddhant Panda,Andreas Kreisel,Laura Fanfarillo,Peter Hirschfeld*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过紧束缚晶格模型计算，分析了扭转双层铜氧化物超导体中时间反演对称性破缺态与范霍夫奇点位置的关系，并计算了约瑟夫森临界电流的角度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自2021年Can等人预测扭转双层铜氧化物超导体中存在时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）的d+id'态以来，多个实验尝试检测该态但结果相互矛盾。目前尚不清楚样品差异或实验条件如何解释这些分歧。

Method: 采用具有唯象层间隧穿（phenomenological interlayer tunneling）的紧束缚晶格模型（tight-binding lattice model）进行计算，研究序参量随扭转角度、层间隧穿、掺杂浓度和温度的变化关系。

Result: 发现TRSB态与正常态中范霍夫奇点（Van Hove singularity）的位置相关，该位置不仅随掺杂浓度变化，也随隧穿强度变化。识别出两种与面内d+id'和d+is序名义上一致的相，但它们在双层对称操作下具有意外的变换性质。计算了约瑟夫森临界电流（Josephson critical current），特别考察了不同隧穿强度下的角度依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了对扭转双层铜氧化物超导体中TRSB态的理论理解框架，并基于计算结果讨论了现有实验观测的潜在解释。

Abstract: Since the prediction of a time-reversal symmetry breaking (TRSB) $d+id^\prime$ state in twisted bilayer cuprate superconductors by Can et al. in 2021, several experiments have attempted to detect this state, yielding conflicting results. At present, it is not clear which differences in samples or experimental conditions might explain these discrepancies. In this work, we perform a tight-binding lattice model calculation with phenomenological interlayer tunneling, examining the order parameter as a function of twist angle, interlayer tunneling, doping, and temperature. We observe the TRSB state to be correlated to the position of the Van Hove singularity in the normal state which changes not only as a function of doping but also the tunneling strength. Two such phases are identified as nominally consistent with in-plane $d+id'$ and $d+is$ order, but with unexpected transformation properties under bilayer symmetry operations. We calculate the Josephson critical current, in particular examining the angle dependence for various tunneling strengths. Finally, we discuss the existing experiments in the context of our results.

</details>


### [5] [Supercurrents in Josephson junctions with chiral molecular potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10925)
*Oleg Kuliashov,Alberto Cappellaro,Oded Millo,Yossi Paltiel,Mikhail Lemeshko,Ragheed Alhyder*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了手性分子势对超导约瑟夫森结中相位相干输运的影响，发现自旋超流对手性表现出显著依赖，而电荷电流则相对不敏感，为分子手性检测提供了相位敏感平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索手性分子势如何影响超导约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）中的相位相干输运，特别是将手性分子功能集成到超导自旋电子器件中的可能性。

Method: 采用Bogoliubov-de Gennes紧束缚框架，构建了由吸附手性分子功能化的SNS结模型，其中分子产生的静电梯度在正常区域诱导了自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）。

Result: 在对称零场构型中，平衡电荷电流-相位关系对手性不敏感；而自旋超流表现出显著的手性依赖响应，相反对映体产生不同且各向异性的自旋极化约瑟夫森电流。手性对比度可通过分子取向和诱导自旋轨道耦合强度等参数增强，且手性依赖特征在远低于超导临界温度的温度范围内持续存在。

Conclusion: 研究确立了约瑟夫森干涉测量作为检测分子手性的相位敏感且易于实现的平台，并突显了自旋极化超导输运作为将手性分子功能集成到超导自旋电子器件中的有前景途径。

Abstract: The influence of chiral molecular potentials on phase-coherent transport in superconducting Josephson junctions is investigated. Within a Bogoliubov-de Gennes tight-binding framework, an SNS junction functionalized by adsorbed chiral molecules is modeled, where electrostatic gradients generated by the molecules induce spin-orbit coupling in the normal region. The equilibrium charge current-phase relation is found to remain largely insensitive to molecular chirality in symmetric, zero-field configurations. In contrast, the spin supercurrent exhibits a pronounced chirality-dependent response, with opposite enantiomers producing distinct and anisotropic spin-polarized Josephson currents. The resulting handedness contrast can be enhanced through control parameters such as molecular orientation and the strength of the induced spin-orbit coupling. The temperature dependence of these currents further shows that the chirality-dependent signatures persist across a range of temperatures well below the superconducting critical temperature. These results establish Josephson interferometry as a phase-sensitive and accessible platform for detecting molecular chirality and highlight spin-polarized superconducting transport as a promising route toward integrating chiral molecular functionality into superconducting spintronic devices.

</details>


### [6] [Ab-initio superfluid weight and superconducting penetration depth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10955)
*Kaja H. Hiorth,Martin Gutierrez-Amigo,Théo Cavignac,Kristjan Haule,Miguel A. L. Marques,Päivi Törmä*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory）能带结构和布洛赫波函数计算零温平均场超流权重（superfluid weight）的高效计算框架，该框架可用于大规模筛选超导候选材料和探索非常规超导体中的量子几何效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习和高通量筛选方法在超导体发现中需要既包含基本物理意义又保持计算可行性的描述符。超流权重是理想的描述符，因为它是超导性的先决条件，决定了二维材料中的磁穿透深度和Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless转变温度，可能通过相位相干限制非常规超导体的临界温度，并揭示超电流输运中的量子几何贡献。

Method: 开发了一个计算高效的框架，用于从密度泛函理论（density functional theory）能带结构和布洛赫波函数（Bloch wavefunctions）计算均匀配对的零温平均场超流权重。该方法分别评估了来自能带曲率的常规贡献和来自量子几何（quantum geometry）的几何贡献。

Result: 通过计算几种常规超导体（Al、Pb、Nb、MgB₂、LuRu₃B₂和YRu₃B₂）的伦敦穿透深度（London penetration depths）验证了该方法，在考虑了非局域修正、强耦合效应和样品质量后，与实验结果吻合良好。在这些宽带材料中，常规贡献比几何贡献高出几个数量级，符合预期。

Conclusion: 该计算框架为大规模筛选超导候选材料和探索非常规超导体中的量子几何效应提供了基础，有助于加速超导材料的发现和理解。

Abstract: Machine learning and high-throughput screening approaches to superconductor discovery require physically meaningful descriptors that capture essential physics while remaining computationally tractable. The superfluid weight is an ideal descriptor as it is a prerequisite for superconductivity, determines the magnetic penetration depth and the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition temperature in two-dimensional materials, may limit the critical temperature in unconventional superconductors through phase coherence, and reveals quantum geometric contributions to supercurrent transport. We develop a computationally efficient framework for calculating the zero-temperature, mean-field superfluid weight for uniform pairing from density functional theory band structures and Bloch wavefunctions. We separately evaluate the conventional contribution from band curvature and the geometric contribution from quantum geometry. To validate the method, we calculate London penetration depths for a few conventional superconductors (Al, Pb, Nb, MgB$_2$, LuRu$_3$B$_2$ and YRu$_3$B$_2$) and find good agreement with experiment after accounting for nonlocal corrections, strong-coupling effects, and sample quality.
  The conventional contribution dominates by orders of magnitude in these wide-band materials, as expected. This framework provides a foundation for large-scale screening of superconducting candidates and exploring quantum geometric effects in unconventional superconductors.

</details>


<div id='physics.plasm-ph'></div>

# physics.plasm-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Beam-Plasma Collective Oscillations in Intense Charged-Particle Beams: Dielectric Response Theory, Langmuir Wave Dispersion, and Unsupervised Detection via Prometheus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10457)
*Brandon Yee,Wilson Collins,Michael Iofin,Jiayi Fu*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了中能（10-100 MeV）强流带电粒子束中束-等离子体集体振荡的理论与计算框架。理论部分推导了Lindhard介电函数和RPA极化张量，证明了临界密度以上无阻尼朗缪尔波的存在；计算部分使用beta-VAE模型验证了理论预测，所有六项验证均通过。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究中能强流带电粒子束中的束-等离子体集体振荡现象，旨在建立理论框架并验证相关预测。该研究关注临界密度以上无阻尼波模式的存在、空间电荷效应导致的异常束展宽，以及这些现象在现有中能束设施中的可观测性。

Method: 研究分为两部分：第一部分基于Vlasov-Poisson系统建立动力学场论，推导Lindhard介电函数和随机相位近似（RPA）极化张量，分析三种束分布函数；第二部分使用名为Prometheus的beta-VAE模型，训练于粒子网格（PIC）束模拟的静态结构因子数据S(q)，验证理论预测。

Result: 理论分析证明了临界密度n_c以上存在无阻尼朗缪尔波模式，朗道阻尼在粒子-空穴连续谱以上消失。等离子体频率Ω_p²由f求和规则固定，与分布形状无关。空间电荷效应导致√(n-n_c)起始的异常束展宽和q=2k_F处的Friedel振荡。所有六项验证检查均通过，beta-VAE成功检测到集体等离子体振荡起始并解析了Kohn异常。

Conclusion: 束-等离子体转变通过重整化群分析属于三维Ising普适类。理论预测的特征——密度可调的等离子体共振、√(n-n_c)起始的异常束展宽和Friedel振荡——在现有中能束设施中均可观测。研究建立了完整的理论框架并通过计算验证了其有效性。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical and computational framework for beam-plasma collective oscillations in intense charged-particle beams at intermediate energies (10-100 MeV). In Part I, we formulate a kinetic field theory governed by the Vlasov-Poisson system, deriving the Lindhard dielectric function and random phase approximation (RPA) polarization tensor for three beam distribution functions. We prove via the dielectric function epsilon(omega,q)=0 the existence of undamped Langmuir wave modes above a critical beam density n_c, obtain explicit beam-plasma dispersion relations, and show that Landau damping vanishes above the particle-hole continuum. The plasma frequency Omega_p^2 = ne^2/(m*epsilon_0) is fixed by the f-sum rule independently of distribution shape; higher dispersion coefficients depend on velocity moments. Space charge effects drive anomalous beam broadening with sqrt(n-n_c) onset and Friedel oscillations at q=2k_F. The beam-plasma transition belongs to the 3D Ising universality class via renormalization group analysis. In Part II, we validate these predictions using Prometheus, a beta-VAE trained on static structure factor data S(q) from particle-in-cell (PIC) beam simulations. Prometheus detects collective plasma oscillation onset in Gaussian and uniform distributions, confirms their absence in the degenerate Fermi gas (n_c -> 0), and resolves the Kohn anomaly at q=2k_F. Dispersion analysis of S(q,omega) from PIC simulations verifies the distribution-independent Omega_p predicted by the f-sum rule. All six validation checks pass. Predicted signatures -- density-tunable plasma resonances at omega_p proportional to sqrt(n), anomalous beam broadening with sqrt(n-n_c) onset, and Friedel oscillations -- are accessible at existing intermediate-energy beam facilities.

</details>


### [8] [Magnetohydrodynamics in turbulent dynamo regime: the stability problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10683)
*Michal Hnatič,Tomáš Lučivjanský,Lukáš Mižišin,Yurii Molotkov nd Andrei Ovsiannikov*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Martin-Siggia-Rose-De Dominicis-Janssen形式下研究随机螺线磁流体动力学，重点关注空间镜像对称性（parity symmetry）被显式破坏时的系统稳定性。研究发现，螺旋强迫（helical forcing）下，单粒子不可约磁响应函数在单圈水平已包含旋度型贡献，该贡献在红外极限主导裸电阻项，导致平凡态$\langle \mathbf{b} \rangle = \mathbf{0}$指数不稳定。通过自洽性条件分析，证明对于任何物理可接受的泵浦函数（pumping function），模型仅存在奇异解，先前关于有限$\mathbf{B}_0$的结论源于渐近展开的不一致截断。最终提出在随机感应方程中加入裸旋度项可实现自发对称破缺稳定，为螺旋湍流磁流体动力学中的大尺度平均场生成（湍流发电机，turbulent dynamo）提供了可行的场论描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究随机螺线磁流体动力学（stochastic solenoidal magnetohydrodynamics）在空间镜像对称性（parity symmetry）被显式破坏时的稳定性问题。重点关注螺旋强迫（helical forcing）下系统如何通过自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）实现稳定，以及这种机制是否能为湍流发电机（turbulent dynamo）提供有效的场论描述。

Method: 采用场论的Martin-Siggia-Rose-De Dominicis-Janssen形式体系（formalism），在螺旋强迫条件下分析单粒子不可约磁响应函数（one-particle-irreducible magnetic response function）。通过推导平均磁场$\mathbf{B}_0$的自洽性条件（self-consistency condition），检验不同泵浦函数（pumping function）下的解的性质，包括标准幂律和"质量型"泵浦函数。

Result: 研究发现，在螺旋强迫下，单圈水平的磁响应函数已包含旋度型贡献，该贡献在红外极限主导裸电阻项，导致平凡态$\langle \mathbf{b} \rangle = \mathbf{0}$指数不稳定。对于任何物理可接受的泵浦函数形式，模型仅存在奇异解（singular solution）。先前关于有限$\mathbf{B}_0$的结论被证明源于渐近展开的不一致截断（inconsistent truncation of asymptotic expansions）。

Conclusion: 要实现系统的自发对称破缺稳定，需要在随机感应方程中加入裸旋度项（bare curl term），这一项自然源于欧姆定律（Ohm's law）的宇称破坏修正。通过这一修正，自发对称破缺稳定机制成为螺旋湍流磁流体动力学中大尺度平均场生成（湍流发电机）的可行场论描述。

Abstract: This paper investigates stochastic solenoidal magnetohydrodynamics within the field-theoretic Martin-Siggia-Rose-De Dominicis-Janssen formalism, with a specific focus on the stability of the system when spatial mirror (parity) symmetry is explicitly broken. Under helical forcing, the one-particle-irreducible magnetic response function already at one loop contains a curl-type contribution that dominates the bare resistive term in the infrared limit, leading to exponential instability of the trivial state $\langle \mathbf{b} \rangle = \mathbf{0}$. We re-examine a stabilization mechanism proposed
  in [L. T. Adzhemyan, et al., Theor. Math. Phys. 72, 940-950 (1987)], in which the system evolves into a phase with a dynamically spontaneously broken rotational symmetry and a generated mean magnetic field
  $\langle \mathbf{b} \rangle = \mathbf{B}_0$. By deriving a self-consistency condition for $ \mathbf{B}_0$, we show that for any physically admissible (infrared) form of the pumping function, the model admits only a singular solution. We illustrate this with the standard power-law and "massive" pumping functions. We further show
  that previous claims of a finite $ \mathbf{B}_0$ arose from an inconsistent truncation of asymptotic expansions. We argue that a consistent physical resolution requires including
  a bare curl term in the stochastic induction equation, which naturally arises from a parity-violating modification of Ohm's law. With this modification, stabilization of the system by spontaneous symmetry breaking becomes a viable field-theoretic description of large-scale mean-field generation (turbulent dynamo) in helical turbulent
  magnetohydrodynamics.

### [9] [Effective theory of surface oscillations in self-bound superfluid droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10304)
*Jun Mitsuhashi,Keisuke Fujii,Masaru Hongo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究推导了真空中球形超流体液滴小振幅表面振荡的低能动力学，建立了包含粒子数约束的有效作用量，确定了表面模式的稳定性条件，并将理论应用于弱相互作用双组分玻色混合物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究球形超流体液滴在真空中的表面振荡低能动力学，旨在建立适用于具有自由界面的非相对论性超流体的普适描述，独立于微观细节。

Method: 从超流体声子（superfluid phonons）的有效场论出发，推导了在固定粒子数约束下控制表面振荡的有效作用量（effective action），确定了不同角动量量子数ℓ对应的本征频率ωℓ。

Result: 发现本征频率依赖于表征表面张力与体压缩能比值的无量纲参数，确定了呼吸模（breathing mode，ℓ=0）变得机械不稳定的临界值，并证明当表面张力足够小时所有多极表面模式（ℓ≥2）进入低能区。

Conclusion: 在低能区内对表面振荡进行了量子化，其量子对应涟漪子（ripplons），建立了满足角动量选择规则的多涟漪子态，并将形式体系应用于弱相互作用双组分玻色混合物（two-component Bose mixture）实现的自束缚超流体液滴。

Abstract: We investigate the low-energy dynamics of small-amplitude surface oscillations of spherical superfluid droplets in vacuum. Starting from the effective field theory of superfluid phonons, we derive an effective action governing the surface oscillations under a fixed particle-number constraint. The normal-mode eigenfrequencies $ω_{\ell}$ for each angular momentum quantum number $\ell$ are determined and shown to depend on a dimensionless parameter measuring the ratio of surface tension to bulk compressibility energy. We identify a critical value of this parameters at which the breathing mode ($\ell = 0$) becomes mechanically unstable, and show that all multipole surface modes with $\ell \geq 2$ enter the low-energy regime when the surface tension is sufficiently small. Within this regime, we further quantize the surface oscillations, whose quanta correspond to ripplons, allowing the construction of general multi-ripplon states obeying angular-momentum selection rules. We also apply our formalism to a concrete example: a weakly interacting two-component Bose mixture realizing a self-bound superfluid droplet. The resulting description is universal in the sense that it applies to surface dynamics of generic nonrelativistic superfluids with a free interface, independent of microscopic details.

### [10] [Realizing the Emery Model in Optical Lattices for Quantum Simulation of Cuprates and Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11037)
*Hannah Lange,Liyang Qiu,Robin Groth,Andreas von Haaren,Luca Muscarella,Titus Franz,Immanuel Bloch,Fabian Grusdt,Philipp M. Preiss,Annabelle Bohrdt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用超冷原子量子模拟平台实现埃默里模型（Emery model）的方案，旨在探索铜氧化物和无限层镍酸盐中高温超导的微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物高温超导的微观起源是凝聚态物理的核心开放问题之一。实验和理论证据表明，单带费米-哈伯德模型（single-band Fermi-Hubbard model）可能无法完全捕捉铜氧化物的超导特性，因此需要重新审视其原始来源——铜氧平面的三带埃默里模型（Emery model）。

Method: 提出并分析了一种量子模拟方案，利用当前超冷原子量子模拟平台实现与铜氧化物和无限层镍酸盐相关的埃默里模型参数区域。具体方案是设计具有叠加排斥势图案的二维光学晶格（two-dimensional optical lattice）。

Result: 该方案能够研究埃默里模型在铜氧化物和无限层镍酸盐相关参数区域下的低温性质，其系统尺寸对当前数值方法具有挑战性。这为使用超冷原子量子模拟器进行真实材料模拟铺平了道路。

Conclusion: 该研究为利用超冷原子量子模拟平台探索非常规超导体物理提供了新途径，有助于更好地理解铜氧化物和无限层镍酸盐中高温超导的微观机制。

Abstract: The microscopic origin of high-temperature superconductivity in cuprates remains one of the central open questions in condensed matter physics. Growing experimental and theoretical evidence suggests that the bare single-band Fermi-Hubbard model may not fully capture properties of cuprates such as superconductivity, motivating us to revisit the canonical three-band model of the copper-oxide planes - the Emery model - from which the single-band counterpart was originally derived. Here, we propose and analyze a quantum simulation scheme for realizing the Emery model in regimes relevant to cuprates and infinite-layer nickelates with today's ultracold atom quantum simulation platforms, enabling the exploration of the three-band physics on system sizes that are challenging for current numerical methods. Specifically, we show that a two-dimensional optical lattice with a superimposed pattern of repulsive potentials can be designed to study low-temperature properties for variable parameter regimes of the Emery model relevant to cuprates as well as infinite-layer nickelates. Our results pave the way for real material simulations with ultracold atom quantum simulators and a better understanding of the physics of unconventional superconductors.

### [11] [The propensity for disobedience: Rule-breaking, compliance and social phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10221)
*Nuno Crokidakis*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个数学模型来描述社会中违规行为的持续性，如交通违规、忽视法律限制等。模型显示，在正反馈机制下系统呈现双稳态和一级相变特征，而负反馈则导致连续相变，揭示了执法力度、社会容忍度等因素如何推动系统跨越临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解社会中违规行为（如交通违规、法律限制忽视等）持续存在的机制，特别是要解释在弱制度环境下社会秩序的脆弱性，并为促进合规提供理论依据。

Method: 采用基于复制者动力学（replicator-type dynamics）的数学模型，效用函数包含个体收益、制度惩罚和社会制裁。在一般框架下分析了两种不同社会反馈机制（正反馈与负反馈）的模型。

Result: 正反馈机制下系统呈现双稳态（bistability），广泛合规与广泛违规作为稳定平衡态，状态转换呈现不连续的一级相变（first-order phase transition）。负反馈机制下则呈现连续相变（continuous phase transition），由违规集体成本增加驱动。

Conclusion: 研究结果为弱制度下社会秩序的脆弱性提供了理论解释，并揭示了通过调整执法力度、社会容忍度或感知收益来推动系统跨越临界点（tipping points）的可能途径，为促进合规提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We develop a mathematical model to describe the persistence of rule-breaking behaviors in societies, such as traffic violations, disregard for legal restrictions and other forms of noncompliance. Using a replicator-type dynamics with utility functions incorporating individual benefits, institutional punishment and social sanctions, we first built a general formulation of the system. Within this framework, we analyze two distinct models differing in the nature of social feedback. In the presence of positive feedback, the system exhibits bistability, with widespread compliance and widespread violation as stable equilibria, and the transition between these states occurs discontinuously once a critical threshold is crossed, resembling a first-order phase transition. By contrast, when negative feedback is present, the population undergoes a continuous phase transition between compliant and noncompliant collective states, driven by an increasing collective cost of rule-breaking. Numerical simulations and analytical results illustrate how changes in enforcement, social tolerance or perceived benefits can shift the system across tipping points. The results provide a theoretical explanation for the fragility of social order under weak institutions and highlight possible pathways to promote compliance.

### [12] [Topological structure of the entanglement radius of Yang-Mills flux tubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10255)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用格点场论方法，考虑纠缠区域V的几何构型，其中区域切割通量管的长度与纠缠半径ξ₀具有相同量级，以此研究色通量管纠缠半径的拓扑结构特性。

Result: 研究进一步证实了纠缠半径ξ₀的存在性，该物理尺度对应于通量管的本征厚度，只有当纠缠区域完全切断通量管时，色自由度才会贡献非零的通量管纠缠熵，并获得了关于色通量管纠缠半径拓扑结构的详细新信息。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了先前研究arXiv:2601.17199的结论，通过分析纠缠区域尺寸与纠缠半径相当的特殊几何构型，深化了对色通量管纠缠半径拓扑结构的理解，为杨-米尔斯理论中通量管纠缠性质提供了新的物理洞察。

Abstract: We expand on recent work arXiv:2601.17199 demonstrating the existence of a novel entanglement radius $ξ_0$ characterizing flux tube entanglement entropy (FTE$^2$) in (2+1)D Yang-Mills theory. This physical scale corresponds to the intrinsic thickness of the flux tube that must be fully severed by an entangling region for color degrees of freedom in the flux tube to contribute non-zero FTE$^2$. We consider here geometries of the entanglement region $V$ on the lattice where the length of the region cross-cutting the flux tube is of the same magnitude as $ξ_0$. Our results further the conclusions of arXiv:2601.17199 by adding detailed new information on the topological structure of the entanglement radius of color flux tubes.

### [13] [A Non-Foster Superconducting Broadband Matching Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10039)
*Andrew K. Yi,Pamela Stark,Chelsea Bartram*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）的非线性电感特性构建宽带阻抗匹配网络，以克服传统线性、时不变、无源电路在增益-带宽上的固有折衷，从而提高轴子（axion）暗物质探测的扫描速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子作为暗物质（dark matter）的有力候选者，会转化为未知频率的微弱电磁信号。理想的轴子探测器需要在保持高灵敏度的同时不牺牲带宽，而传统线性、时不变、无源电路存在固有的增益-带宽折衷问题，这是高能粒子物理领域长期存在的挑战。

Method: 提出一种利用约瑟夫森结构建阻抗匹配网络（impedance matching network）的电路方案。通过偏置约瑟夫森结使其呈现负电感（negative inductance），能够抵消几何电感（geometric inductance），其作用类似于电容器但工作频率范围更宽。

Result: 该电路方案能够克服传统线性电路的增益-带宽约束（gain-bandwidth constraints），有望显著提高轴子搜索的扫描速率（scan rate）。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森结在宽带阻抗匹配中的应用为解决高能粒子物理中长期存在的探测难题提供了潜在解决方案，突破了传统被动电路的性能限制。

Abstract: The nonlinear inductance of the Josephson junction has enabled the development of a wide range of continuous-variable amplifiers and qubit-based devices with unprecedented sensitivity. We present an alternative use of the Josephson junction in the context of broadband impedance matching. The idea poses a potential solution to a longstanding problem in the field of high energy particle physics. The axion, a compelling candidate for the dark matter, converts to a weak electromagnetic signal at an as-yet unknown frequency. As such, the ideal axion detector does not compromise bandwidth for sensitivity, a trade-off intrinsic to all linear, time-invariant and passive circuits. We propose a circuit that uses a Josephson junction in an impedance matching network to overcome these gain-bandwidth constraints and increase the scan rate of axion searches. The Josephson junction can be biased to exhibit negative inductance capable of canceling geometric inductance similar to a capacitor but across a wider frequency range.

### [14] [Model-derived conversion formula for real-time gas monitoring based on chemiresistive sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10036)
*Fernando Massa Fernandes,Benoît Hackens*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于气体调制势垒的物理模型，能够动态地将电阻变化转换为相应气体浓度，解决了传统化学电阻式气体传感器响应慢和恢复慢的主要缺点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统化学电阻式气体传感器（chemiresistive gas sensors）通常使用经验公式进行校准，忽略了吸附动力学和转导过程中的物理现象，导致直接评估气体浓度时存在响应延迟和缓慢恢复的问题。

Method: 首先提出基于气体调制势垒（gas-modulated potential barriers）的物理模型，考虑非平衡动态响应，并推导出原创的转换公式，能够动态地将电阻变化转换为相应气体浓度。

Result: 新策略在基于氧化PbS纳米晶体的化学电阻器上实现了实时NO2气体传感，并在基于聚吡咯/金结的NH3传感中展示了该模型和策略的更广泛应用。

Conclusion: 提出的物理模型和动态转换策略能够消除传统化学电阻式气体传感器的主要缺点，为实时气体传感提供了更准确和快速的方法。

Abstract: Chemiresistive gas sensors transduce gas adsorption into changes in the electrical resistance across a pair of electrodes connected by a sensitive layer of material. This type of sensor is used due to its simple operation, high sensitivity, low cost, and convenience for scaled-up manufacturing of microsized devices. The conversion of the electrical resistance to a corresponding gas concentration is often performed through calibration procedures using empirical formulas, overlooking part of the physical phenomena involved in the process, both on the sorption kinetics and on the transduction. Consequently, a direct evaluation of gas concentration is plagued by the response delays and slow recovery intrinsic to these processes. In contrast to this approach, here we first propose a physical model, based on gas-modulated potential barriers, and considering the out-of-equilibrium dynamic response. Based on this model, we derive an original conversion formula able to dynamically convert the resistance changes into a corresponding gas concentration thus eliminating the main drawback related to slow response and recovery. This new strategy is demonstrated for real-time NO2 gas sensing, using chemiresistors based on oxidized PbS nanocrystals. In addition, the broader application of the proposed model and strategy is demonstrated for NH3 sensing, based on polypyrrole/gold junctions.

### [15] [Development of Implosions of Solutions to the Three-Dimensional Degenerate Compressible Navier-Stokes Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10141)
*Gui-Qiang G. Chen,Lihui Liu,Shengguo Zhu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了多维可压缩Navier-Stokes方程中非线性黏性系数（具有幂律密度依赖性）的情况，发现存在一个依赖于绝热指数（adiabatic exponent）的阈值。当幂指数低于该阈值时，存在一类密度严格为正的光滑初始数据，其对应的光滑解会在原点处发生有限时间坍塌（implosion）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多维可压缩Navier-Stokes方程理论中的一个基本开放问题是：光滑解是否能在有限时间内产生奇异性。对于常黏性系数，已有研究表明存在光滑初始数据会导致密度在原点处爆炸至无穷的有限时间坍塌。然而，当黏性系数线性依赖于密度时（如浅水情况），大范围球对称初始数据的解保持全局正则性。这些结果表明多维解的定性行为对黏性系数结构敏感。

Method: 本文研究具有幂律密度依赖性的非线性黏性系数情况。通过首先推导密度的逐点估计，然后通过精心构造的加权高阶能量估计（weighted high-order energy estimates）和插值不等式（interpolation inequalities）获得速度梯度的空间衰减估计。所得的衰减速率足够快，能够补偿密度的奇异增长，从而实现对黏性项的随时间一致控制，最终导致坍塌形成。

Result: 识别出一个依赖于绝热指数的阈值，对于任何低于该阈值的幂指数，存在一类密度严格为正的光滑初始数据，其对应的光滑解会在原点处发生有限时间坍塌。关键发现是：在此机制下，退化的黏性项不足以抑制驱动坍塌的对流机制（convective mechanism）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，对于具有幂律密度依赖性的非线性黏性系数，存在一个临界阈值，低于该阈值时退化的Navier-Stokes方程无法阻止有限时间坍塌的形成。这进一步证实了多维解的定性行为对黏性系数结构的敏感性，并揭示了退化黏性项在抑制奇异性形成方面的能力限制。

Abstract: A fundamental open problem in the theory of the multidimensional compressible Navier-Stokes equations is whether smooth solutions can develop singularities in finite time. For constant viscosity coefficients, recent remarkable results show that there exist smooth initial data for which the corresponding smooth solutions of the barotropic flow undergo finite-time implosion at the origin, with the density blowing up to infinity. In contrast, when the viscosity coefficients depend linearly on the density (as in the shallow water case), it has been established that, for general large spherically symmetric initial data, the solutions remain globally regular. These results indicate that the qualitative behavior of multidimensional solutions is sensitive to the structure of the viscosity coefficients. In this paper, we investigate the case of nonlinear viscosity coefficients with power-law density dependence. We identify a threshold value, depending on the adiabatic exponent, such that, for any power below this threshold, there exists a class of smooth initial data with strictly positive density for which the corresponding smooth solutions implode in finite time at the origin. The key issue is to show that, in this regime, the degenerate viscous terms are not sufficiently strong to suppress the convective mechanism driving the implosion. Establishing this rigorously is highly nontrivial due to the degenerate structure of the Navier-Stokes equations. To overcome this difficulty, we first derive a pointwise estimate for the density and then obtain spatial decay estimates for the velocity gradient via carefully constructed weighted high-order energy estimates and interpolation inequalities. The resulting decay rate is sufficiently rapid to compensate for the singular growth of the density, leading to uniform-in-time control of the viscous terms and ultimately to the formation of implosion.

</details>


### [16] [Emergent Loewner Dynamics in Slime Mold Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10201)
*Claire David,Aurèle Boussard,Nizare Riane,Michel L. Lapidus,Audrey Dussutour*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本研究通过基于Loewner演化（Loewner evolution）的直接几何分析，首次从活体生长界面重建了Loewner驱动函数，揭示了黏菌生长前沿的布朗运动样共形生长机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立分析生物生长界面的定量框架，探索形态发生（morphogenesis）、随机几何（stochastic geometry）和网络重组（network reorganization）之间的新联系，特别是在不同环境条件下的动态过程。

Method: 采用基于Loewner演化的直接几何分析方法，利用实验获取的时间分辨图像，从扩展的伪足边界重建相关的Loewner驱动函数，并进行统计特性分析。

Result: 重建的驱动函数显示出类似高斯（Gaussian-like）的统计特性；通过分形标度（fractal scaling）推断出扩散参数κ的几何估计；布朗运动诊断（Brownian diagnostics）在重建的驱动信号中得到验证。

Conclusion: 研究首次从活体生长界面明确重建了Loewner驱动函数，揭示了生长前沿出现的布朗运动样共形生长机制（Brownian-like conformal growth regime），表明生长生物体边界在实验可及尺度上展现出与涌现的Loewner动力学一致的统计和几何特性。

Abstract: Growth fronts of slime molds are characterized through a direct geometric analysis based on Loewner evolutions, using experimentally acquired time-resolved images. The associated Loewner driving functions reconstructed from expanding pseudopod boundaries display statistical properties consistent with Gaussian-like behavior.
  A geometric estimate of the diffusivity parameter~$κ$ is inferred from fractal scaling, while Brownian diagnostics are assessed on the reconstructed driving signal.
  These findings show that the boundaries of a growing living organism display statistical and geometric properties consistent with emergent Loewner dynamics over experimentally accessible scales. This study establishes a quantitative framework for analyzing biological growth interfaces and suggests new connections between morphogenesis, stochastic geometry, and network reorganization under varying environmental conditions.
  We provide, to our knowledge, the first explicit reconstruction of a Loewner driving function from a living growth interface, revealing an emergent Brownian-like conformal growth regime at expanding fronts.

### [17] [Local-in-Time Existence of $L^1$ solutions to the Gravity Water Wave Kinetic Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10882)
*Yulin Pan,Xiaoxu Wu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了描述重力水波弱湍流的四波动力学方程的柯西问题。主要贡献包括：在高度非局域区域中建立了碰撞核的严格上界$\mathcal{O}(|k||k_3|)$，改进了现有估计；并利用这一可积性增益证明了$L^1$强解的局部存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究重力水波弱湍流的四波动力学方程（four-wave kinetic equation）的柯西问题。分析的主要数学挑战源于两个方面：碰撞核（collision kernel）在高度非局域区域中的极端代数复杂性，以及在由此产生的奇异积分算子下构造强解。

Method: 首先，在波数满足$|k|, |k_3| \gg |k_1|, |k_2|$的精确区域中重新分析相互作用核（interaction kernel），建立$\mathcal{O}(|k||k_3|)$的严格上界。其次，利用这一关键的可积性增益，结合碰撞算子（collision operator）的精细结构分解，建立$L^1$强解的局部存在性。

Result: 证明了相互作用核的严格上界为$\mathcal{O}(|k||k_3|)$，改进了近期提出的$\mathcal{O}\big((|k||k_3|)^{3/2}\big)$估计，表明在此极限下波相互作用的奇异性更弱。对于初始数据在适当加权的$L^2 \cap L^\infty$空间中的情况，证明了重力水动力学方程的$L^1$强解的局部存在性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了重力水波弱湍流四波动力学方程柯西问题的严格数学框架。所得结果不仅验证了物理学文献中预期的相互作用系数渐近小性，而且证明了$L^1$强解的存在性，这些解严格传播加权$L^2 \cap L^\infty$正则性并守恒动力学模型的基本物理性质。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the Cauchy problem for the four-wave kinetic equation describing the weak turbulence of gravity water waves. The mathematical challenges of this analysis stem primarily from two interrelated aspects: (1) the extreme algebraic complexity of the collision kernel, where controlling its growth in the highly non-local regime constitutes the primary analytical bottleneck, and (2) the construction of strong solutions under the resulting singular integral operators. First, we re-analyze the interaction kernel in this precise regime, where the interacting wave numbers satisfy $|k|, |k_3| \gg |k_1|, |k_2|$. We establish a rigorous upper bound of $\mathcal{O}(|k||k_3|)$, which rigorously verifies the asymptotic smallness of the interaction coefficient anticipated in the physics literature \cite{zakharov2010energy, geogjaev2017numerical, geogjaev2025properties}. Furthermore, this result improves upon the recent $\mathcal{O}\big((|k||k_3|)^{3/2}\big)$ estimate proposed in \cite{waterkernel2024}, demonstrating a strictly milder singularity of wave interactions in this limit. Physically, this regime governs the energy exchange between disparate scales, such as the modulation of short gravity waves by long ocean swells. Second, leveraging this crucial integrability gain alongside a refined structural decomposition of the collision operator, we establish the local-in-time existence of $L^1$ strong solutions to the gravity water kinetic equation for initial data in a suitably weighted $L^2 \cap L^\infty$ space. Specifically, we prove that for any initial data in this class, the resulting $L^1$ strong solution strictly propagates the weighted $L^2 \cap L^\infty$ regularity and conserves the fundamental physical properties of the kinetic model.

</details>


### [18] [Arnold stability and rigidity in Zeitlin's model of hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10993)
*Luca Melzi,Klas Modin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了Zeitlin模型中稳态的Lyapunov稳定性，并揭示了Arnold稳定稳态解需满足的刚性条件，表明该离散化模型对研究二维Euler方程稳态解具有可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zeitlin模型作为二维Euler方程的离散化方法，保留了原方程的几何结构，适合研究动力学定性行为。本文旨在利用Arnold几何方法分析该模型中稳态解的稳定性。

Method: 采用Arnold的几何方法（Arnold's geometric approach）证明Zeitlin模型中稳态的Lyapunov稳定性。论证基于矩阵理论（matrix theory），与二维Euler方程的非线性稳定性分析在概念上不同。

Result: 证明了Zeitlin模型中稳态的Lyapunov稳定性，并发现Arnold稳定稳态解需满足刚性条件，强制描述状态的矩阵具有特定形式。结果与二维Euler方程的已知结论一致。

Conclusion: Zeitlin模型作为数值离散化方法，在研究二维Euler方程的稳态解方面具有可靠性。研究结果暗示了矩阵理论与非线性偏微分方程技术之间存在联系。

Abstract: Zeitlin's model is a discretisation of the 2-D Euler equations that preserves the underlying geometric structure. This feature makes it suitable for studying the qualitative behaviour of the dynamics. Here, we utilise Arnold's geometric approach to prove Lyapunov stability of steady states in Zeitlin's model. Furthermore, we show that such Arnold stable stationary solutions are subject to a rigidity condition that enforces a specific form of the matrix describing the state. Our argument relies on matrix theory and is therefore detached, and conceptually different, from the nonlinear stability analysis as developed for the 2-D Euler equations. Nevertheless, our results concur with those known for the 2-D Euler equations, which hints at links between matrix theory and nonlinear PDE techniques. Furthermore, our results show that the Zeitlin's model, as a numerical discretisation, is reliable for studying stationary solutions.

</details>

### [19] [On the angular localization of gravitational-wave signals by pulsar timing arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10120)
*Stephen R. Taylor*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）中引力波信号定位精度的关键影响因素，推导了Cramér-Rao定位精度的解析表达式，明确了脉冲星与波源角度接近度ξ和脉冲星距离精度σ_L的作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在全面理解影响脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）中引力波信号定位精度的各种因素，特别是脉冲星与波源角度接近度ξ和脉冲星距离测量精度σ_L对定位性能的具体影响机制。

Method: 通过推导Cramér-Rao定位精度的解析表达式，分析地球项（Earth term）与脉冲星项（pulsar term）干涉产生的快速角度振荡效应，以及天线响应梯度信息（antenna response gradient information）的贡献，并考虑脉冲星距离精度不同情况下的定位机制。

Result: 当脉冲星距离精确已知时（σ_L≤λ_GW/(1-cosξ)），提高距离精度可使定位精度按ΔΩ_sky∝σ_L²改善，直至达到衍射极限（diffraction limit）。当距离精度较差时，增加靠近波源的脉冲星数量是改善定位的最佳途径，在小角度极限下ΔΩ_sky∝(∑_αSNR_α²/ξ_α²)^{-1}。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了脉冲星计时阵列引力波定位的两种不同机制：距离精确已知时的衍射极限机制和距离精度较差时的天线响应驱动机制。当前所有PTA连续波搜索采用的相位解耦方案（phase-decoupled scenario）定位性能与天线响应驱动情况相似，且不会随距离精度提高而显著改善。

Abstract: We provide a complete study of the factors influencing gravitational-wave signal localization using pulsar timing arrays. We derive analytical expressions for the Cramér-Rao sky localization precision that delineate the impact of the angular proximity, $ξ$, between the pulsar and the gravitational wave source, and the precision, $σ_L$, with which pulsar distances are known. Interference between the Earth and pulsar terms creates rapid angular oscillations for sky-coordinate Fisher matrix elements that aids localization, which is complemented by more broadly varying antenna response gradient information. The relative importance of these factors depends on whether pulsar distances are known precisely [i.e., $σ_L\leqλ_\mathrm{GW}/(1-\cosξ)$] or imprecisely, respectively. If the former, tightening pulsar distance precisions improves signal localization according to $ΔΩ_\mathrm{sky}\proptoσ_L^2$ until the Earth-pulsar system reaches its diffraction limit. If the latter, localization precision is degraded, but more pulsars in close proximity to the source is the best means of improving. With $α$ indexing pulsars, this scales as $ΔΩ_\mathrm{sky}~\propto~(\sum_α\mathrm{SNR}_α^2/ξ_α^2)^{-1}$ in the small-angle limit of the unmarginalized Fisher matrix, and we derive the analytic generalization to any angle between a pulsar and the source. Finally, we study a scenario where pulsar-term phases are treated as nuisance variables that are unconnected to binary or PTA properties. This phase-decoupled scenario, which is how all PTA continuous wave searches are currently conducted, delivers localization performance similar to the antenna-response--driven case, and does not exhibit significant improvement as pulsar distance precisions are tightened.

</details>


### [20] [Kick matters: The impact of a new recoil model on the retention of hierarchical black-hole remnants in globular clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10170)
*Tousif Islam,Digvijay Wadekar,Konstantinos Kritos*

TL;DR: 本研究采用基于数值相对论和黑洞微扰理论数据构建的先进反冲速度模型gwModel_flow_prec，发现在球状星团中该模型相比传统解析模型能显著提高分级合并残余黑洞的保留概率，并改变分级合并形成的黑洞质量和自旋分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在球状星团（globular clusters）中，分级合并（hierarchical mergers）是形成大质量黑洞（如GW231123）的重要途径。决定合并残余黑洞能否保留在星团环境中参与后续分级合并的关键因素是反冲速度（recoil kick velocity），而目前几乎所有群体合成框架都采用解析模型来估算该速度。

Method: 本研究采用基于数值相对论（numerical-relativity）和黑洞微扰理论（black-hole perturbation-theory）数据构建的先进反冲速度模型gwModel_flow_prec，该模型结合了数据驱动技术如归一化流（normalizing flows）和后牛顿（post-Newtonian）结构。研究同时采用粗略估算和详细的N体模拟（N-body simulations）以及半解析星团模拟（semi-analytical cluster simulations）进行分析。

Result: gwModel_flow_prec模型相比先前使用的解析模型，显著提高了分级合并残余黑洞的保留概率（retention probability），并改变了通过分级合并形成的黑洞质量和自旋分布（mass and spin distribution）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，采用更精确的反冲速度模型对理解球状星团中分级合并过程至关重要，并讨论了这些结果对GW231123等大质量双星系统的意义。

Abstract: In globular clusters, hierarchical mergers are among the most promising pathways to forming massive black holes such as GW231123. A key factor determining whether a merger-remnant black hole will be retained in these environments and thus participate in subsequent hierarchical mergers is the recoil kick velocity. Analytic models for the recoil velocity are currently employed in nearly all population-synthesis frameworks. We instead use a state-of-the-art recoil-kick model gwModel_flow_prec developed from a combination of numerical-relativity and black-hole perturbation-theory data, together with data-driven techniques such as normalizing flows and the post-Newtonian structure of the kick. Employing both back-of-the-envelope estimates and detailed N-body as well as semi-analytical cluster simulations, we show that gwModel_flow_prec leads to a noticeable increase in the retention probability of hierarchical-merger remnants compared to the previously used analytic model and changes the mass and spin distribution of the black holes formed through hierarchical mergers. Additionally, we discuss the implications of our results in the context of massive binaries such as GW231123.

### [21] [Unexpectedly Weak General Relativistic Effects in Strongly Relativistic Tidal Disruption Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10208)
*Ho-Sang Chan,Taeho Ryu,Julian Krolik,Tsvi Piran*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过广义相对论流体动力学模拟发现，强相对论性潮汐瓦解事件（TDEs）的演化过程与弱相对论性TDEs相似：碎片保持高偏心轨道，大部分返回物质位于轨道远心点附近，冲击波而非吸积主导事件能量释放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为当恒星近心点小于约10倍引力半径时，强相对论效应会迅速耗散轨道能量并产生快速盘形成。本研究旨在通过模拟验证这一假设，探究强相对论性TDEs的实际演化过程。

Method: 采用广义相对论流体动力学模拟（general relativistic hydrodynamic simulation），研究围绕10^6太阳质量黑洞的强相对论性TDE。模拟从恒星初始接近开始，跟踪碎片演化至峰值质量返回时间后35天（约23天峰值时间）。

Result: 模拟显示整体演化与弱相对论性TDEs相似：碎片保持高偏心轨道，大部分返回质量位于轨道远心点附近（约初始近心点距离的250倍）。早期冲击波由强相对论性近心点进动（apsidal precession）和近心点喷嘴压缩驱动，但仅持续约一周（约峰值质量返回时间的0.3倍）。流自相互作用增加入流角动量，扩大近心点距离，减弱进动和冲击波，减少能量耗散。

Conclusion: 结合先前对弱相对论性TDEs的研究，结果表明无论相对论效应强度如何，轨道圆化（circularization）本质上可能都是缓慢过程。在光学/紫外光度峰值期间，流动保持高度偏心且延展状态，冲击波而非吸积主导事件能量释放。

Abstract: Tidal disruption events (TDEs) occur when stars are destroyed by supermassive black holes and are among the brightest nuclear transients. It has been thought that strong relativistic effects rapidly dissipate orbital energy and produce prompt disk formation when the stellar pericenter is smaller than $\sim 10$ gravitational radii. Using a general relativistic hydrodynamic simulation of a strongly relativistic TDE around a $10^{6}\,M_{\odot}$ black hole, we find instead that the overall evolution is similar to weakly relativistic TDEs: the debris remains highly eccentric, with most of the returned mass residing near the orbital apocenter ($\sim 250\times$ the initial pericenter distance), and shocks, rather than accretion, power the event. The simulation starts from the initial stellar approach and follows the debris evolution up to $35\,\text{days}$ after the peak mass-return time ($\simeq$ $23\,\text{days}$). Although early shocks driven by strong relativistic apsidal precession and pericenter nozzle compression dissipate orbital energy efficiently, they last only about a week ($\sim 0.3$ of the peak mass-return time). Stream self-interactions increase the incoming stream's angular momentum, thereby expanding its pericenter distance, weakening precession and shocks, and reducing dissipation. These results, along with previous work on weakly relativistic TDEs, suggest that circularization may be intrinsically slow regardless of the strength of relativistic effects, and the flow remains highly eccentric and extended during the peak of optical/UV luminosity.

</details>

### [22] [MITRA: An AI Assistant for Knowledge Retrieval in Physics Collaborations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09800)
*Abhishikth Mallampalli,Sridhara Dasu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了MITRA系统原型，这是一个基于检索增强生成（RAG）的问答系统，专为大型科学合作项目（如CERN的CMS）设计，用于从海量内部文档中检索和回答特定物理分析问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型科学合作项目（如CERN的紧凑μ子螺线管CMS）产生大量内部文档，这些复杂的信息环境对新老研究人员都构成挑战，阻碍知识共享并减缓科学发现速度。

Method: MITRA采用检索增强生成（Retrieval-Augmented Generation, RAG）架构，使用Selenium进行文档自动检索，结合光学字符识别（Optical Character Recognition, OCR）和布局解析进行高保真文本提取。系统采用双层向量数据库架构，先通过摘要识别相关分析，再聚焦完整文档。

Result: 原型系统在真实查询中展现出优于标准基于关键词基线的检索性能。整个框架（从嵌入模型到大语言模型LLM）都在本地部署，确保敏感合作数据的隐私性。

Conclusion: MITRA原型为解决大型实验合作中的信息检索挑战提供了有效方案，未来工作将致力于开发更全面的研究智能体（research agent）。

Abstract: Large-scale scientific collaborations, such as the Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS) at CERN, produce a vast and ever-growing corpus of internal documentation. Navigating this complex information landscape presents a significant challenge for both new and experienced researchers, hindering knowledge sharing and slowing down the pace of scientific discovery. To address this, we present a prototype of MITRA, a Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) based system, designed to answer specific, context-aware questions about physics analyses. MITRA employs a novel, automated pipeline using Selenium for document retrieval from internal databases and Optical Character Recognition (OCR) with layout parsing for high-fidelity text extraction. Crucially, MITRA's entire framework, from the embedding model to the Large Language Model (LLM), is hosted on-premise, ensuring that sensitive collaboration data remains private. We introduce a two-tiered vector database architecture that first identifies the relevant analysis from abstracts before focusing on the full documentation, resolving potential ambiguities between different analyses. We demonstrate the prototype's superior retrieval performance against a standard keyword-based baseline on realistic queries and discuss future work towards developing a comprehensive research agent for large experimental collaborations.

### [23] [ALD Oxidant as A Tuning Knob for Memory Window Expansion in Ferroelectric FETs for Vertical NAND Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10127)
*Ranie Jeyakumar,Prasanna Venkatesan,Lance Fernandes,Salma Soliman,Priyankka Ravikumar,Taeyoung Song,Chengyang Zhang,Woohyun Hwang,Kwangyou Seo,Suhwan Lim,Wanki Kim,Daewon Ha,Shimeng Yu,Suman Datta,Asif Khan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文发现，在铁电场效应晶体管（FeFET）中，用于沉积Al2O3中间层的原子层沉积（ALD）氧化剂选择是调控存储窗口（MW）的关键工艺参数。相比O3，H₂O生长的Al2O3能显著扩大MW，但不同堆叠结构下的保持特性表现不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究主要关注材料选择和堆叠位置对铁电场效应晶体管（ferroelectric FETs, FeFETs）存储窗口（memory window, MW）的影响。本文旨在探索工艺层面的调控参数，特别是原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition, ALD）氧化剂选择对MW工程的作用。

Method: 研究比较了使用H₂O和O3作为氧化剂通过ALD沉积的Al2O3中间层。分析了两种堆叠配置：栅注入（gate-injection, 12/3）结构和隧道电介质（tunnel dielectric, 8/3/8）结构，评估了它们对存储窗口和保持特性的影响。

Result: H₂O生长的Al2O3产生显著更大的存储窗口（7-8 V），而O3仅为4 V。隧道电介质（8/3/8）堆叠在125°C下保持稳健的保持特性至1e4秒，而栅注入（12/3）配置在H₂O情况下表现出明显的保持退化。增强的MW归因于H₂O基ALD相关的更高中间层泄漏。

Conclusion: 氧化剂选择是铁电NAND技术中共同优化存储窗口和保持特性的关键工艺参数。H₂O基ALD能有效扩大MW，但需要根据具体堆叠结构权衡保持特性，为工艺优化提供了新维度。

Abstract: Dielectric inserts are widely used to expand the memory window (MW) in ferroelectric FETs (FeFETs) for vertical NAND applications, with prior efforts focused primarily on material selection and stack positioning. Here, we demonstrate that the ALD oxidant used for the Al2O3 interlayer serves as a process-level tuning knob for MW engineering. H2O-grown Al2O3 yields a significantly larger MW (7-8 V) compared to O3 (4 V) for both gate-injection (12/3) and tunnel dielectric (8/3/8) configurations. While the tunnel dielectric (8/3/8) stack maintains robust retention up to 1e4s at 125C despite the larger MW, the gate-injection (12/3) configuration exhibits pronounced retention degradation for the H2O case. The enhanced MW is attributed to higher interlayer leakage associated with H2O-based ALD. These results establish oxidant choice as a key process parameter for co-optimizing MW and retention in ferroelectric NAND technologies.

Abstract: The quasi-hexagonal phase of the two-dimensional fullerene network (qHPC$_{60}$), recently synthesized, has emerged as a stable carbon-based material with distinct structural and electronic features. In this work, we employed density functional theory (DFT) calculations to investigate the electronic and optical properties of its endohedral derivatives. The encapsulation of nitrogen, cerium, and strontium atoms inside fullerene cages was systematically analyzed at different concentrations. Our results show that encapsulation preserves the semiconducting backbone of pristine qHPC$_{60}$ while introducing localized electronic states that alter the bandgap and enable new transition channels. Nitrogen encapsulation produces intragap states with potential relevance for discrete optical emission, whereas cerium and strontium generate intraband states near the conduction edge. These modifications induce a red shift of the absorption onset into the visible spectrum, accompanied by enhanced refractive and absorptive responses. The robustness of the electronic structure under reduced concentrations indicates that the fully encapsulated limit adequately represents the system. Overall, the findings highlight impurity-endowed qHPC$_{60}$ as a promising platform for optoelectronic and light-harvesting applications.

### [25] [Intertwined Swirling Polarization States in BaTiO$_3$ with Embedded BaZrO$_3$ Nanoregions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10154)

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials embedded with dielectric inclusions offer a unique platform for exploring novel topological polar textures. Using first-principles-based atomistic simulations, we investigate the polarization behavior of a BaTiO$_3$ matrix containing segregated BaZrO$_3$ nanoregions. We demonstrate that the polar texture in three-dimensionally ordered arrays of dielectric inclusions is governed by their size and spacing, revealing three distinct regimes. At large separations, the nanocomposite exhibits bulk-like BaTiO3 phase transitions, while at smaller spacings, interconnected swirling polarization patterns give rise to vortex supercrystal states. We analyze the stabilization mechanisms of these states and show that each regime is characterized by distinct switching behavior. Furthermore, we find that nanocomposites with randomly distributed dielectric inclusions exhibit swirling polarization textures, giving rise to an amorphous network of entangled vortices. Our findings provide new insights into the physics of relaxor ferroelectrics, are consistent with recent experimental observations, and open up new possibilities for designing materials with emergent topological functionalities.

### [26] [Bias in Universal Machine-Learned Interatomic Potentials and its Effects on Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10159)
*Nicolas Wong,Julia H. Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIPs）的微调策略，发现周期性微调相比朴素微调能产生更准确、可泛化的分子动力学模拟，并揭示了模型偏差在微调过程中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine learned interatomic potentials, uMLIPs）因其在周期表中的可迁移性而受到关注，但在域外任务上需要更高精度预测。研究旨在探索微调策略对模型性能的影响，特别是针对分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟中的模型偏差问题。

Method: 研究比较了两种数据生成方法：从多个并行MD轨迹进行朴素微调（naive fine-tuning），以及从单个MD轨迹进行周期性微调（periodic fine-tuning）。通过主成分空间（principal component space）分析非物理行为，并使用Q残差分析（Q-residual analysis）量化外推性能。

Result: 朴素微调产生受约束的数据集，无法准确表示MD模拟，导致下游微调模型在外推时失败。相比之下，周期性微调产生更可泛化和准确的模型，能生成低误差动力学。Q残差分析可作为更大模拟中认知不确定性（epistemic uncertainty）的代理指标。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了uMLIP偏差在微调过程中的作用，强调了多次微调步骤的必要性。周期性微调策略能有效提升模型在分子动力学模拟中的准确性和泛化能力，为改进机器学习原子间势提供了方法论指导。

Abstract: Universal machine learned interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) embody a growing area of interest due to their transferability across the periodic table, displaying an error of about 0.6 kcal/mol against the Matbench Discovery test set. However, we show that achieving more accurate predictions on out-of-domain tasks requires fine-tuning. Additionally, we investigate the existence and influence of model biases in molecular dynamics (MD) by examining two approaches for data generation: from multiple MD trajectories in parallel, which we call naive fine-tuning, and from a single MD trajectory with fine-tuning after set intervals, which we call periodic fine-tuning. Our results find that naive fine-tuning generates constrained datasets that fail to represent MD simulations, and thus downstream fine-tuned models fail during extrapolation. In contrast, periodic fine-tuning yields models which are more generalizable and accurate, producing low-error dynamics. These findings indicate the role of uMLIP bias in fine-tuning, and highlights the need for multiple fine-tuning steps. Lastly, we relate unphysical behavior to principal component space, and quantify extrapolations through Q-residual analysis, which are useful as a proxy for epistemic uncertainty for larger simulations.

### [27] [Engineering photomagnetism in collinear van der Waals antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10186)

TL;DR: 本文通过过渡金属离子掺杂（TM-ion doping）工程化范德华反铁磁体（van der Waals antiferromagnets）的光磁效应（photomagnetism），在Mn₁₋ₓNiₓPS₃中实现高效超快自旋动力学控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现反铁磁自旋动力学的高效超快光学控制是下一代高速太赫兹自旋电子学（THz spintronic）和磁子学（magnonic）器件的核心目标。然而，现有基于晶体场分裂d-d轨道多重态（crystal-field-split d-d orbital multiplets）共振光泵浦（resonant optical pumping）的方法仅限于少数体系，缺乏增强反铁磁体中d-d光磁效应的通用策略。

Method: 通过过渡金属离子掺杂工程化共线范德华反铁磁体（collinear van der Waals antiferromagnets）的光磁效应。在Mn₁₋ₓNiₓPS₃体系中，少量Ni²⁺掺杂激活强光磁响应，同时基本保持奈尔基态（Néel ground state）。通过调节泵浦能量（pump energy）跨越整个Mn₁₋ₓNiₓPS₃组分范围，研究Ni激发在不同反铁磁态中的有效性。

Result: 仅10% Ni掺杂即可使光磁响应相比纯MnPS₃提升一个数量级以上。Ni²⁺的d-d跃迁共振泵浦驱动大振幅相干自旋进动（large-amplitude coherent spin precession），并提供螺旋度依赖的相位控制（helicity-dependent phase control）。Ni激发在竞争的奈尔和锯齿形反铁磁态（zig-zag antiferromagnetic states）中均保持有效，同时支持可调频率的相干自旋进动。

Conclusion: 过渡金属离子掺杂被确立为一种通用策略，可用于利用轨道多重态激发（orbital multiplet excitations）实现范德华反铁磁体中的超快、低耗散自旋控制。

Abstract: Achieving efficient ultrafast optical control of antiferromagnetic spin dynamics is a central goal for next-generation high-speed THz spintronic and magnonic devices. Resonant optical pumping of crystal-field-split d-d orbital multiplets in magnetic TM ions directly modulates exchange and spin-orbit interactions, inducing large-amplitude coherent spin precession. However, such effects are limited to a handful of systems and there is no general strategy to enhance d-d photomagnetism in antiferromagnets. Here, we demonstrate the engineering of photomagnetism via TM-ion doping in collinear van der Waals antiferromagnets. In Mn$_{1-x}$Ni$_x$PS$_3$, small amounts of Ni$^{2+}$ activate a strong photomagnetic response while largely preserving the Néel ground state. Even 10% Ni boosts the response by more than an order of magnitude compared to pure MnPS$_3$, with resonant pumping of Ni$^{2+}$ d-d transitions driving large-amplitude coherent spin precession and providing helicity-dependent phase control. Tuning the pump energy across the full Mn$_{1-x}$Ni$_x$PS$_3$ composition range shows that Ni excitations remain effective across competing Néel and zig-zag antiferromagnetic states while supporting tunable-frequency coherent spin precession. These results establish TM-ion doping as a versatile strategy to harness orbital multiplet excitations for ultrafast, low-dissipation spin control in van der Waals antiferromagnets.

### [28] [Flexible Cutoff Learning: Optimizing Machine Learning Potentials After Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10205)
*Rick Oerder,Jan Hamaekers*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出柔性截断学习（FCL）方法，用于训练机器学习原子间势（MLIPs），使其截断半径可在训练后调整。该方法通过在训练时为每个原子随机采样截断半径，使模型可在部署时根据不同应用需求调整截断半径，实现精度与计算成本的平衡优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）在训练时固定截断半径（cutoff radius），限制了模型在不同应用场景下的灵活性。需要一种方法使MLIPs能够在训练后根据具体应用需求调整截断半径，以优化精度与计算成本之间的权衡。

Method: 提出柔性截断学习（Flexible Cutoff Learning, FCL）方法，在训练过程中为每个原子独立随机采样截断半径。采用改进的MACE架构在MAD数据集上进行训练，并使用可微分成本模型在训练后针对特定目标系统优化每个原子的截断半径。

Result: 在分子晶体子集上的实验表明，优化后的每个原子截断半径可将计算成本降低60%以上，而力误差增加不到1%。这证明FCL能够通过训练后截断优化，使单个通用MLIP适应多样化应用需求。

Conclusion: FCL方法实现了训练后截断半径的可调整性，消除了重新训练的需求。该方法使单个通用MLIP能够通过训练后优化适应不同应用场景，在保持精度的同时显著降低计算成本。

Abstract: We introduce Flexible Cutoff Learning (FCL), a method for training machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) whose cutoff radii can be adjusted after training. Unlike conventional MLIPs that fix the cutoff radius during training, FCL models are trained by randomly sampling cutoff radii independently for each atom. The resulting model can then be deployed with different per-atom cutoff radii depending on the application, enabling application-specific optimization of the accuracy-cost tradeoff. Using a differentiable cost model, these per-atom cutoffs can be optimized for specific target systems after training. We demonstrate FCL with a modified MACE architecture trained on the MAD dataset. For a subset featuring molecular crystals, optimized per-atom cutoffs reduce computational cost by more than 60% while increasing force errors by less than 1%. These results show that FCL enables training of a single general-purpose MLIP that can be adapted to diverse applications through post-training cutoff optimization, eliminating the need for retraining.

Abstract: We investigated the structural evolution and optical properties of beta-Ga2O3 crystals implanted with different rare-earth (RE) ions using channeling Rutherford Backscattering Spectrometry, Positron Annihilation, Photoluminescence, and Photoluminescence Excitation spectroscopies. The studies reveal that implantation-induced disorder, accompanying phase transitions, and post-annealing structural recovery are largely insensitive to the implanted RE species. The defect microstructure is also found to be similar for all implanted RE ions.
  Thermal annealing does not completely remove radiation-induced defects but instead drives their rearrangement into larger defect complexes. Unimplanted (virgin) beta-Ga2O3 exhibits strong UV-visible emission attributed to oxygen vacancies, whereas the introduction of RE ions produces additional emission lines originating from electronic transitions within RE3+ ions.

Fluence-dependent studies of Yb3+ reveal the onset of concentration quenching, while RE-related emission remains efficient even in the presence of substantial lattice disorder.
  These findings provide new insight into defect evolution in ion-implanted beta-Ga2O3 and clarify the excitation mechanisms of RE3+ ions, offering guidance for optimizing the optical performance of beta-Ga2O3:RE materials.

Motivation: 固态半导体激光器支撑着从电信、数据存储到传感、医疗诊断和新兴量子通信的多种技术。有机半导体因其大的激子结合能（exciton binding energy）、强光学非线性和简单的加工工艺，成为极化激元学（polaritonics）的理想材料。然而，虽然溶液加工的有机薄膜已被广泛研究，但其光学微腔几乎总是通过真空沉积（vacuum deposition）制备，限制了真正可扩展和低成本器件的实现。

Method: 研究采用完全溶液加工（solution processing）的方法制备有机激光微腔，该微腔在强耦合（strong coupling）机制下工作。通过将微腔驱动到高激发密度，观察极化激元凝聚体（polariton condensate）的行为。

Result: 该平台能够可靠地驱动到高激发密度，观察到极化激元凝聚体（polariton condensate）的可逆、相互作用驱动的重新分布。这揭示了有机微腔中独特的极化激元激光行为（polariton lasing behaviour）。

Conclusion: 这种制备方法和观察到的激光动力学为可扩展的极化激元（polaritonic）和量子光子技术（quantum photonic technologies）开辟了道路，并为研究有机系统中的非线性极化激元物理（nonlinear polariton physics）提供了新的机会。

Abstract: Solid-state semiconductor lasers underpin technologies from telecommunications and data storage to sensing, medical diagnostics, and emerging quantum communication. Polaritons-hybrid exciton-photon states have further extended this reach, enabling room-temperature quantum effects such as low-threshold lasing and single-photon nonlinearities. Organic semiconductors are ideal for polaritonics due to their large exciton binding energy, strong optical nonlinearities, and straightforward processing, making them attractive for both classical and quantum photonics. While solution-processed organic films have been widely explored, their optical cavities have almost always been fabricated using vacuum deposition, limiting the realization of truly scalable and low-cost devices. Here, we report the first organic laser microcavities fabricated entirely by solution processing, which operate in the strong coupling regimeThe resulting platform can be driven reliably to high excitation densities, where we observe a reversible, interaction-driven redistribution of the polariton condensate, revealing a distinct polariton lasing behaviour in organic microcavities. Together, the fabrication approach and the observed lasing dynamics establish a route toward scalable polaritonic and quantum photonic technologies and provide new opportunities for studying nonlinear polariton physics in organic systems.

</details>

Method: 基于对电子-声子插值算法计算复杂度的系统分析，设计了自然集成到当前EPW实现中的GPU移植策略。该策略无缝移植到NVIDIA、AMD和Intel GPU，并采用混合MPI-GPU-OpenMP并行化方案替代原有的单一MPI并行化方案。

Abstract: We demonstrate a highly efficient GPU implementation of the Wannier interpolation of electron-phonon matrix elements in the EPW code. This framework also achieves nearly ideal scalability up to thousands of GPU nodes on the Aurora supercomputer. With this development, EPW is ready to support electron-phonon physics calculations on exascale platforms.

### [33] [Polarization transfer force on ferroelectric domain walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10460)
*Huanhuan Yang,Peng Yan,Gerrit E. W. Bauer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了由极化电流驱动的铁电纹理动力学，发现铁子（ferrons）作为集体极化激发的量子，为畴壁动力学提供了一种不同于磁振子（magnons）的奇异驱动机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将畴壁的线性极化动力学映射到具有Pöschl-Teller势的类薛定谔问题，分析极化波的传输特性；同时考虑内在非线性效应，研究其对畴壁运动的影响。

Result: 在线性区域，极化波完全透射，不对畴壁产生净作用力；然而内在非线性效应导致负辐射压力（negative radiation pressure），将畴壁拉向源端。这一机制使得通过光激发和温度梯度实现高效的畴壁控制成为可能。

Conclusion: 铁子驱动的畴壁动力学机制为铁电存储器（ferroelectric memory）和逻辑器件提供了新的控制手段，通过负辐射压力效应可实现高效的光学和热学畴壁操控。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of ferroelectric textures driven by polarization currents. We show that, ferrons, the quanta of collective polarization excitations, provide an exotic driving mechanism for domain wall (DW) dynamics, compared with their magnonic counterparts. By mapping the linear polarization dynamics of a DW onto a Schrödinger-like problem with a Pöschl-Teller potential, we show that polarization waves are fully transmitted and therefore do not exert a net force on the DW in the linear regime. However, intrinsic nonlinearities give rise to a negative radiation pressure that pulls the DW toward the source. This mechanism allows efficient DW control by optical excitation and temperature gradients with application potential in ferroelectric memory and logic devices.

*Eric Viklund,David N. Seidman,Sam Posen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过聚焦离子束（FIB）层析成像技术分析Nb3Sn超导射频腔薄膜的亚表面微观结构，发现锡（Sn）缺乏区域比预期更普遍，但这些区域位于薄膜表面以下，受超电流屏蔽效应影响，可能不是限制腔性能的主要因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nb3Sn超导射频（SRF）腔的加速梯度目前受到限制，其根本原因仍是该领域的开放性问题。一个主要假设认为这种限制源于Nb3Sn涂层中锡（Sn）缺乏区域的存在，这些区域可能抑制超热场（superheating field）。由于Nb3Sn具有相对较大的相干长度（coherence length），表面附近的缺陷可能与射频（RF）场发生显著相互作用。

Method: 本研究采用聚焦离子束（focused ion beam, FIB）层析成像技术（tomography）来分析Nb3Sn薄膜的亚表面微观结构。该技术能够对薄膜内的锡（Sn）分布和晶粒结构进行三维重建（three-dimensional reconstruction）。

Result: 通过关联锡含量与晶粒结构，研究发现锡缺乏区域比先前认为的更为普遍。然而，这些锡缺乏区域始终位于薄膜表面以下，该处的射频场因超电流屏蔽（supercurrent screening）而强烈衰减，因此可能不是限制腔性能的因素。

Conclusion: 虽然Nb3Sn薄膜中普遍存在亚表面锡缺乏区域，但由于它们位于射频场衰减的深度，可能不是限制超导射频腔加速梯度的主要因素。这表明需要寻找其他限制性能的根本原因。

Abstract: The accelerating gradient of Nb3Sn superconducting radiofrequency (SRF) cavities is currently limited, and the underlying cause remains an open question in the field. One leading hypothesis attributes this limitation to the presence of tin-deficient regions within the Nb3Sn coating, which can suppress the superheating field. Due to the relatively large coherence length of Nb3Sn, defects near the surface may significantly interact with the RF field. However, these subsurface defects have proven difficult to characterize. This research aims to investigate the structure and distribution of subsurface Sn deficient regions to better understand their influence on cavity performance. We employ focused ion beam (FIB) tomography to analyze the subsurface microstructure of Nb3Sn thin films. This technique enables three-dimensional reconstruction of both the tin distribution and the grain structure within the film. By correlating Sn content with grain structure, we find that Sn deficient regions are more prevalent that previously thought. However, the Sn deficient regions are consistently located below the surface of the film where RF fields are strongly attenuated by supercurrent screening and are likely not a limiting factor for cavity performance.

Abstract: The electronic structure of materials is fundamentally governed by their crystal symmetry. While most research on two-dimensional materials has focused on hexagonal lattices, such as graphene, hexagonal boron nitride, and transition metal dichalcogenides. This work explores a square-lattice system: the experimentally realized phthalocyanine-based metal-organic framework (ZnPc-MOF). Using group representation theory, we classify the electronic bands of ZnPc-MOF monolayer, AA- and AB-stacked bilayers, and twisted bilayers in terms of the irreducible representations (irreps) of their little groups. We find that bands in the AB-stacked bilayer remain two-fold degenerate along the $Y$ and $Y^{\prime}$ high-symmetry lines, as a consequence of the sole presence of two-dimensional irreps along these directions. We further derive optical transition selection rules to interpret the optical conductivity, revealing pronounced polarization-dependent optical responses. Additionally, we investigate the quasicrystalline electronic states in the 45$^{\circ}$ twisted bilayer (ZnPc-MOF quasicrystal) using the resonant coupling Hamiltonian. Compared to graphene quasicrystals, ZnPc-MOF quasicrystal exhibits weaker resonant coupling strengths, yet its quasicrystalline states lie closer to the Fermi energy, suggesting a greater contribution to low-energy electronic phenomena.

### [37] [Transverse and Longitudinal Magnetothermopower Promoted by Ambipolar Effect in Half-Heusler Topological Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10499)
*Orest Pavlosiuk,Marcin Matusiak,Andrzej Ptok,Piotr Wiśniewski,Dariusz Kaczorowski*

TL;DR: 该研究发现半赫斯勒拓扑半金属DyPtBi同时具有大的纵向和横向磁热电功率，打破了传统电子-空穴补偿系统中两者难以兼得的局限，为热电材料优化提供了新方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑平凡和非平凡半金属在高载流子补偿条件下通常表现出大的横向磁热电功率，但纵向磁热电功率往往被抑制。本研究旨在探索同时实现大纵向和横向磁热电功率的可能性。

Method: 通过实验测量DyPtBi半赫斯勒拓扑半金属的纵向和横向磁热电功率，并与DyPdBi进行对比分析，研究其能带结构和补偿调节对热电性能的影响。

Result: DyPtBi在14T磁场下表现出显著的热电性能：纵向磁热电功率在149K时达到131μV/K，横向磁热电功率在200K时达到-297μV/K。即使在290K和1T的实用条件下，横向磁热电功率仍为-18μV/K，属于同类条件下的最大值之一。

Conclusion: DyPtBi中不完全的电子-空穴补偿和空穴-电子型载流子的内在不对称性使其同时具备大的纵向和横向磁热电功率，这突显了化学掺杂和能带工程在稀土基半赫斯勒材料中优化热电性能的潜力。

Abstract: Topologically trivial and non-trivial semimetals with a high degree of carrier compensation are well known for demonstrating large transverse magnetothermopower ($S_{yx}$). However, in such systems, the longitudinal magnetothermopower ($S_{xx}$) is typically suppressed due to nearly perfect electron-hole compensation. Here, we show that the half-Heusler topological semimetal DyPtBi exhibits simultaneously large $S_{xx}$ and $S_{yx}$ magnetothermopowers, defying this conventional trade-off. In $B=14$\,T, thermopower of DyPtBi reaches peak values of $S_{xx}=131\,μ\rm{V/K}$ at $T=149$\,K and $S_{yx}=-297\,μ\rm{V/K}$ at $T=200$\,K, and transverse component remains significantly large even at $290$\,K ($S_{yx}=-213\,μ\rm{V/K}$). Remarkably, at $T=290$\,K and in relatively weak magnetic field of $1$\,T, both relevant for practical applications, DyPtBi shows $S_{yx}=-18\,μ\rm{V/K}$, which is one of the largest values reported under such conditions. The large transverse thermopower originates from an ambipolar effect associated with thermal excitation occurring in zero-gap semiconductors. Due to the imperfect electron-hole compensation, an intrinsic asymmetry between hole- and electron-type carriers enables pronounced values of both $S_{xx}$ and $S_{yx}$, resulting in high effective thermopower ($S_{xx}+|S_{yx}|=379\,μ\rm{V/K}$) in DyPtBi at 200\,K. A comparative analysis with DyPdBi, another half-Heusler material that demonstrates large $S_{xx}=123\,μ\rm{V/K}$ but small $S_{yx}=-16\,μ\rm{V/K}$ (both values obtained at $T=293$\,K and $B=14$\,T), highlights the critical role of band structure and compensation tuning. These findings underscore the potential of chemical doping and band engineering in rare-earth-based half-Heusler materials for optimizing both transverse and longitudinal thermoelectric properties.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电负性是化学直觉的基石，但现有标度多为经验性推导，依赖于参数化模型或复合物理量。本研究旨在建立一种基于量子力学可测量性质的普适电负性标度。

Method: 引入基于原子平均内势（atomic mean inner potential, AMIP）的普适电负性标度$χ_{\mathrm{AMIP},p}$，该标度是三个基态原子描述符的解析函数，具有明确的物理单位，可通过第一性原理计算和电子散射实验获得。

Result: 该电负性标度与现有标度吻合良好，成功分类了358种化合物的键合类型，包括符合类金属"Si规则"。在预测性能方面，$χ_{\mathrm{AMIP,1/2}}$能准确确定超过14,000个配位环境的路易斯酸强度（$R^2=0.93$）和36种元素的γ射线湮没谱宽度（$R^2=0.97$），优于先前方法。

Conclusion: 通过将电负性与可测量的量子性质直接关联，该工作为整个周期表的电子结构和化学行为提供了一个统一且具有预测性的描述符。

Abstract: Electronegativity is a cornerstone of chemical intuition, essential for rationalizing bonding, reactivity, and material properties. However, prevailing scales remain empirically derived, often relying on parameterized models or composite physical quantities. In this work, we introduce a universal electronegativity scale founded on the atomic mean inner potential (AMIP), also known as the average Coulomb potential, a fundamental, quantum-mechanical property accessible through both first-principles computation and electron-scattering experiments. Our scale, denoted $χ_{\mathrm{AMIP},p}$, is an analytic function of just three ground-state atomic descriptors and carries explicit physical units. It demonstrates excellent agreement with established scales and successfully classifies bonding types across 358 compounds, including adherence to the metalloid ``Si rule". Beyond replicating known trends, $χ_{\mathrm{AMIP,1/2}}$ proves to be a powerful predictive tool, accurately determining Lewis acid strengths for over 14,000 coordination environments ($R^2=0.93$) and $γ$-ray annihilation spectral widths for 36 elements ($R^2=0.97$), outperforming previous methods. By linking electronegativity directly to a measurable quantum property, this work provides a unified and predictive descriptor for electronic structure and chemical behavior across the periodic table.

Method: 采用高能电子辐照技术调控典型半赫斯勒外尔半金属GdPtBi的费米能级，使其偏离原始位置的外尔节点，系统研究费米能级变化对磁输运性质的影响。

Result: 即使费米能级从原始位置偏移100 meV，作为拓扑半金属中手征磁异常明确指标的负纵向磁电阻仍然持续存在。反常霍尔效应随费米能级变化呈现复杂变化，这归因于避免能带交叉产生的贝里曲率的能量依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究发现外尔节点对GdPtBi磁输运性质的影响具有鲁棒性，不受费米能级位置的限制。这一行为很可能适用于许多半赫斯勒外尔半金属，揭示了拓扑非平庸态在能带结构中的稳定存在。

Abstract: Half-Heusler compounds from the $RE$PtBi family exemplify Weyl semimetals in which external magnetic field induce Weyl nodes. These materials exceptionally host topologically non-trivial states near the Fermi level and their manifestation can be clearly seen in the magnetotransport properties. In this study, we tune the Fermi level of the archetypal half-Heusler Weyl semimetal GdPtBi through high-energy electron irradiation, moving it away from the Weyl nodes to investigate the resilience of the contribution of topologically non-trivial states to magnetotransport properties. Remarkably, we observe that the negative longitudinal magnetoresistance, which is a definitive indicator of the chiral magnetic anomaly occurring in topological semimetals, persists even when the Fermi level is shifted by 100\,meV from its original position in the pristine sample. Additionally, the anomalous Hall effect shows complex variations as the Fermi level is altered, attributed to the energy-dependent nature of the Berry curvature, which arises from avoided band crossing. Our findings show the robust influence of Weyl nodes on the magneto-transport properties of GdPtBi, irrespective of the Fermi level position, a behaviour likely applicable to many half-Heusler Weyl semimetals.

### [40] [High-Throughput-Screening Workflow for Predicting Volume Changes by Ion Intercalation in Battery Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10631)
*Aljoscha Felix Baumann,Daniel Mutter,Daniel F. Urban,Christian Elsässer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种优先筛选候选材料的工作流程，使用原子级特征和机器学习模型预测键长来计算插层体积变化。该模型基于"相同离子物种在相似局部配位环境中的键长在不同晶体结构中具有可比性"的假设，并在DFT生成的数据集上进行训练。

Result: 该工作流成功筛选了约1,175,000种过渡金属氧化物和氟化物，并对最有前景的候选材料进行了DFT验证。结果表明，该方法能够有效过滤大规模候选材料集，加速发现低体积变化的电池插层材料。

Conclusion: 提出的工作流程实现了大规模候选材料的高通量筛选，为加速发现具有优异结构稳定性的电池插层材料提供了有效工具，有望促进低体积变化电极材料的开发。

Abstract: Mechanical stresses and strains developing locally within the microstructure of active ion-battery-electrode materials during charge-discharge cycles can compromise their long-term stability. In this context, crystalline compounds exhibiting low volume changes are of particular interest. Atomistic simulations can be employed to quantify the volume change of the crystal structure upon intercalation and deintercalation of ions and to elucidate the local mechanisms underlying the global structural response. While density functional theory (DFT) offers a robust and accurate framework for such calculations, its computational cost limits its applicability for large-scale screening of diverse intercalation structures and sites. In this work, we present a workflow designed to prioritize candidate materials for subsequent detailed characterization. The workflow calculates the volume change upon intercalation using atomic-level features and a machine-learning model for bond-length prediction. The bond-length predictions are based on the assumption that bonds between the same ionic species in similar local coordination environments exhibit comparable lengths across different crystallographic structures. The model was trained on a DFT-generated dataset, which inherently defines the chemical space in which reliable predictions can be expected. We demonstrate the workflow's utility by screening approximately 1,175,000 transition-metal oxides and fluorides, followed by DFT validation of the most promising candidates. The proposed workflow enables filtering of large candidate sets and accelerates the potential discovery of low volume change intercalation materials for batteries.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铬硫溴化物（CrSBr）是一种具有直接带隙和显著各向异性的磁性范德华半导体，其电子、光学、自旋和晶格自由度均表现出各向异性特征。研究其光学各向异性对于理解该材料中的光-物质相互作用至关重要，尤其对未来自旋光电子和光子学应用具有重要意义。

Method: 采用光谱成像椭偏仪（spectroscopic imaging ellipsometry, SIE）结合穆勒矩阵分析（Mueller-matrix analysis）方法，系统测量了顺磁性CrSBr薄膜的完整介电张量（full dielectric tensor）。

Result: 测量结果显示CrSBr具有显著的光学各向异性，介电张量包含三个不同的对角分量。面内元素主要由沿两个主要晶轴偏振的显著激子共振主导，识别出两个主要激子能带：中心位于1.3eV的A激子和中心位于1.7eV的B激子。A激子沿b晶轴方向偏振，而B激子由两个近乎简并的贡献组成，分别沿两个正交的面内晶轴偏振。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解CrSBr中各向异性光-物质相互作用（anisotropic light-matter interactions）提供了基础性见解，这些发现对于未来自旋光电子（spin-optoelectronic）和光子学应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Chromium sulfur bromide (CrSBr) is a magnetic van der Waals semiconductor with a direct bandgap and pronounced anisotropy in its electronic, optical, spin and lattice degrees of freedom. Here, we employ spectroscopic imaging ellipsometry (SIE) and Mueller-matrix analysis to determine the full dielectric tensor of paramagnetic CrSBr thin films. Our measurements reveal optical anisotropy, characterized by three distinct diagonal components of the dielectric tensor. The in-plane elements are dominated by prominent excitonic resonances polarized along the two main crystallographic axes. Two main excitonic bands (A and B excitons) centered around 1.3eV and 1.7eV, respectively, are identified; the A-exciton polarized along the b-crystallographic direction, whereas the B-exciton appears to consist of two nearly degenerate contributions polarized along two orthogonal in-plane crystal axes. These results provide fundamental insight into anisotropic light-matter interactions in CrSBr, relevant for future spin-optoelectronic and photonic applications.
