Artificially engraved microstructures further allow domain configurations and domain-wall trajectories to be directed along predefined pathways, exemplified by the creation of a chessboard-like magnetic landscape. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究结合扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）、临界标度分析（critical scaling analysis）和磁热测量（magnetocaloric measurements），将实空间结构与磁临界性直接关联。

Result: STM显示MnBi₂Te₄具有原子级平坦的七重层平台，而MnBi₄Te₇则呈现共存的七重层和五重层终止面，反映其交替堆叠序列。MnBi₂Te₄表现出稳健的三维伊辛类临界行为及独特的低温一级相变，而MnBi₄Te₇则显示由层间交换减弱和竞争磁相导致的交叉主导临界性。两者的磁热响应显著不同：MnBi₂Te₄具有双类型磁热行为，而MnBi₄Te₇仅显示常规磁热响应。

Despite extensive interest in their topological properties, how the insertion of Bi$_2$Te$_3$ quintuple layers modifies magnetic critical fluctuations near the antiferromagnetic transition remains unresolved. Here, we combine scanning tunneling microscopy (STM), critical scaling analysis, and magnetocaloric measurements to directly correlate real-space structures with magnetic criticality. STM reveals atomically flat septuple-layer terraces in MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ whereas MnBi$_4$Te$_7$ displays coexisting septuple and quintuple layer terminations reflecting its alternating stacking sequence. MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ exhibits robust three-dimensional Ising-like critical behavior together with a distinct low-temperature first-order transition. In contrast, MnBi$_4$Te$_7$ displays crossover-dominated criticality arising from weakened interlayer exchange and competing magnetic phases. Correspondingly, the magnetocaloric response differs significantly between the two compounds. MnBi$_2$Te$_4$ shows dual-type magnetocaloric behavior with a sharp field-induced sign reversal of the isothermal magnetic entropy change ($-ΔS_M$). It exhibits both inverse ($-ΔS_M < 0$) and conventional ($-ΔS_M > 0$) magnetocaloric effects. In contrast, MnBi$_4$Te$_7$ shows only conventional magnetocaloric response with a broad positive entropy peak. These results establish structural layering as a key parameter governing magnetic critical fluctuations and magnetocaloric behavior in MnBi$_{2n}$Te$_{3n+1}$ topological magnets.

Existing electron-ion interaction models, such as the tensorial unified two-temperature model, were developed to study self-irradiation scenarios, but their suitability for light-ion irradiation remains unexplored. Here, we propose that for light projectiles, stepping back from the tensorial formulation toward a simpler, local model of electronic stopping provides a more efficient and physically transparent trajectory-dependent description. *Noah Schnitzer,Mariana Palos,Geri Topore,Nishkarsh Agarwal,Maya Gates,Yaqi Li,Robert Hovden,Ismail El Baggari,Suk Hyun Sung,Michele Shelly Conroy*

TL;DR: 本研究实现了在低至20K温度下的原子分辨率扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）成像和4D-STEM电子叠层衍射成像，解决了低温条件下原子分辨率成像的技术挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子材料（quantum materials）的许多奇异功能特性源于只能在低温下访问的结构和电子基态。理解器件操作需要在相同低温条件下进行结构表征，因为室温测量通常探测的是不同的结构状态。

Method: 使用商用氦冷却样品台，结合快速扫描和多阶段配准工作流程来减少低温不稳定性相关伪影。对于叠层衍射成像，采用包含探针像差与位置优化耦合补偿的扫描位置校正方法。

Result: 成功实现了低至20K温度下的原子分辨率STEM成像和多层电子叠层衍射成像（multislice electron ptychography），建立了可靠的低温原子分辨率成像路径。

Conclusion: 这些结果为低温下可靠的原子分辨率STEM和叠层衍射成像建立了技术路径，使得与量子技术相关的结构基态能够被直接可视化观测。

Abstract: Much of the exotic functionality of prime interest in quantum materials emerges from structural and electronic ground states that can only be accessed at cryogenic temperatures. Understanding device operation therefore requires structural characterization under the same low-temperature conditions at which these functional phases exist, as room-temperature measurements often probe a different structural state. Achieving atomic-resolution in scanning transmission electron microscopy imaging and particularly 4D-STEM electron ptychography at liquid helium temperature has remained extremely challenging because even small amounts of drift, vibration, and thermal instability associated with the cryogen can disrupt the stringent stability requirements of atomic-resolution STEM. In this work we demonstrate atomic-resolution STEM and multislice electron ptychography at temperatures as low as 20 K using a commercial helium cooled holder. We find that rapid scans and a multi-stage registration workflow are critical to reducing artifacts associated with cryogenic instability for atomic-resolution imaging, while for ptychography scan position correction including compensation for coupling between probe aberrations and position refinement is necessary for successful reconstructions. Together these results establish a pathway for reliable atomic-resolution STEM and ptychography at low temperature, enabling direct visualization of structural ground states relevant to quantum technology.

### [47] [Sliding Ferroelectricity Driven Spin-Layertronics in Altermagnetic Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10907)
*Rui Peng,Guangxu Su,Yangyang Fan,Jiaan Li,Fanxin Liu,Yee Sin Ang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁性（ferroicity）与交变磁性（altermagnetism）的协同效应为设计多功能交变磁自旋电子器件提供了新平台。本研究旨在探索通过滑动铁电性实现交变磁双层结构中自旋和层自由度的非易失性电操控机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究双层CuF₂中通过层间平移（interlayer translation）诱导可切换的面外铁电极化（out-of-plane ferroelectric polarization）。

Result: 层间平移可在双层CuF₂中诱导可切换的面外铁电极化，该极化直接耦合并反转d波交变磁自旋劈裂（d-wave altermagnetic spin splitting）。交变磁自旋劈裂具有层锁定（layer-locked）特性，滑动铁电性驱动的切换实现了非易失性自旋-层电子功能（spin-layertronics functionality）。在四层CuF₂中识别出四种极化状态，可用于多态逻辑器件。

Conclusion: 滑动铁电性为设计基于交变磁体的电压控制、高速且高能效的自旋-层电子器件（spin-layertronic devices）提供了多功能工具，为多功能交变磁自旋电子器件技术开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The synergy of ferroicity with altermagnetism offers a novel platform for designing multifunctional altermagnetic-spintronic device technology. In this work, we propose a mechanism to achieve nonvolatile electrical manipulation of spin and layer degrees of freedom in an altermagnetic bilayer via sliding ferroelectricity. Using first-principles calculations, we show that an interlayer translation can induce a switchable out-of-plane ferroelectric polarization in bilayer CuF2, which directly couples to and reverses the d-wave altermagnetic spin splitting. Notably, the altermangetic spin splitting is layer-locked, the sliding ferroelectricity-driven switching thus embodying a nonvolatile spin-layertronics functionality that couples spin-polarized transport and layer degree of freedom in a single platform. We show that in quadrilayer CuF2, four polarization states are identified which may offer multi-state logic device applications. These findings establish sliding ferroelectricity as a versatile tool for designing voltage-controlled, high-speed and energy-efficient spin-layertronic devices based on altermagnets.

*Matthew Houtput,Ingvar Zappacosta,Serghei Klimin,Samuel Poncé,Jacques Tempere,Cesare Franchini*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究通常假设线性电子-声子相互作用，即电子每次仅与一个声子相互作用。然而，在极性非谐性材料中，大的离子位移可能使线性相互作用假设失效，其有效性尚未得到验证。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算电子迁移率，使用自能弛豫时间近似和长程近似。通过最近推导的一电子-二声子矩阵元的长程部分表达式，将非线性相互作用效应纳入考虑。

Result: 由于CsPbI₃的低声子频率，一电子-二声子相互作用改变了迁移率的温度标度关系，并在室温下对迁移率贡献约10%。

Abstract: The interaction between the electrons and the lattice vibrations in a solid is responsible for various important effects, such as formation of polarons, temperature dependent bandgaps, phonon-limited carrier transport, and conventional superconductivity. Most works assume a linear electron-phonon interaction, where the electron only interacts with one phonon at a time. However, the validity of this assumption has not been verified in polar anharmonic materials, where large ionic displacements may invalidate the assumption of linear interaction. Here, we show that nonlinear electron-phonon interactions contribute significantly to the finite-temperature electron mobility of the inorganic lead halide perovskite CsPbI$_3$. We calculate the electron mobility from first principles using the self-energy relaxation time approximation and the long-range approximation. The effect of nonlinear interaction is taken into account using the recently derived expression for the long-range part of the one-electron-two-phonon matrix element. We show that due to the low phonon frequencies of CsPbI$_3$, the one-electron-two-phonon interaction changes the temperature scaling of the mobility and contributes about 10\% to the mobility at room temperature. The results underscore the importance of including nonlinear electron-phonon interaction in anharmonic halide perovskites.

### [49] [Island Sliding Barriers: A first-principles metric for determining remote epitaxy viability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10968)
*Quinn T. Campbell,Manny Xavier de Jesus Lopez,Anthony Rice,Timothy J. Ruggles,Taisuke Ohta,Caitlin McCowan,Sadhvikas Addamane,Scott W. Schmucker,Justine Koepke*

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算研究了远程外延（remote epitaxy）的机制，发现表面小岛（small islands）的滑动势垒（sliding barrier）是判断衬底-薄膜对是否适合远程外延的最可靠标准，表明该现象与石墨烯表面岛迁移的动力学（kinetics）有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远程外延（remote epitaxy）作为一种有前景的电子器件生长方法，其确切机制尚未明确，且难以预测新的衬底-薄膜对是否兼容该工艺。因此需要建立可靠的判断标准。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first principles calculations）测试多种机制，评估不同衬底-薄膜对在远程外延中的适用性，重点关注表面小岛在原子位置优化后的滑动势垒。

Result: 研究发现先前计算的静电势（electrostatic potential）等指标解释力不足，而表面小岛的滑动势垒提供了最严格的判断标准，能够有效预测衬底-薄膜对是否具有远程外延活性（remote epitaxy active）。

Conclusion: 远程外延很可能是一种与石墨烯表面岛迁移动力学相关的现象，表面小岛的滑动势垒是判断衬底-薄膜对兼容性的关键物理指标。

Abstract: Remote epitaxy, where a 2D van der Waals material (usually graphene) is inserted on top of the substrate before film epitaxy, has emerged as a promising path for growing electronics with lower defect rates and less stringent lattice matching requirements. The exact mechanism behind remote epitaxy has not been definitively shown, however, and it is not obvious when examining a new substrate-film pair whether they would be compatible with the remote epitaxy process. In this paper, we use first principles calculations to test several different mechanisms for determining whether a given substrate-film pair will successfully be grown with remote epitaxy. We find that previously calculated metrics such as electrostatic potential do not hold sufficient explanatory power. We find that the sliding barrier of small islands on the surface when the atomic positions are allowed to optimize provides the most rigorous criteria for whether a given substrate-film pair is remote epitaxy active. This indicates that remote epitaxy is likely a phenomenon related to the kinetics and ease of island migration on the graphene surface.

Method: 本文通过三个关键方面进行审查：1) 将赝快度（pseudorapidity）接受窗口识别为有限尺寸标度关系中使用的物理系统尺寸；2) 评估接受度驱动的多重性标度对用于标度分析的磁化率的影响；3) 处理标度变量中的热力学标度场（thermodynamic scaling fields）。

Result: 这些考虑澄清了与重离子碰撞实验中有限尺寸标度分析的一致实施和解释相关的若干问题，但摘要未提供具体的数值结果或明确的结论性发现。

Conclusion: 本文的分析有助于澄清在重离子碰撞实验中一致实施和解释有限尺寸标度分析的相关问题，为未来更可靠的临界终点搜索提供了方法论上的改进方向。

Abstract: Finite-size scaling (FSS) provides a framework for investigating the possible presence of a critical end point (CEP) in the QCD phase diagram using fluctuation observables measured in relativistic heavy-ion collisions. A recent analysis reported a FSS collapse of a susceptibility constructed from net-proton cumulants, which was interpreted as evidence for a CEP near $μ_B \approx 625$ MeV \cite{FSSpaper}. This note examines several aspects of that scaling construction. These include identifying the pseudorapidity acceptance window with the physical system size used in the finite-size scaling relations, assessing the influence of acceptance-driven multiplicity scaling on the susceptibility used for the scaling analysis, and treating thermodynamic scaling fields in the scaling variable. These considerations clarify several issues relevant for the consistent implementation and interpretation of finite-size scaling analyses in heavy-ion collision experiments.

### [51] [A Resolution of the Ito-Stratonovich Debate in Quantum Stochastic Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.16314)
*Aritro Mukherjee*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种量子噪声均匀化方案，通过时间粗粒化处理非马尔可夫、有色噪声驱动的量子随机过程，并将其连接到有效的白噪声（马尔可夫）极限，解决了Ito和Stratonovich约定之间的模糊性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子随机过程在描述开放量子系统和量子基础理论中广泛应用。由乘性有色噪声驱动的物理相关量子随机过程通常是非马尔可夫的且解析上难以处理，同时其马尔可夫极限在使用Ito或Stratonovich约定时通常不等价，需要解决这一模糊性问题。

Method: 引入量子噪声均匀化方案，采用新颖的相空间增广方法将非马尔可夫动力学映射到高维马尔可夫系统，然后在噪声特征时间尺度上应用受控的微扰粗粒化方案，从而推导具有重整化系数的有效马尔可夫生成元。

Result: 该方案能够解析地推导具有重整化系数的有效马尔可夫生成元，并允许施加因果性等物理约束。研究解决了乘性有色噪声驱动量子随机过程的Ito-Stratonovich模糊性，表明其一致的马尔可夫极限对应于具有重整化系数的Stratonovich约定以及Ito约定中的修正项。

Conclusion: 通过假设马尔可夫极限展开为因果、完全正且保迹的动力学，进一步表征了由乘性有色噪声驱动的物理相关非马尔可夫量子随机过程家族，为这类系统的分析提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Quantum stochastic processes are widely used in describing open quantum systems and in the context of quantum foundations. Physically relevant quantum stochastic processes driven by multiplicative colored noise are generically non-Markovian and analytically intractable. Further, their Markovian limits are generically inequivalent when using either the Ito or Stratonovich conventions for the same quantum stochastic processes. We introduce a quantum noise homogenization scheme that temporally coarse-grains non-Markovian, colored-noise-driven quantum stochastic processes and connects them to their effective white-noise (Markovian) limits. Our approach uses a novel phase-space augmentation that maps the non-Markovian dynamics into a higher-dimensional Markovian system and then applies a controlled perturbative coarse-graining scheme in the characteristic time scales of the noise. This allows an explicit analytical algorithm to derive effective Markovian generators with renormalized coefficients and enables various physical constraints, such as causality, to be imposed on them. We thus resolve the Ito--Stratonovich ambiguity for multiplicative colored-noise-driven quantum stochastic processes, wherein we show that their consistent Markovian limit corresponds to the Stratonovich convention with renormalized coefficients as well as correction terms in Ito's convention. By assuming their Markovian limit unravels causal, completely positive and trace-preserving dynamics, we further characterize a physically relevant family of non-Markovian quantum stochastic processes driven by multiplicative colored~noise.

</details>


### [52] [Tight Quantum Speed Limit for Ergotropy Charging in the N-Qubit Dicke Battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10415)
*Anass Jad,Abderrahim El Allati*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文推导并严格证明了N-qubit Dicke量子电池中ergotropy充电的紧致量子速度极限（QSL）：归一化ergotropy ε的首达时间满足τ*(ε) ≥ √(Nε)/(2λ√n̄)，其中λ是耦合强度，n̄是平均充电器光子数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为量子电池的ergotropy充电过程建立精确的量子速度极限（quantum speed limit, QSL），特别是针对N-qubit Dicke量子电池系统，以量化其充电速度的基本限制。

Method: 方法基于精确的微扰恒等式ε(t) = Aλ²n̄t² + O((λt)⁴)，其中A=4/N是短时ergotropy系数，并结合对所有N都成立的全局上界进行解析证明。

Result: 主要结果是推导出紧致的量子速度极限：τ*(ε) ≥ √(Nε)/(2λ√n̄)，并证明复合参数Γ_N = 2λ√(n̄/N)是充电速度的唯一品质因数（figure of merit），所有协议都收敛于Γ_Nτ* ≥ √ε，且在小ε时该界限饱和度在1%以内。

Conclusion: 结论表明ergotropy充电速度存在基本量子极限，复合参数Γ_N = 2λ√(n̄/N)完全表征了充电性能，为量子电池的优化设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We derive and analytically prove a tight quantum speed limit (QSL) for ergotropy charging in the $N$-qubit Dicke quantum battery: the first-passage time to normalised ergotropy $ε$ satisfies $τ^{*}(ε) \geq \sqrt{Nε}/(2λ\sqrt{\bar{n}})$, where $λ$ is the coupling and $\bar{n}$ is the mean charger photon number. The bound follows from an exact perturbative identity $ε(t) = Aλ^2\bar{n}t^2 + \mathcal{O}((λt)^4)$, where $A=4/N$ is the short-time ergotropy coefficient, combined with a global upper bound proved analytically for all $N$. The composite parameter $Γ_N = 2λ\sqrt{\bar{n}/N}$ is the unique figure of merit for charging speed; all protocols collapse onto $Γ_N τ^{*} \geq \sqrtε$, with the bound saturated to within 1% at small $ε$.

</details>


### [53] [Is the existence of unbounded operators a problem for quantum mechanics? In response to Carcassi, Calderon, and Aidala](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10601)
*Zhonghao Lu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文反驳了Carcassi等人关于希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）不具物理性应被施瓦茨空间（Schwartz space）取代的主张，论证无限期望值在量子力学中不构成问题，而改用施瓦茨空间反而会排除有意义的哈密顿演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回应Carcassi、Calderon和Aidala最近提出的论点，他们认为希尔伯特空间因包含某些可观测量具有无限期望值的态而不具物理性，应被施瓦茨空间取代。作者同时关注Streater、Wightman、Heathcote和Lemos提出的关于无界算符（unbounded operators）的问题。

Method: 通过分析论证的方式，作者反驳了无限期望值导致问题的观点，并指出施瓦茨空间替代方案的缺陷。方法包括讨论本质自伴算符（essentially self-adjoint operators）与自伴算符（self-adjoint operators）在量子力学重构中的潜在问题，以及分析"物理性"概念在基础物理学中的层次结构。

Result: 论证表明无限期望值的存在不会在量子力学中引发问题，而将希尔伯特空间替换为施瓦茨空间反而会产生更多问题，特别是会排除一类有意义的哈密顿演化。作者进一步指出"物理性"是一个模糊概念，并将Carcassi等人提出的问题与量子场论中的哈达玛条件（Hadamard condition）问题联系起来。

Conclusion: 希尔伯特空间不应被施瓦茨空间取代，因为无限期望值不构成实质问题，而替代方案会带来更严重的理论限制。基础物理学中的"物理性"概念需要更清晰的界定，相关讨论与量子场论中的哈达玛条件问题存在理论联系。

Abstract: In this paper I argue against Carcassi, Calderon, and Aidala's recent claim that the Hilbert spaces are unphysical and should be replaced with the Schwartz spaces in quantum mechanics, since Hilbert spaces include states with infinite expectation values for certain observables. I also review and discuss issues regarding unbounded operators in quantum mechanics raised by Streater and Wightman, Heathcote, and Lemos. I argue that the existence of infinite expectation values does not cause problems in quantum mechanics. On the other hand, replacing the Hilbert spaces with the Schwartz spaces would cause more issues, as it would exclude a class of meaningful Hamiltonian evolutions. I also discuss the question in literature whether reformulating quantum mechanics with essentially self-adjoint operators instead of self-adjoint operators may cause problems. I further analyse the hierarchies of the notions of "physicality" and possibility in fundamental physics, and suggest that "physicality" is a vague concept. Finally, I connect the problem raised by Carcassi, Calderon, and Aidala with the problem of the Hadamard condition in quantum field theory.

</details>


### [54] [Graph Symmetry Organizes Exceptional Dynamics in Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10654)
*Eric R. Bittner,Bhavay Tyagi,Kevin E. Bassler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种从微观耗散模型直接识别和表征奇异点（exceptional points）的对称性解析方法，无需先验构造有效哈密顿量，并引入了基于本征向量条件的数值诊断指标$\mathcal{E}$来量化接近缺陷动力学的程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前奇异点（exceptional points）研究大多从刻意设计的有效哈密顿量出发，其参数被调谐以展现奇异行为。然而，在现实开放量子系统中，动力学由Lindblad超算符（superoperators）支配，其谱结构高维、受对称性约束，且不易约化为最小非厄米模型。缺乏直接从微观耗散模型发现奇异动力学的通用框架。

Method: 引入对称性解析方法（symmetry-resolved approach），直接从完整的Liouvillian生成元识别和表征奇异点。相关耗散诱导图对称性（graph symmetries），将Liouville空间分解为低维不变扇区（invariant sectors），其中最小非厄米块（non-Hermitian blocks）支配奇异点和宇称-时间对称性破缺（PT-breaking）行为的出现。进一步引入基于本征向量条件（eigenvector conditioning）的数值诊断指标——奇异点强度$\mathcal{E}$。

Result: 应用于具有相关退相位（correlated dephasing）和弛豫（relaxation）的紧束缚模型（tight-binding models），该方法重现了解析预测的奇异缝（exceptional seams），并揭示了奇异点流形（EP manifolds）附近$\mathcal{E}$的普适标度行为（universal scaling）。

Conclusion: 该框架能够系统性地发现复杂或高维开放系统中隐藏的奇异结构，并且天然兼容无矩阵（matrix-free）和张量网络（tensor-network）实现，适用于可扩展的多体应用（many-body applications）。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs), indicative of parity-time (PT) symmetry breaking, play a central role in non-Hermitian physics, yet most studies begin from deliberately engineered effective Hamiltonians whose parameters are tuned to exhibit exceptional behavior. In realistic open quantum systems, however, dynamics are governed by Lindblad superoperators whose spectral structure is high-dimensional, symmetry-constrained, and not obviously reducible to minimal non-Hermitian models. A general framework for discovering exceptional dynamics directly from microscopic dissipative models has been lacking. Here we introduce a symmetry-resolved approach for identifying and characterizing exceptional points directly from the full Liouvillian generator. Correlated dissipation induces graph symmetries that decompose Liouville space into low-dimensional invariant sectors, within which minimal non-Hermitian blocks govern the onset of EPs and PT-breaking behavior. We further introduce a numerical diagnostic - the exceptional-point strength $\mathcal{E}$ - based on eigenvector conditioning, which quantifies proximity to defective dynamics without requiring analytic reduction. Applied to tight-binding models with correlated dephasing and relaxation, the method reproduces analytically predicted exceptional seams and reveals universal scaling of $\mathcal{E}$ near EP manifolds. More broadly, the framework enables systematic discovery of hidden exceptional structure in complex or high-dimensional open systems and is naturally compatible with matrix-free and tensor-network implementations for scalable many-body applications.

</details>


### [55] [Digital dissipative state preparation for frustration-free gapless quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10119)
*Johannes Feldmeier,Yu-Jie Liu,Mikhail D. Lukin,Soonwon Choi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于局域投影测量和酉反馈的协议，用于制备量子多体系统的代数关联基态，特别针对无阻挫无能隙系统。该协议能在系统尺寸的多项式时间内制备未知基态，并通过数值模拟验证了在一维和二维海森堡模型、Fredkin自旋链及二维共振价键态模型中的有效性。

Method: 引入了一种结合局域投影测量（local projective measurements）和酉反馈（unitary feedback）的协议，专门针对无阻挫无能隙（frustration-free gapless）系统。该方法通过分析单粒子动力学性能并基于准粒子（quasiparticles）物理推广到多体系统，实现了完全数字化的基态制备。

Result: 理论预测表明，瞬态冷却动力学直接揭示了系统的普适临界性质。当系统的动力学临界指数（dynamical critical exponent）大于或等于准粒子探索的有效空间维度时，态制备时间与有限尺寸能隙（finite-size gap）的倒数呈线性关系（含对数修正）。数值模拟验证了这些预测在一维和二维铁磁海森堡模型、Fredkin自旋链及二维共振价键态模型中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该协议能够完全数字化地稳定无能隙多体基态，无需模拟旋转操作，为近期实验提供了超越传统绝热方法的高保真态制备途径。该方法在系统尺寸的多项式时间内实现未知基态制备，为量子模拟中的基态制备问题提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Preparing algebraically correlated ground states of quantum many-body systems is an important, yet challenging task for quantum simulation. We introduce a protocol that employs local projective measurements and unitary feedback for frustration-free gapless systems. Our approach prepares a priori unknown ground states in time that scales polynomially with system size. We analytically show the performance our protocol for the dynamics of a single-particle; we argue the same mechanism generalizes to many-body systems based on the physics of quasiparticles. Our theory predicts that a transient cooling dynamics directly reveals the system's universal critical properties. In particular, the state preparation time is linear in the inverse of the finite-size gap (up to log correction) when the system's dynamical critical exponent is larger or equal the effective spatial dimension explored by the quasiparticles. We verify these predictions in numerical simulations of ferromagnetic Heisenberg models in one- and two dimensions, a Fredkin spin chain, and a two-dimensional model of resonating valence bond states. Our protocol stabilizes gapless many-body ground states fully digitally without requiring analog rotations, enabling access to high-fidelity states beyond conventional adiabatic approaches in near-term experiments.

### [56] [Light-Matter Interactions Beyond the Dipole Approximation in Extended Systems Without Multipole Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10271)
*Rishabh Dora,Roman Korol,Vishal Tiwari,Rahul Chourasiya,Ignacio Franco*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个超越电偶极近似（EDA）的光-物质相互作用理论框架，适用于纳米/微米尺度材料与空间结构电场的相互作用。该框架基于PZW哈密顿量和最大局域化Wannier函数（MLWFs），能够以标准偶极计算的计算成本捕获超越偶极的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于Power-Zienau-Woolley（PZW）哈密顿量描述光-物质相互作用，并结合材料哈密顿量的最大局域化Wannier函数（maximally localized Wannier functions, MLWFs）表示。该框架适用于均匀和非均匀强度电场，并考虑系统尺寸与光波长的不同比例关系。

Result: 研究发现，对于均匀照明的1-D或2-D材料，当光垂直入射时，EDA表现出惊人的鲁棒性。然而，对于3-D材料或低维材料的非垂直入射，当波长与系统尺寸相当时，EDA开始失效。此外，材料部分或非均匀照明时EDA也会失效。对于缓慢变化的场强度，可通过有限阶多极修正来纠正，但对于急剧变化的场，多极修正计算上不切实际。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法能够以标准偶极计算的计算成本捕获超越偶极的光-物质相互作用，为纳米器件、量子材料和界面的空间结构光-物质动力学提供了准确的第一性原理模拟途径。

Abstract: We present a general theoretical framework to capture light-matter interactions beyond the electric-dipole approximation (EDA), applicable to extended nano- and microscale materials interacting with spatially structured electric fields without truncation at finite multipolar order. The approach is based on the Power-Zienau-Woolley (PZW) Hamiltonian for light-matter interactions and a representation of the material's Hamiltonian in a basis of maximally localized Wannier functions (MLWFs), obtainable from first-principles calculations. We utilize this approach to clarify the limitations of the ubiquitous dipole approximation. We consider electric fields with both uniform and non-uniform intensities and a range of ratios of system size to the wavelength of light. Through this analysis, we identify the conditions under which the EDA breaks down, leading to significant errors in the light-induced dynamics. Contrary to conventional belief, we find that the EDA is remarkably robust for uniformly illuminated 1-D or 2-D materials when light propagates perpendicular to the material. For 3-D materials or non-perpendicular illumination of lower-dimensional materials, conventional wisdom holds and the EDA begins to break down when the wavelength becomes comparable to the system size. Furthermore, the EDA fails when the material is illuminated partially or non-uniformly. For slowly varying field intensities this failure can be corrected by finite-order multipolar corrections. However, for fields that vary substantially, correcting via multipolar terms becomes computationally impractical. In contrast, our approach captures beyond-dipole light-matter interactions at the computational cost of a standard dipole calculation. This efficiency enables accurate first-principles simulations of spatially structured light-matter dynamics in nanoscale devices, quantum materials, and interfaces.

Abstract: Quantum fluctuation relations provide a microscopic formulation of thermodynamics beyond equilibrium, but experimentally accessing many-body quantum work statistics remains an outstanding challenge. The quantum piston constitutes a canonical model of boundary-driven nonequilibrium dynamics, where finite-time deformation of a confining potential generates non-adiabatic transitions, dissipation and irreversibility. Here we experimentally simulate the nonequilibrium dynamics of a two-boson quantum piston on a programmable photonic quantum computer. Using two indistinguishable photons, we encode a truncated piston propagator through a quasi-unitary embedding, with an ancilla mode representing leakage into higher-energy states outside the resolved manifold. This architecture enables direct reconstruction of thermodynamic transition statistics for both expansion and compression protocols as functions of driving speed and final trap length. We observe the crossover from quasi-adiabatic to strongly non-adiabatic evolution and show that bosonic interference restructures the resulting two-particle Fock-state populations and work distributions. The measured statistics are in close agreement with theoretical predictions and satisfy the Jarzynski equality across expansion and compression protocols for cyclic driving we further quantify irreversibility through dissipated work and state overlap. Our work identifies programmable photonic quantum hardware as a powerful platform for simulating nonequilibrium quantum thermodynamics and for experimentally resolving how indistinguishability and many-body interference shape quantum work, dissipation and entropy production.

Method: 利用随机矩阵理论（RMT）的预测作为遍历性基准，重点关注两个RMT预测：量子费希尔信息（quantum Fisher information）的时间演化，以及涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）。在三种遍历性破缺机制中进行分析。

Abstract: Quantum many-body systems can exhibit distinct regimes where dynamics is either ergodic, dynamically exploring an extensive region of available state-space, or non-ergodic, where the dynamics may be restricted. An example is the many-body localization (MBL) transition, where disorder induces non-ergodic behaviour. Most measures of ergodicity notably rely on global quantities, such as level spacing statistics. We explore the ability for a subsystem to probe the ergodicity of dynamics via measurement of local observables, and use expected results from random matrix theory (RMT) as a benchmark for the ergodic regime. We exploit two predictions from RMT as ergodicity is broken: the time evolution of the quantum Fisher information, and a fluctuation-dissipation relation. These are investigated in three different ergodicity breaking mechanisms, namely, as a consequence of transition to integrability, MBL, and Quantum Many-Body Scars (QMBS). We show that the predicted behaviour from RMT can be used as a potential witness for transition to non-ergodic behaviour from the measurement of local observables alone.

### [59] [Universal purification dynamics in real non-unitary quantum processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10751)
*Federico Gerbino,Donghoon Kim,Guido Giachetti,Andrea De Luca,Xhek Turkeshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受监测量子过程中纯化动力学（purification dynamics）的普适性特征，提出了两种揭示互补视角的玩具模型，并提供了Rényi熵（Rényi entropies）普适衰减的显式表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解混合量子系统中纯化过程（purification process）的普适性类别，特别是在远离测量诱导相变（measurement induced phase transition）的区域和体积/弱测量相（volume/weak measurement phase）内部。研究关注大时间和希尔伯特空间维度（Hilbert space dimension）极限下的普适特征。

Method: 提出了两种互补的玩具模型：i) 离散时间动力学（discrete-time dynamic），其中每个时间步对应乘以高斯随机矩阵（Gaussian random matrix）；ii) 弱连续时间监测（weak continuous-time monitoring），诱导密度矩阵（density matrix）特征值的Dyson布朗运动（Dyson brownian motion）。第一种方法基于Kraus算子空间（Kraus's operator space）中出现的旋转不变性（rotational invariance）提供代数表征；第二种方法通过将特征值的Fokker-Planck演化映射到Calogero-Sutherland可积哈密顿量（Calogero-Sutherland integrable Hamiltonian），实现对任意Dyson随机矩阵指数（Dyson random-matrix index）β的统一处理。

Result: 研究提供了Rényi熵普适衰减的显式表达式，并展示了在接近普适标度极限（universal scaling limit）时，不同模型的数值模拟结果相互一致且与理论预测相符。结果阐明了随机电路架构（random circuit architectures）和弱测量协议（weak measurement protocols）中纯化过程存在不同的普适性类别。

Conclusion: 该研究通过两种互补方法揭示了受监测量子过程中纯化动力学的普适特征，为理解混合量子系统中纯化过程的普适性类别提供了理论框架和定量工具，特别关注了不同随机矩阵对称性类（random-matrix symmetry classes）中的普适行为。

Abstract: We study purification dynamics in monitored quantum processes governed by ensembles of quantum circuits in different random-matrix symmetry classes. We analyze the universal aspects that emerge away from the measurement induced phase transition and inside the volume/weak measurement phase and in the scaling limit of large time and Hilbert space dimension. We present two toy models that reveal two complementary visions and provide quantitative access to universal scaling: i) a discrete-time dynamic in which each time step corresponds to multiplication by a Gaussian random matrix; ii) weak continuous-time monitoring that induces a Dyson brownian motion of the eigenvalues of the density matrix. The first approach provides an algebraic characterization based on rotational invariance emerging in Kraus's operator space, focusing in particular on the unitary and orthogonal cases, respectively $β=2$ and $β=1$, with $β$ the Dyson random-matrix index. The second approach, on the other hand, allows for a unified treatment for any $β$, thanks to the mapping of the Fokker-Planck evolution of eigenvalues onto the Calogero-Sutherland integrable Hamiltonian diagonalized in terms of Jack polynomials. We provide explicit expressions for the universal decrease of Rényi entropies. We show that, approaching the universal scaling limit, numerical simulations of different models agree with each other and with our theoretical predictions. Our results clarify the existence of different classes of universality for the purification process in hybrid quantum systems, accessible in random circuit architectures and weak measurement protocols.

### [60] [Open quantum systems beyond equilibrium: Lindblad equation and path integral molecular dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10839)
*Benedikt M. Reible,Somayeh Ahmadkhani,Luigi Delle Site*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了Lindblad方程与路径积分分子动力学（PIMD）之间的形式等价关系，使得PIMD能够用于计算非平衡情况下系综平均物理量的时间演化及其向稳态的收敛，而无需显式求解Lindblad方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lindblad方程虽然适用于任意系统尺寸，但在实际应用中受限于量子复杂性，通常只能处理原型模型。PIMD能够处理包含数千原子的平衡系统，但无法描述非平衡情况下的直接时间演化和稳态收敛。本研究旨在分析两者之间的联系。

Method: 通过建立Lindblad方程与PIMD之间的形式等价关系，论证PIMD可用于计算非平衡情况下系综平均物理量的时间演化。采用化学物理中感兴趣的原型系统进行数值研究，以展示该方法。

Result: 研究建立了Lindblad方程与PIMD之间的形式等价关系，使得PIMD能够绕过显式求解Lindblad方程的需求，直接计算非平衡情况下物理量的时间演化和稳态收敛。该等价关系为PIMD结果的一致性提供了论证依据。

Conclusion: Lindblad方程与PIMD之间存在形式等价关系，这一联系不仅使得PIMD能够用于非平衡情况的时间演化计算，同时也为PIMD结果（特别是密度算符的正定性）的一致性提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: The Lindblad equation determines the time evolution of the density operator of open quantum systems. While valid for any system size, its use is, in practice, restricted to prototype/surrogate models with the aim of tackling specific aspects of the overall quantum complexity of a multi-atomic system. Path integral molecular dynamics (PIMD) instead provides static and dynamical quantum statistical averages of physical observables for systems in equilibrium composed of up to thousands of atoms over timescales up to nanoseconds, under the condition that short-time quantum coherence is not relevant for the properties of interest. PIMD relies on the well-established technique of molecular dynamics (MD) with its associated classical trajectories. However, it cannot describe a direct time evolution of a system and its convergence to a stationary state in situations out of equilibrium. In this work, we analyze the link between the Lindblad equation and PIMD; specifically, we will discuss how PIMD can actually be used to calculate the time evolution of ensemble-averaged physical observables and their convergence to a stationary state for situations out of equilibrium, bypassing the need of explicitly solving the Lindblad equation. Yet, at the same time, the Lindblad equation and PIMD are linked to one another through a formal relation of equivalence, which provides an argument for the consistency of PIMD results, namely the positivity of the density operator at any time. A numerical study of a prototype system, which is of interest in chemical physics, will be used to showcase the method.

### [61] [Star Topology Optimizes the Charging Power of Quantum Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10853)
*Matthieu Sarkis,Oskar A. Prośniak,Samuel Nigro,Alexandre Tkatchenko*

TL;DR: 该研究证明星型拓扑（star topology）在量子电池早期充电功率方面具有最优性能，为可扩展量子电池平台提供了架构设计指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电池（quantum batteries）的实用价值取决于其充电速度，虽然已知集体充电协议和全局控制能提升充电功率，但电池内部相互作用架构如何约束性能尚不清楚。

Method: 研究相互作用费米子电池（interacting fermionic batteries），其内部耦合由图邻接矩阵（graph adjacency matrix）编码，通过与外部费米子设备的简单相互作用进行充电。通过穷举搜索N≤7的所有图，并在更大N时与随机图集合进行基准测试。

Result: 证明星型拓扑（star topology）最大化早期充电功率，这是量子电池质量度量中广泛使用的最大平均功率（maximal average power）的代理指标。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了架构作为快速充电的可控旋钮，并激励在可扩展量子电池平台中采用中心辐射型设计（hub-and-spoke designs）。

Abstract: Quantum batteries are quantum systems that store energy and deliver it on demand, and their practical value hinges on how fast they can be charged. While collective charging protocols and global control are known to enhance charging power, it remains unclear how the battery's internal interaction architecture itself constrains performance. Here we study interacting fermionic batteries whose internal couplings are encoded by a graph adjacency matrix, charged via a simple interaction with an external fermionic device. We prove that the star topology maximises the early time charging power, which proxies the maximal average power - a widely used quantum battery quality metric. We substantiate the result numerically by an exhaustive sweep over all graphs with $N\leq 7$ vertices and by benchmarks against random graph ensembles at larger $N$. Our findings shed light on architecture as a controllable knob for fast charging and motivate hub-and-spoke designs in scalable quantum-battery platforms.

</details>

### [62] [CHRONOS Science Program](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10070)
*Yuki Inoue,Mario Juvenal S Onglao,Vivek Kumar,Daiki Tanabe*

Method: 采用低温扭杆干涉仪配置（cryogenic torsion-bar interferometric configuration）结合量子非破坏速度计读数（quantum non-demolition speed-meter readout）技术。这种设计专门针对亚赫兹频段进行优化，以实现前所未有的探测灵敏度。

Result: CHRONOS将能够长期追踪致密双星系统在合并前的演化过程，显著改进源定位、参数估计和对广义相对论的检验。同时，它还能探测亚赫兹频段的随机引力波背景，对原初引力波、暴胀张量谱、一级相变、宇宙弦等高能物理遗迹提供强有力约束。

Abstract: Cryogenic sub-Hz cROss torsion-bar detector with quantum NOn-demolition Speed meter(CHRONOS) is a proposed next-generation ground-based gravitational-wave observatory designed to explore the sub-Hz frequency band with unprecedented sensitivity. Utilizing a cryogenic torsion-bar interferometric configuration with quantum non-demolition speed-meter readout, CHRONOS targets a frequency window that bridges space-based missions and current high-frequency ground-based detectors, opening a new frontier in gravitational-wave astronomy. The observatory will enable long-duration tracking of compact binary inspirals well before merger, significantly improving source localization, parameter estimation, and tests of general relativity. In addition to transient signals, CHRONOS is optimized to probe the stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) in the sub-Hz regime, providing powerful constraints on primordial gravitational waves, inflationary tensor spectra with red or blue tilts, first-order phase transitions, cosmic strings, and other relics of high-energy physics. By connecting gravitational-wave measurements across cosmological frequency scales-from cosmic microwave background polarization to pulsar timing arrays and high-frequency interferometers-CHRONOS will contribute to a coherent reconstruction of the gravitational-wave spectrum over more than twenty orders of magnitude. Crossing critical sensitivity thresholds in the sub-Hz band, CHRONOS will establish a new pillar of gravitational-wave astronomy and cosmology, enabling transformative advances in astrophysics and fundamental physics.

### [63] [Fragmentation contributions to transverse nucleon spin observables in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering at NLO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10628)
*Diego Scantamburlo,Marc Schlegel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了半包含深度非弹性轻子-核子碰撞中的自旋相关截面，重点关注横向动量积分后的截面，并在微扰QCD的共线扭曲-3因子化框架下分析了大虚度Q^2下的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究半包含深度非弹性散射（semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering, SIDIS）中自旋相关截面的物理机制，特别关注两个主要横向自旋观测量：单核子自旋不对称性（single nucleon spin asymmetry, SSA）和双纵向轻子-横向核子自旋不对称性（double longitudinal lepton-transverse nucleon spin asymmetry, DSA）。

Method: 在微扰量子色动力学（perturbative QCD）的共线扭曲-3因子化（collinear twist-3 factorization）框架下，分析大虚度Q^2下的截面，并研究手征-奇（chiral-odd）扭曲-3三部分子碎裂函数（three-parton fragmentation functions）的贡献，计算到次领头阶（Next-To-Leading Order, NLO）。

Result: 明确观察到在单圈水平上共线扭曲-3因子化对这些贡献成立，将NLO公式与HERMES实验数据进行比较，并为电子-离子对撞机（EIC）运动学提供了数值预测。

Conclusion: 成功建立了半包含深度非弹性散射中自旋相关截面的NLO理论框架，验证了扭曲-3因子化的有效性，并为未来EIC实验提供了理论预测。

Abstract: We study the spin-dependent cross section in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic lepton-nucleon collisions, $\ell + N^\uparrow\to \ell+h+X$. We focus on the cross section that is integrated over the transverse momentum $P_{h\perp}$ of the detected unpolarized hadron. We analyze this cross section at large virtuality $Q^2$ of the exchanged virtual photon within the framework of collinear twist-3 factorization in perturbative QCD. The two main transverse spin observables, the single nucleon spin asymmetry (SSA) and the double longitudinal lepton-transverse nucleon spin asymmetry (DSA), both receive contributions from chiral-odd twist-3 three-parton fragmentation functions. We study these fragmentation contributions to Next-To-Leading Order (NLO) in perturbative QCD. We explicitly observe that collinear twist-3 factorization holds for these contributions at the one-loop level. We confront our NLO formulae with HERMES data and provide numerical predictions for EIC kinematics.

*Omer Albayrak,Tanmay Vachaspati*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索散射体（scatterer）与涡旋自由度之间通过中介量子变量（intermediary quantum variables）间接相互作用时，全局涡旋产生的物理机制，特别是在参数空间中涡旋产生的敏感性和混沌特性。

Method: 研究方法采用2+1维数值模拟，包含支持全局涡旋的复标量场φ、作为散射体的实标量场ψ，以及作为中介耦合两者的量子场ρ。通过模拟相对论性高斯波包（relativistic Gaussian wavepackets）的散射过程，并扫描参数空间来识别涡旋-反涡旋对产生的区域。

Result: 结果显示涡旋产生对初始高斯参数高度敏感，参数空间呈现混沌特性，包含"空洞（holes）"和孤立的涡旋产生区域，表明涡旋产生过程具有复杂的非线性动力学行为。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，通过中介量子变量耦合的散射过程能够产生全局涡旋-反涡旋对，且该过程对初始条件极为敏感，参数空间结构复杂，揭示了此类系统中涡旋产生的非平凡动力学特性。

Abstract: We study global vortex production in (numerical) scattering experiments when the scatterer and the vortex degrees of freedom interact only due to intermediary quantum variables. We work in $2+1$ dimensions with a complex scalar field, $φ$, that supports global vortices, a real scalar field, $ψ$, that is the scatterer, and a quantum field, $ρ$, that couples to both $φ$ and $ψ$, acting as a mediator. We simulate the scattering of relativistic Gaussian wavepackets of $ψ$ and scan parameter space for regions where vortex-antivortex pairs are produced. The results show that vortex production is highly sensitive to the initial Gaussian parameters, and the parameter space is chaotic with ``holes" and isolated regions of vortex production.

### [65] [Mapping the critical region along the second-order chiral phase boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10260)
*Shi Yin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文使用功能重整化群（fRG）方法研究夸克-介子模型中手征相变临界标度区域的范围随化学势增加的变化，发现标度区域随化学势增加而系统性收缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限化学势下手征相变临界标度区域的范围，这对于理解量子色动力学（QCD）相图在有限密度下的临界行为具有重要意义。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalization group, fRG）方法分析夸克-介子（quark-meson, QM）模型，通过分析手征序参量和关联长度在二阶相变附近随温度和π介子质量的标度行为来提取临界指数。

Result: 研究发现，随着化学势增加，主导阶和次主导阶的标度区域均系统性收缩；这一现象在局域势近似（local potential approximation, LPA）及其包含反常维度的扩展（LPA'）中均被观察到，且LPA'中的标度区域略小于LPA。

Conclusion: 有限化学势下，手征相变的临界标度区域范围随化学势增加而减小，这一结论在LPA和LPA'两种近似下均成立，为理解QCD相图在有限密度下的临界行为提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the extent of the critical scaling region of the chiral phase transition at finite chemical potential within the quark-meson (QM) model using the functional renormalization group (fRG) approach. By analyzing the scaling behavior of the chiral order parameter and correlation length with respect to temperature and pion mass near the second-order phase transition, we extract critical exponents from the data and quantify the range over which the scaling relations remain valid. We find that both the leading order and the next-to-leading-order scaling regions systematically shrink as the chemical potential increases. This behavior is observed in both the local potential approximation (LPA) and its extension including anomalous dimensions (LPA'), with qualitatively consistent results, while the scaling region in LPA' is slightly smaller than that in LPA.

### [66] [Geometric control of motility-induced phase separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10259)
*Toler H. Webb,Helen S. Ansell,Daniel M. Sussman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了弱曲率对活性物质非平衡相分离的几何控制作用，通过环面（torus）上的活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）系统，展示了曲率如何调控运动诱导相分离（MIPS）的簇结构形态和位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 曲率（curvature）显著影响软物质、活性物质和生物材料的集体性质。研究旨在探索曲率如何控制运动诱导相分离（motility-induced phase separation, MIPS）这一典型的非平衡相变，特别是弱曲率和缓慢变化曲率对MIPS致密相的影响。

Method: 研究聚焦于限制在环面（torus）表面的活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）系统。通过改变环面的纵横比（aspect ratio），分析曲率变化如何驱动致密簇的结构转变，并比较不同理论框架对MIPS相的预测。

Result: 研究发现，即使弱且缓慢变化的曲率也能对MIPS致密相提供稳健的几何控制，包括决定MIPS簇的位置和形态。改变纵横比驱动了致密簇从位于外赤道的圆盘（disk）到环绕小圆周的带状结构（band）的结构转变。通过分析簇边界几何，比较了热力学和动力学图景预测的结构差异。

Conclusion: 曲率空间不仅是塑造和引导非平衡动力学的工具，更是探测活性物质（active matter）基本机制的独特敏感平台。研究结果为利用几何控制非平衡相变提供了新视角。

Abstract: Curvature fundamentally alters the collective properties of soft, active, and biological materials. Here we study motility-induced phase separation (MIPS), a canonical non-equilibrium transition, and demonstrate that even weak and slowly varying curvature provides robust geometric control over the dense MIPS phase. This includes dictating both the location and morphology of the MIPS cluster, even in regimes where the effect on the overall phase boundaries is minimal. Focusing on active Brownian particles confined to the surface of a torus, we show that varying the aspect ratio drives a structural transition of the dense cluster from a disk localized at the outer equator to a band wrapping the minor circumference. We then discuss how the curved geometry provides a platform for comparing different theoretical frameworks for the MIPS phase: by analyzing the geometries of the cluster boundaries, we compare the structures predicted by thermodynamic and kinetic pictures. Our results establish curved space not only as a tool to shape and guide non-equilibrium dynamics, but as a uniquely sensitive arena for probing the fundamental mechanisms of active matter.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究垂直振动板间单层非极性棒状介质中运动棒状粒子的动力学行为，并通过最小平均场模型对观察到的现象进行理论解释。

Result: 发现反扩散不稳定性导致运动棒状粒子与非极性介质分离并形成集群，集群尺寸随介质浓度增加而增大；增强的分离反而降低了全局极性有序度；集群结构受介质棒状粒子各向异性影响显著，小长径比时集群沿运动垂直方向伸长，大长径比时沿运动方向伸长。

Conclusion: 运动棒状粒子在非极性介质中表现出反扩散不稳定性导致的相分离和集群形成，这种分离诱导的无序现象可以通过最小平均场模型进行合理化解释，揭示了介质各向异性对集群结构的关键影响。

Abstract: We investigate the collective behavior of motile rods immersed in a monolayer of apolar rods confined between vertically vibrating plates using numerical simulations. We uncover an antidiffusive instability whereby motile rods segregate from the apolar medium and form flocks whose size increases with the medium concentration. Remarkably, enhanced segregation leads to a reduction of the global polar order. The flock structure is strongly influenced by the anisotropy of the medium rods. For small aspect ratios, the flocks are elongated perpendicular to the mean direction of motion, whereas for larger aspect ratios, they elongate along the direction of motility. We rationalize the emergence of segregation-induced disorder using a minimal mean-field model.

### [68] [Theory of Cell Body Lensing and Phototaxis Sign Reversal in "Eyeless" Mutants of $Chlamydomonas$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10986)
*Sumit Kumar Birwa,Ming Yang,Adriana I. Pesci,Raymond E. Goldstein*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了绿藻衣藻（Chlamydomonas reinhardtii）趋光性符号反转的定量理论，解释了无眼点突变体相对于野生型趋光方向逆转的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释衣藻无眼点突变体（"eyeless" mutants）趋光性符号反转的现象。十年前发现衣藻球形细胞体作为透镜会聚入射光，当聚焦光从后方到达光感受器时，导致突变体相对于野生型趋光方向发生逆转。

Method: 通过完善近期关于透镜效应的简化分析，并将其整合到衣藻趋光性的自适应模型中，建立了定量理论。该模型考虑了细胞折射率超过水时内部光焦散（light caustics）的存在。

Result: 模型显示趋光动力学具有微妙特性，光感受器在细胞旋转周期内接收两个竞争信号：来自直接照明的缓慢变化信号，以及更强、更短、快速变化的透镜信号。趋光性符号反转是鞭毛光响应优先响应时间导数更高信号的结果。

Conclusion: 这些特征导致了对趋光性符号反转的定量理解，包括方向选择中的双稳态（bistability），这一预测可在突变体趋光性的单细胞追踪研究中验证。

Abstract: Phototaxis of many species of green algae relies upon directional sensitivity of their membrane-bound photoreceptors, which arises from the presence of a pigmented "eyespot" behind them that blocks light passing through the cell body from reaching the photoreceptor. A decade ago it was discovered that the spherical cell body of the alga $Chlamydomonas~reinhardtii$ acts as a lens to concentrate incoming light, and that in "eyeless" mutants of $Chlamydomonas$ the consequence of that focused light reaching the photoreceptor from behind is a reversal in the sign of phototaxis relative to the wild type behavior. We present a quantitative theory of this sign reversal by completing a recent simplified analysis of lensing [Yang, et al., Phys. Rev. E 113, 022401 (2026)] and incorporating it into an adaptive model for $Chlamydomonas$ phototaxis. This model shows that phototactic dynamics in the presence of lensing is subtle because of the existence of internal light caustics when the cellular index of refraction exceeds that of water. During each period of cellular rotation about its body-fixed axis, the photoreceptor receives two competing signals: a relatively long, slowly-varying signal from the direct illumination, and a stronger, shorter, rapidly-varying lensed signal. The reversal of the sign of phototaxis is then a consequence of the dominance of the flagellar photoresponse to the signal with the higher time derivative. These features lead to a quantitative understanding of phototaxis sign reversal, including bistability in the direction choice, a prediction that can be tested in single-cell tracking studies of mutant phototaxis.

</details>

### [69] [Nuclear Quantum Effects in Multi-Step Condensed Matter Chemistry: A Path Integral Molecular Dynamics Study of Thermal Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10939)
*Jalen Macatangay,Alejandro Strachan*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比路径积分分子动力学（PIMD）、量子热浴（QTB）和经典分子动力学（ClMD）方法，分析了核量子效应（NQEs）对含能材料TATB晶体热分解的影响。研究发现PIMD预测更快的化学分解速率，而QTB显著高估了量子加速效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核量子效应（Nuclear Quantum Effects, NQEs）对化学反应速率预测至关重要，但在凝聚态体系研究中常被忽略或近似处理。本研究旨在阐明NQEs在分子晶体中多步骤、多分子反应中的作用，特别是对含能材料TATB热分解过程的影响。

Method: 采用三种方法对比研究TATB晶体的热分解：路径积分分子动力学（Path Integral Molecular Dynamics, PIMD）通过将每个原子表示为珠串（beads）来采样量子正则分布；量子热浴（Quantum Thermal Bath, QTB）使用频率相关恒温器再现玻色-爱因斯坦分布；经典分子动力学（Classical MD, ClMD）作为基准。

Result: PIMD显示TATB晶体化学分解比ClMD更快，初始步骤涉及氢转移过程。有趣的是，后续反应（如N2形成）在相同时间尺度发生。PIMD预测总体活化能比经典结果降低约8%。QTB显著高估了化学反应的量子加速效应和活化能降低幅度。

Conclusion: 核量子效应对TATB晶体热分解具有重要影响，PIMD提供了更准确的量子效应描述。QTB方法在复杂多分子反应中显著高估量子效应，通过对比PIMD和质心动力学（centroid dynamics）的动能算符可深入理解两者差异的物理机制。

Abstract: Nuclear quantum effects (NQEs) are often central to a predictive understanding of chemical reactions and rates. While their incorporation in gas-phase reactions is well established, studies involving condensed matter often neglect or approximate such effects. To clarify the role of NQEs in multi-step, multi-molecular reactions in a molecular crystal, we compare atomistic simulations of the thermal decomposition of the energetic material TATB using path integral molecular dynamics (PIMD), the more approximate quantum thermal bath (QTB), and classical MD (ClMD). PIMD samples the quantum canonical distribution by representing each atom as a string of beads (replicas), while QTB uses a frequency-dependent thermostat to reproduce the Bose-Einstein distribution. We find that PIMD results in faster chemical decomposition of the TATB crystal compared to ClMD, as the initial steps involve hydrogen transfer processes. Interestingly, some of the subsequent reactions (e.g. the formation of N2) occur on identical timescales. The PIMD simulations also predict a reduction in overall activation energy by ~8% as compared to the classical result. As observed in model systems and simple unimolecular gas-phase reactions, the QTB significantly overestimates quantum acceleration of chemical reactions and the reduction in activation energy. A comparison of the kinetic energy operator in PIMD and the centroid dynamics provides insight into the physics behind the differences between the QTB and PIMD results.

</details>

### [70] [Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky quantization of Einstein gravity with off-diagonal solutions encoding Hořava type generating functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10082)
*Elşen Veli Veliev,Sergiu I. Vacaru*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发并应用Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky（BFV）形式体系来量化广义相对论中爱因斯坦方程的非对角解，这些解在量子引力的准经典极限下具有特定非线性对称性并编码了具有各向异性标度和有效宇宙学常数的Hořava-Lifshitz构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发BFV形式体系以量化广义相对论中爱因斯坦方程的非对角解（off-diagonal solutions），这些解在量子引力的准经典极限下具有重要物理意义。

Conclusion: 本文成功开发并应用BFV形式体系量化了广义相对论中的非对角解，揭示了这些解在准经典极限下的非线性对称性和与Hořava-Lifshitz理论的联系。

Abstract: We develop and apply the Batalin-Fradkin-Vilkovisky (BFV) formalism for quantizing off-diagonal solutions of the Einstein equations in general relativity. Abstract: Horizon scale imaging and precision lensing have turned black holes into quantitative laboratories for strong gravity and for non standard electromagnetic physics. ### [73] [Regular Geometries from Singular Matter in Quasi-Topological Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10110)
*Pablo Bueno,Robie A. Hennigar,Ángel J. Murcia,Aitor Vicente-Cano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 真空准拓扑引力（vacuum quasi-topological gravity）的无穷级数作用量满足马尔可夫极限曲率假设（Markov's limiting curvature hypothesis），但加入物质耦合后该性质被破坏。研究建立了保证曲率有界的充分条件，并发现特定非最小耦合理论可恢复马尔可夫假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究真空准拓扑引力耦合物质后如何影响马尔可夫极限曲率假设。该假设认为球对称解是正则的，且所有曲率不变量受限于与解无关的尺度。需要探究物质耦合是否会破坏这一性质。

Method: 首先分析最小耦合（minimally coupled）物质如何破坏真空方程的标度性质；然后建立一般静态球对称应力-能量张量的充分条件，确保对应解具有有界曲率；最后探索包含无穷高阶曲率和电磁项作用量的非最小耦合（non-minimal couplings）理论。

Result: 最小耦合物质破坏了马尔可夫假设的标度性质，但几何结构通常保持正则。建立的充分条件覆盖了正则物质区域和特定奇异物质分布。非最小耦合理论中，马尔可夫假设可以恢复：存在与质量和电荷无关的曲率普适上界。

Conclusion: 准拓扑引力与物质的耦合存在微妙性，马尔可夫极限曲率假设可作为重整化引力-物质有效理论（resummed gravity-matter effective theories）的选择判据。该研究对理解这些模型中的质量暴胀（mass inflation）现象具有潜在意义。

Abstract: Vacuum quasi-topological gravity with infinitely many terms in the action satisfies Markov's limiting curvature hypothesis: the spherically symmetric solutions are regular and all curvature invariants are bounded by solution-independent scales. We study how this picture changes when the theory is coupled to matter. We find that minimally coupled matter spoils the scaling properties of the vacuum equations that lead to the validity of Markov's hypothesis, but the corresponding geometries often remain regular. We make this precise by developing a set of sufficient conditions on general static, spherically symmetric stress-tensors such that the corresponding solutions have bounded curvature. These conditions cover regular matter sectors but also singular matter profiles that are sufficiently singular in a sense we quantify. Our conclusions hold independently of the matter field equations and include configurations in which matter exhibits divergent energy density and pressure at finite radius or at Killing horizons, results that may have implications for mass inflation in these models. We then explore non-minimal couplings, focusing on theories with infinite towers of higher-curvature and electromagnetic terms in the action. In this class, Markov's hypothesis can be restored: we present theories admitting a universal upper bound on curvature, independent of the mass and charge. Overall, our results highlight subtleties in coupling quasi-topological gravity to matter and suggest Markov's hypothesis as a potential selection criterion for resummed gravity-matter effective theories.

We investigate the complete set of scalar fluxes at infinity and through the horizon across the relevant parameter space and analyze their harmonic structure as a function of orbital geometry and black-hole spin. Our results advance ongoing efforts to construct accurate waveform models for asymmetric binaries beyond GR and lay the groundwork for precision tests of fundamental physics with next-generation gravitational-wave detectors.

### [75] [Quantum Dynamics of the Schwarzschild Interior in Ashtekar-Barbero Variables with Minimal Length Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10297)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Ashtekar-Barbero公式化（Ashtekar-Barbero formulation）研究量子动力学，首先使用迷你超空间惠勒-德威特量子化（minisuperspace Wheeler-DeWitt quantization）分析标准薛定谔表示（Schrödinger representation）。随后引入广义不确定原理（GUP），通过正则代数变形（deformation of the canonical algebra）诱导最小长度效应，求解修正后的惠勒-德威特方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）。

Result: 研究发现，在标准量子化中，"湮灭至无"行为仅出现在特定的因子排序选择（specific choice of factor ordering）下，并非普适现象。当包含GUP修正后，通过构建局域于视界的（localized at the horizon）高斯波包（Gaussian wave packets）进行分析，发现"湮灭至无"行为被显著抑制。

Conclusion: 最小长度效应（minimal-length effects）从本质上改变了黑洞内部的量子动力学，挑战了"湮灭至无"场景作为奇点解决机制（singularity resolution mechanism）的鲁棒性。这表明量子引力修正对黑洞内部行为的描述具有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the quantum dynamics of the Schwarzschild interior in the Ashtekar-Barbero formulation, focusing on the fate of the classical singularity and the annihilation-to-nothing scenario. Using minisuperspace Wheeler-DeWitt quantization, we first analyze the standard Schrödinger representation and show that the annihilation-to-nothing behavior appears only for a specific choice of factor ordering and is not generic.
  We then introduce a generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), which induces minimal-length effects through a deformation of the canonical algebra. Solving the modified Wheeler-DeWitt equation and constructing Gaussian wave packets localized at the horizon, we find that the annihilation-to-nothing behavior is suppressed once the GUP corrections are included. Our results indicate that minimal-length effects qualitatively alter the quantum interior dynamics and challenge the robustness of this scenario as a mechanism for singularity resolution.

### [76] [The moduli space of dynamical spherically symmetric black hole spacetimes and the extremal threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10378)
*Yannis Angelopoulos,Christoph Kehle,Ryan Unger*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文完整描述了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-中性标量场系统中，在赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦（Reissner-Nordström）黑洞家族附近无限维模空间（moduli space）内的黑洞形成阈值（black hole threshold）。研究揭示了黑洞形成与不形成解的分类、临界标度律（scaling laws）以及相关的不稳定性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于完整描述爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-中性标量场系统（Einstein-Maxwell-neutral scalar field system）中，在赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦黑洞家族附近的无限维模空间内，黑洞形成的临界行为。这涉及理解黑洞形成阈值附近的动力学特性。

Method: 方法包括在赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦家族附近的模空间邻域内，分析球对称动力学解的行为。研究采用定量控制近阈值解（near-threshold solutions）的技术，证明了解的分类和标度律。

Result: 主要结果包括：(i) 形成黑洞的解最终衰减为赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦黑洞；(ii) 不形成黑洞的解在零无穷远处（null infinity）变为超极端（superextremal）并在特征初值数据的依赖域内全局存在；(iii) 黑洞解子集允许按最终荷质比（charge-to-mass ratio）常数超曲面进行C¹叶状结构（foliation）；(iv) 黑洞阈值是叶状结构的极端叶（extremal leaf）。

Conclusion: 结论表明黑洞阈值在赖斯纳-诺德斯特伦家族附近具有精确的数学描述，临界指数为1/2的普适标度律（universal scaling laws）成立。此外，阿雷塔基斯不稳定性（Aretakis instability）在阈值解的稠密开集中被激活，近阈值亚极端黑洞经历瞬态视界不稳定性（transient horizon instability）。

Abstract: In this paper, we give a complete description of the black hole threshold, locally near the Reissner-Nordström family, in the infinite-dimensional moduli space $\mathfrak M$ of dynamical spherically symmetric solutions to the Einstein-Maxwell-neutral scalar field system. In a neighborhood of the full Reissner-Nordström family in $\mathfrak M$, we prove the following: (i) Any solution that forms a black hole eventually decays to a Reissner-Nordström black hole. (ii) Any solution that fails to collapse into a black hole eventually becomes superextremal along null infinity and exists globally in the domain of dependence of the bifurcate characteristic initial data. (iii) The subset of this neighborhood consisting of black hole solutions admits a $C^1$ foliation by hypersurfaces of constant final charge-to-mass ratio, up to and including extremality. (iv) The mutual boundary between the set of black hole solutions and noncollapsing solutions, i.e., the black hole threshold, is the extremal leaf of the foliation. Black holes which are not on the threshold are asymptotically subextremal. Our quantitative control of near-threshold solutions allows us to prove "universal" scaling laws for the location of the event horizon and its final area and temperature (surface gravity), with critical exponent $\frac 12$. Moreover, we show that the celebrated Aretakis instability is activated for an open and dense set of threshold solutions and that generic near-threshold subextremal black holes experience a transient horizon instability on the timescale of their inverse final temperature.

### [78] [Thermodynamically massless Simpson-Visser black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10429)
*Thanasis Karakasis,Emmanuel N. Saridakis,Zi-Yu Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文重新审视Simpson-Visser (SV)时空的热力学性质，发现在非线性电动力学和负动能标量场耦合的Einstein引力框架下，该正则黑洞具有零热力学质量但非零磁荷，其热力学第一定律以修正形式成立。与相应的奇异黑洞相比，SV正则黑洞在相同热浴中具有更高的自由能，表明奇异构型在热力学上更受青睐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在深入探究Simpson-Visser (SV)时空的热力学特性，特别是在Einstein引力与非线性电动力学（NLED）及负动能标量场耦合的框架下。研究动机源于理解正则黑洞构型的热力学行为及其与相应奇异黑洞的比较。

Method: 采用Euclidean方法分析热力学性质，在积分常数不显式出现在作用量中的表述下重新推导解。通过这种方法，可以一致地处理积分常数在热力学分析中的变化，并计算守恒荷。

Result: 研究发现SV正则黑洞具有零热力学质量，但拥有守恒磁荷，并描述了一个具有单一视界、有限温度和熵的正则黑洞。热力学第一定律以修正形式成立。与正则参数为零时获得的相应奇异黑洞相比，在相同温度和磁化学势的热浴中，SV正则黑洞总是具有更高的自由能。

Conclusion: SV正则黑洞虽然具有正则结构和有限热力学性质，但在热力学上不如相应的奇异黑洞构型稳定。奇异构型在相同热浴条件下具有更低的自由能，因此在热力学上更受青睐，这揭示了正则黑洞与奇异黑洞在热力学稳定性方面的差异。

Abstract: In this work, we scrutinize the thermodynamic properties of the Simpson-Visser (SV) spacetime. Working within Einstein gravity coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED) and a scalar field with negative kinetic energy, we rederive the solution in a formulation where the integration constants do not explicitly appear in the action, allowing them to vary consistently in the thermodynamic analysis. Using the Euclidean method, we show that the regular spacetime structure modifies the boundary contributions to the conserved charge associated with time translations, allowing the NLED sector to cancel the mass term and yielding a black hole with vanishing thermodynamic mass. Nevertheless, the spacetime admits a conserved magnetic charge and describes a regular black hole with a single horizon, finite temperature, and entropy, while the first law of thermodynamics holds in a modified form. We further compare this solution with the corresponding scalar-free singular black hole obtained when the regular parameter vanishes. Placing the two configurations in the same heat bath with identical temperature and magnetic chemical potential, we find that the SV regular black hole always has a larger free energy, indicating that the scalar-free singular configuration is thermodynamically preferred.

</details>


### [79] [Gauss-Bonnet scalarization of charged qOS-black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10461)
*Hong Guo,Wontae Kim,Yun Soo Myung*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了带电量子Oppenheimer-Snyder黑洞在Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet-标量理论中的Gauss-Bonnet标量化现象，重点关注非线性电动力学项的影响。研究发现标量化分为GB⁺和GB⁻两种类型，取决于耦合常数λ的符号，并构建了稳定的标量化黑洞解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索带电量子Oppenheimer-Snyder黑洞在Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet-标量理论中的Gauss-Bonnet标量化行为。特别关注非线性电动力学项如何影响标量化过程，以及不同参数条件下标量化现象的特征。

Method: 采用Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet-标量理论框架，引入非线性电动力学项。标量耦合函数设为$f(φ)=2λφ^2$，其中λ为耦合常数。研究涉及质量M、作用参数α和磁荷P三个关键参数，通过分析GB项的符号变化来研究标量化现象。

Result: 研究发现Gauss-Bonnet标量化分为GB⁺和GB⁻两种情况：当α=0且λ>0时允许GB⁺标量化；当α≠0且λ<0时，在3.5653≤α≤4.6875的窄带范围内出现GB⁻标量化。构建的标量化qcOS黑洞属于单分支解，标量场在视界附近非单调而在无穷远处渐近有限值。稳定性分析表明这些标量化黑洞在线性标量扰动下是稳定的。

Abstract: The Gauss-Bonnet (GB) scalarization for charged quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (cqOS)-black holes is investigated in the Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet-scalar theory with the nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) term. Here, the scalar coupling function to GB term is given by $f(φ)=2λφ^2$ with a coupling constant $λ$. Three parameters of mass ($M$), action parameter ($α$), and magnetic charge ($P$) are necessary to describe the cqOS-black hole, and it may become the qOS-black hole when $P=M$. The GB scalarization of cqOS-black holes comes into two cases GB$^\pm$, depending on the sign of GB term which triggers the different phenomena. For $α=0$ and $λ>0$, GB$^+$ scalarization is allowed, while for $α\not=0$ and $λ<0$, GB$^-$ scalarization appears for a narrow band of $3.5653\le α\le 4.6875$. After discussing the onset GB$^-$ scalarization, we construct scalarized qcOS-black holes which belong to the single branch. The scalar field is nonmonotonic near the horizon while it asymptotes to a finite value at infinity, indicating a distinct scalarization mechanism for negative coupling $λ$. Stability analysis shows these scalarized black holes are linearly stable under scalar perturbations.

### [80] [Energy extraction-driven instability and horizon formation in Kerr-Newman naked singularities and their limiting cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10727)
*Vishva Patel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文对Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman时空中的旋转与电磁能量提取机制进行了统一分析，比较了不同机制的效率，并研究了持续提取对裸奇点长期演化的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自彭罗斯过程（Penrose process）提出以来，从致密天体提取能量一直是广义相对论的核心课题。本研究旨在统一分析不同时空几何中的能量提取机制，并探讨其对无视界天体演化的影响。

Method: 采用粒子能量学（particle energetics）和不可约质量形式（irreducible mass formalism）分析Kerr、Reissner-Nordstrom和Kerr-Newman时空中的能量提取。通过推导质量、自旋和电荷参数的耦合演化方程，研究持续提取下的长期演化。

Result: 纯旋转提取在Kerr时空中受几何约束限制，而电磁相互作用通过有效能层（effective ergoregion）扩大了负能量轨道区域，显著提高了提取效率。在Kerr-Newman几何中，旋转与电荷的联合效应进一步增强了可提取能量。持续提取能逐渐驱动超极端裸奇点（naked singularity）趋向极端边界，特征演化时间尺度约为10^9年。

Conclusion: 能量提取为Reissner-Nordstrom、Kerr和Kerr-Newman裸奇点提供了不稳定的能量指示，并可能导致视界形成作为长期的稳定化结果。

Abstract: Energy extraction from compact objects has been a central topic in general relativity since the introduction of the Penrose process. In this work we present a unified analysis of rotational and electromagnetic energy extraction in Kerr, Reissner-Nordstrom, and Kerr-Newman spacetimes. Using particle energetics and the irreducible mass formalism, we compare the efficiencies of these mechanisms and examine their consequences for horizonless objects. While purely rotational extraction in Kerr spacetime is fundamentally limited by geometric constraints, electromagnetic interactions enlarge the region of negative energy orbits through an effective ergoregion, allowing significantly higher efficiencies. In Kerr-Newman geometry, the combined effect of rotation and charge further enhances the extractable energy. We then study the long-term evolution of over-extremal cases under continuous extraction. By deriving coupled evolution equations for the mass, spin, and charge parameters, we show that continuous extraction can gradually drive a naked singularity toward the extremal bound. For astrophysically realistic luminosities, the characteristic evolution timescale is of order about 10^9 years. These results suggest that energy extraction provides an energetic indication of instability in Reissner-Nordstrom, Kerr, and Kerr-Newman naked singularities and may lead to horizon formation as a long-term stabilizing outcome.

### [81] [Long-lived quasinormal modes, shadows and particle motion in four-dimensional quasi-topological gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10844)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了四维准拓扑引力（four-dimensional quasi-topological gravity）中正则黑洞（regular black holes）的标量场微扰和粒子运动特性，计算了准正规模（quasinormal modes），并探讨了光子运动与圆形测地线（circular geodesics）等特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索四维准拓扑引力框架下正则黑洞的物理特性，特别是标量场微扰和粒子运动行为，以理解这类黑洞与经典黑洞模型的差异。

Method: 采用高阶WKB近似（high-order WKB approximations）配合Padé重整化（Padé resummation）计算准正规模，并通过时域积分（time-domain integration）进行验证；同时分析光子运动、圆形测地线、光子球半径（photon-sphere radius）、阴影尺寸（shadow size）、李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）和ISCO特性。

Result: 对于中等质量的标量场，时域剖面（time-domain profiles）与WKB结果高度吻合；随着质量增加，阻尼率显著降低，接近长寿命模式的准共振态（quasi-resonant regime）；质量足够大时，晚期信号由振荡幂律尾迹（oscillatory power-law tails）主导。光子运动相关量仅与史瓦西（Schwarzschild）值有适度偏差，与黑洞霍金温度（Hawking temperature）的显著变化形成对比。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了四维准拓扑引力中正则黑洞的微扰动力学特征：标量场质量变化导致准正规模行为显著改变，而光子运动特性相对稳定，表明该理论框架下的黑洞在某些方面接近经典解，但在热力学性质上存在差异。

Abstract: We investigate massive scalar perturbations and several characteristics of particle motion in the spacetime of regular black holes arising in four-dimensional quasi-topological gravity. Quasinormal modes are computed using high-order WKB approximations with Padé resummation and verified through time-domain integration. For moderate values of the scalar-field mass, the time-domain profiles confirm the WKB results with excellent accuracy. As the mass increases, the damping rate decreases substantially, indicating the approach to the quasi-resonant regime of long-lived modes. For sufficiently large masses, the late-time signal becomes dominated by oscillatory power-law tails, which mask the quasi-resonant mode in the time-domain profile. In addition, we analyze photon motion and circular geodesics, including the photon-sphere radius, shadow size, Lyapunov exponent, and ISCO characteristics. These quantities exhibit only moderate deviations from their Schwarzschild values, unlike the Hawking temperature of the black hole.

</details>

*Yashmitha Kumaran*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟早期宇宙的一阶相变（first-order phase transition）及其产生的湍流，计算了原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）的能量密度、振幅和频率谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将一阶相变建模为湍流流体，运用相对论流体动力学方程估算物理量；主要研究两种模型，均采用指数Kraichnan函数作为时间退相关函数，并假设等离子体流动中的湍流是平稳的，遵循Kolmogorov湍流条件。

Result: 两种模型均计算了必要的引力波谱，但采用不同的退相关函数：第一个模型使用依赖于波数和时间的退相关函数，第二个模型则使用top hat相关函数来计算各向异性应力。

Conclusion: 新引入的模型遵循自由衰减湍流模型，但在计算中采用了时间依赖的退相关函数，为研究一阶相变产生的引力波背景提供了新的计算框架。

Abstract: This project is aimed at studying the first-order phase transitions, that is presumed to have ensued in the early universe, and its consequences on the primordial gravitational waves. The effects of bubble nucleation, growth, and coalescence are reviewed. The resulting first-order phase transition is taken as the source of the gravitational waves that were produced, in order to determine the energy density, amplitude, and frequency spectra of the relic gravitational wave background. This is accomplished by modelling the first-order phase transition as a turbulent fluid and employing relativistic hydrodynamic equations to estimate the required physical quantities. Two models are majorly studied for all the analysis done in this project. Both models compute the necessary gravitational wave spectra using the exponential Kraichnan function as the temporal decorrelation function. Also, both models contemplate the turbulence in the flow of plasma to be stationary, obeying the conditions dictated by the Kolmogorov turbulence. However, the first model uses a de-coherence function that depends on the wavenumber and time, while, the second model uses the top hat correlation, to compute the anisotropic stress. The new model introduced here adheres to the freely decaying turbulence model, but employs the time dependent de-coherence function in its computations.

Abstract: In the most general formulation of gravity, the metric and connection are independent degrees of freedom, and the connection may include torsion and non-metricity (or distortion, collectively) degrees of freedom, resulting in a huge number of possible dynamical fields. However, the most fields are either non-dynamical or extremely heavy and the general relativity is recovered at low energy. Abstract: We formulate an extended holographic dark energy scenario based on a recently proposed two-parameter generalized entropic functional. Unlike constructions that phenomenologically impose modified entropy-area relations at the horizon level, the present framework is rooted in a microscopic entropy functional and the corresponding microstate counting. For bounded systems, the entropy acquires a generalized holographic scaling with two independent area contributions, recovering the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy in the appropriate limits. Implementing this entropy within the holographic principle, we derive a generalized dark energy density containing two distinct holographic sectors, naturally embedding standard holographic dark energy and $Λ$CDM as limiting cases. We analyze the cosmological evolution for both Hubble and future event horizon cutoffs and show that the model successfully reproduces the matter-to-dark-energy transition. ### [85] [Reduced phase space induced decay conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11010)
*Thomas Thiemann*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对场论中柯西曲面边界条件下的相空间定义问题，提出了一种基于约化相空间（reduced phase space）的衰减问题处理方法。通过设计适应约束代数结构的规范条件，将运动学相空间分解为规范自由度和真实自由度，从而系统性地参数化衰减条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在柯西曲面边界的场论中，相空间定义需要选择边界条件或场的衰减行为。对于规范场论（gauge field theories），初始数据受初值约束限制，但衰减行为通常针对未受约束的运动学相空间（kinematical phase space）指定，这可能导致实际问题：约束求解通常偏好仅代数依赖的场变量，但指定的衰减行为可能阻碍这一过程。

Method: 本文发展了一种约化相空间诱导方法（reduced phase space induced approach）。通过设计适应约束代数结构的规范条件（gauge conditions），将运动学相空间分解为规范自由度（gauge degrees of freedom）和真实自由度（true degrees of freedom）。然后，衰减条件仅需针对真实自由度（即约化相空间）进行选择，规范自由度的衰减则通过求解约束和规范条件唯一确定。

Result: 该方法建立了约束结构与运动学相空间衰减特性之间的系统联系。通过将衰减条件参数化为仅对真实自由度的选择，避免了为所有运动学场指定精确衰减的不必要性，同时确保了规范不变性（gauge invariance）定义所需的泊松括号（Poisson brackets）计算。

Conclusion: 约化相空间诱导方法为解决规范场论中约束结构与衰减特性之间的复杂相互作用提供了系统框架。该方法通过将衰减条件简化为仅对真实自由度的选择，同时确保规范自由度的衰减由约束和规范条件唯一确定，从而优化了相空间边界条件的定义过程。

Abstract: The definition of the phase space of field theories in presence of boundaries of Cauchy surfaces requires a choice of boundary conditions or decay behaviour of those fields. Often these conditions are motivated in part by the decay behaviour of the initial data of known exact solutions.
  In the case of gauge field theories the initial data are not free but are subject to initial value constraints. Still, the decay behaviour is commonly specified for the kinematical, i.e. unconstrained phase space. This can lead to the following practical problem: The constraints are preferably solved for field variables on which they depend only algebraically, i.e. not involving derivatives, as otherwise one would need to solve partial differential equations. However, the specified decay behaviour may prevent from doing that.
  On the other hand, a precise specification of decay for all kinematical fields appears unnecessary because the decay of gauge degrees of freedom is not observable. Yet, knowledge of their decay is required as one needs to compute Poisson brackets on the kinematical phase space in order to define what gauge invariance means. Thus the interplay between the constraint structure and the decay properties of the kinematical phase space is complex.
  In this contribution we develop a reduced phase space induced approach to the decay problem. Upon specifying gauge conditions tailored to the algebraic structure of the constraints, these define a split of the kinematical phase space into gauge and true degrees of freedom. Then the decay conditions of the kinematical phase space is systematically parametrised by a choice of decay for just the true degrees of freedom (i.e. the reduced phase space), the decay of the gauge degrees of freedom then follows unambiguously from solving both the constraints and the gauge conditions.

</details>

Abstract: Heavy-ion experiments at the CERN SPS began in the mid-1980s to study nuclear matter at extreme temperatures and densities. The program started with light ions, such as oxygen and sulphur, at energies of 60A GeV and 200A GeV, later advancing to lead ions at 158A GeV. A series of experiments, employing novel detector technologies, explored various signatures of quark-gluon plasma (QGP) formation. In February 2000, these results led CERN to announce evidence for the QGP formation. Subsequently, an energy scan was conducted with lead ions from 20A GeV to 158A GeV, to locate the threshold of QGP creation.

### [88] [Linear Readout of Neural Manifolds with Continuous Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10956)
*Will Slatton,Chi-Ning Chou,SueYeon Chung*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种统计力学理论，将连续变量（如物体位置和大小）的线性解码效率与神经流形的几何特性联系起来，揭示了沿猴子视觉通路的解码能力增强现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大脑和人工神经网络使用连续变量（如物体位置或刺激方向）进行计算，但神经反应的复杂变异性使得难以将内部表征结构与任务表现联系起来。需要建立理论框架来解析这种关系。

Method: 开发了一种统计力学理论（statistical-mechanical theory）的回归容量（regression capacity）框架，将连续变量的线性解码效率与神经流形（neural manifolds）的几何特性相关联。该理论能够处理复杂的神经变异性并适用于真实数据。

Result: 理论分析揭示了沿猴子视觉通路（monkey visual stream）对物体位置和大小解码能力的增强趋势，表明神经流形的几何特性与解码效率之间存在系统性关系。

Conclusion: 该统计力学理论为理解神经表征结构与连续变量解码性能之间的关系提供了新框架，能够解析复杂神经变异性并揭示视觉信息处理中的系统性容量变化。

Abstract: Brains and artificial neural networks compute with continuous variables such as object position or stimulus orientation. However, the complex variability in neural responses makes it difficult to link internal representational structure to task performance. We develop a statistical-mechanical theory of regression capacity that relates linear decoding efficiency of continuous variables to geometric properties of neural manifolds. Our theory handles complex neural variability and applies to real data, revealing increasing capacity for decoding object position and size along the monkey visual stream.

</details>


### [89] [Uncovering statistical structure in large-scale neural activity with Restricted Boltzmann Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11032)
*Nicolas Béreux,Giovanni Catania,Aurélien Decelle,Francesca Mignacco,Alfonso de Jesús Navas Gómez,Beatriz Seoane*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 该研究使用受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machines, RBMs）建模小鼠大脑约1500-2000个同时记录神经元的群体活动，通过潜在变量扩展最大熵框架，捕捉高阶依赖关系并提取有效交互网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模电生理记录能够同时监测多个脑区的数千个神经元，揭示了神经群体活动的结构化变异性。理解这些集体模式如何从微观神经相互作用中涌现，需要可扩展、可预测且可解释的模型。统计物理学提供了处理这种复杂性的原则性框架，但现有最大熵模型主要局限于成对相互作用和较小系统规模。

Method: 研究使用受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machines, RBMs）建模来自艾伦研究所视觉行为Neuropixels数据集的约1500-2000个同时记录神经元的活动，这些神经元跨越小鼠大脑的多个皮层和皮层下区域。RBMs通过潜在变量扩展最大熵框架，结合高效马尔可夫链采样和训练的最新进展，能够在此规模上准确学习模型。

Result: RBMs以高精度再现了神经记录的复杂统计特性。生成的样本匹配经验性的成对和高阶相关性，以及群体活动分布等全局统计量。推断的参数提供了对有效神经元相互作用的直接访问，揭示了群体活动中的协调模式。这些耦合显示出清晰的解剖结构：视觉皮层区域内的神经元表现出更强的相互作用，与视觉驱动行为一致，而跨区域耦合较弱。尽管在时间洗牌数据上训练，马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛模拟也再现了神经活动的全局弛豫动力学。

Conclusion: 受限玻尔兹曼机为大规模神经群体活动建模提供了可扩展且可解释的框架，能够捕捉高阶依赖关系并提取有效的交互网络，揭示了神经协调的解剖结构基础。

Abstract: Large-scale electrophysiological recordings now allow simultaneous monitoring of thousands of neurons across multiple brain regions, revealing structured variability in neural population activity. Understanding how these collective patterns emerge from microscopic neural interactions requires models that are scalable, predictive, and interpretable. Statistical physics provides principled frameworks to address this complexity, including maximum-entropy models that offer transparent descriptions of collective neural activity but remain largely limited to pairwise interactions and modest system sizes. Here, we use Restricted Boltzmann Machines (RBMs) to model the activity of $\sim1500$-$2000$ simultaneously recorded neurons from the Allen Institute Visual Behavior Neuropixels dataset, spanning multiple cortical and subcortical regions of the mouse brain. RBMs extend the maximum-entropy framework through latent variables, enabling the capture of higher-order dependencies while allowing explicit extraction of effective interaction networks. Recent advances in efficient Markov Chain sampling and training enable accurate learning of these models at this scale. RBMs reproduce the complex statistics of neural recordings with high accuracy. Generated samples match empirical pairwise and higher-order correlations, as well as global statistics such as the distribution of population activity. The inferred parameters provide direct access to effective neuronal interactions, revealing coordination patterns in population activity. These couplings display clear anatomical structure: neurons within visual cortical areas show stronger interactions, consistent with visually driven behavior, while cross-area couplings are weaker. Despite being trained on temporally shuffled data, Markov Chain Monte Carlo simulations also reproduce the global relaxation dynamics of neural activity.

</details>
