### [90] [Plasmon-driven exciton formation in a non-equilibrium Fermi liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10108)
*Rishi Acharya,Eli Gerber,Nina Bielinski,Hannah E. Aguirre,Younsik Kim,Camille Bernal-Choban,Gaurav Tenkila,Suhas Sheikh,Pranav Mahaadev,Faren Hoveyda-Marashi,Subhajit Roychowdhury,Chandra Shekhar,Claudia Felser,Peter Abbamonte,Benjamin J. Wieder,Fahad Mahmood*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在非平衡条件下，费米液体中的集体模式（如体等离子体激元）不仅可作为耗散通道，还能驱动相关电子态的形成，通过体到表面的能量重分布稳定了马汉激子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为费米液体中的集体模式主要通过朗道阻尼耗散电子激发。本研究旨在探索在非平衡条件下，这些集体模式是否能够介导相关电子态的形成，这仍是一个开放性问题。

Method: 采用时间与角分辨光电子能谱（Tr-ARPES）技术研究EuCd$_2$As$_2$材料，并结合电子结构计算进行支持性分析。

Result: 在高激发密度下，观察到等离子体激元将能量从弱色散的体带转移到未占据的表面态。这种体到表面的能量重分布稳定了一个长寿命、能量局域化的谱特征，与马汉激子（Mahan exciton）一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了费米液体物理的一个非平衡机制，其中集体模式不仅耗散能量，还能稳定相关的束缚态，为集体模式在非平衡条件下介导相关电子态形成提供了实验证据。

Abstract: Collective modes in Fermi liquids are usually regarded as dissipation channels that relax electronic excitations through Landau damping. Whether such modes can instead mediate the formation of correlated electronic states under non-equilibrium conditions remains an open question. Here we show that, under optical photo-doping, a bulk plasmon can drive correlated inter-band transfer within a transient electronic continuum. Using time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (Tr-ARPES) on EuCd$_2$As$_2$ supported by electronic structure calculations, we observe that at high excitation density, plasmons transfer energy from a weakly dispersing bulk band into unoccupied surface states. This bulk-to-surface redistribution stabilizes a long-lived, energy-localized spectral feature consistent with a Mahan exciton. Our results uncover a non-equilibrium regime of Fermi-liquid physics in which collective modes do not merely dissipate energy, but also stabilize correlated bound states.

### [91] [A unifying framework for sum rules and bounds on optical, thermoelectric and thermal transport from quantum geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10121)
*M. Nabil Y. Lhachemi,Jennifer Cano*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于广义时变量子几何张量（g-tQGT）的几何框架，用于统一描述清洁零温带绝缘体的光学、热电和热线性响应，揭示了响应张量的几何内容并建立了相关界限关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为清洁零温带绝缘体的光学、热电和热线性响应建立一个统一的几何表述框架。传统方法通常分别处理这些响应，而本文试图通过单一几何对象来统一描述这些现象。

Method: 方法基于构建广义时变量子几何张量（generalized time-dependent quantum geometric tensor, g-tQGT），该张量来源于投影粒子算符和热极化算符的相关函数。采用希尔伯特-施密特内积形式，并利用g-tQGT的时间导数生成广义热电和热求和规则。

Result: AC输运张量获得了紧凑表达式，明确揭示了其几何内容。响应分为贝里曲率贡献（在DC极限下保持有限）和由量子度规支配的频率修正。在热通道中获得了热量子几何张量（thermal quantum geometric tensor），并建立了热QGT迹的界限、投影极化算符的不确定关系以及有限时间累积响应的纯几何上界。

Conclusion: 该几何框架成功统一了带绝缘体的多种线性响应，揭示了即使拓扑平凡绝缘体中也存在几何驱动效应。建立的界限关系可用于推导不同物理对象（如光学质量、磁化率函数和磁化强度）之间的不等式。

Abstract: We present a geometric formulation of optical, thermoelectric, and thermal linear response in clean, zero temperature band insulators based on a single object: a generalized time-dependent quantum geometric tensor (g-tQGT) built from correlations of projected particle and heat polarization operators. Within this framework, the AC transport tensors admit compact expressions that make their geometric content explicit. The response splits into a Berry curvature contribution that remains finite in the DC limit and a frequency correction governed by the quantum metric, implying geometry driven effects even in topologically trivial insulators. At equal times, the g-tQGT recovers the usual integrated QGT and yields energy-weighted thermal analogs whose antisymmetric parts are fixed by orbital and heat magnetization. Importantly, in the thermal channel, a thermal quantum geometric tensor is obtained. Casting the theory in a Hilbert-Schmidt inner product form yields a bound on the trace of the thermal QGT, an uncertainty relation on the projected polarization operators and a purely geometric upper bound on the finite-time accumulated response. The latter is used in the optical channel to derive a geometric upper bound on the electric current. Finally, time derivatives of the g-tQGT are used to generate a hierarchy of generalized thermoelectric and thermal sum rules, and bounds on these sum rules are obtained. These bounds are used to find inequalities between different physical objects such as the optical mass, susceptibility functions and magnetizations.

</details>


### [92] [Unveiling local magnetic moments in copper-oxide atomic junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10129)
*Marcel Strohmeier,Samanwita Biswas,Wolfgang Belzig,Regina Hoffmann-Vogel,Elke Scheer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过低温输运测量，为空气氧化机械可控铜断裂结中的局域磁性提供了实验证据，包括磁输运测量和强零偏压异常下的反常散粒噪声分析，以确定电流的自旋极化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将氧掺入金属原子尺度结会改变原子间键合，甚至可能促进单原子链的形成。对于氧化铜，第一性原理研究预测了铁磁基态的出现，赋予某些原子构型自旋过滤能力，但需要实验验证。

Method: 采用低温输运测量，对空气氧化的机械可控铜断裂结进行实验研究。方法包括磁输运测量以及在强零偏压异常（zero-bias anomalies）存在下的反常散粒噪声（anomalous shot noise）分析。

Result: 提供了一系列实验证据，表明空气氧化机械可控铜断裂结中存在局域磁性。通过分析反常散粒噪声，确定了电流的自旋极化（spin polarization, SP），并用近藤物理（Kondo physics）图像进行解释。

Conclusion: 实验证实了氧化铜原子尺度结中存在局域磁性，并通过散粒噪声分析确定了电流的自旋极化特性，为第一性原理预测的铁磁基态和自旋过滤能力提供了实验支持。

Abstract: Incorporating oxygen into metallic atomic-scale junctions modifies the interatomic bonding and may even promote the formation of monoatomic chains. In the specific case of copper oxide, first-principles studies have predicted the emergence of ferromagnetic ground states, attributing certain atomic configurations with spin filtering capabilities. By means of low-temperature transport measurements, we provide a series of experimental evidence indicating the presence of local magnetism in air oxidized mechanically controllable copper break junctions. Our investigations on ultimately small contacts range from magnetotransport measurements to the analysis of anomalous shot noise in the presence of strong zero-bias anomalies. The analysis of the latter allows to determine the spin polarization (SP) of the current and that is interpreted with the Kondo physics picture.

</details>


### [93] [Geometry of Contact Terms in Linear Response: Applications to Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10144)
*Ian Osborne,Gustavo Monteiro,Barry Bradlyn*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过分析Kubo线性响应公式在计算各向异性系统弹性时产生奇弹性模量（odd elastic moduli）的矛盾，揭示了应变扰动空间的几何结构如何引入修正因子，从而解决哈密顿系统中能量守恒的悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 采用Kubo线性响应形式（Kubo linear response formalism）计算各向异性系统的弹性时会产生奇弹性模量，这与哈密顿系统的能量守恒原则相矛盾。本文旨在解决这一理论上的不一致性。

Method: 通过比较量子线性响应（quantum linear response）的预测与经典弹性理论的期望，建立了一个理论框架。该框架分析了应变扰动空间的几何结构如何引入修正因子。以磁场中的二维电子气作为教学示例，并使用广义f求和规则（generalized f-sum rules）来展示接触项在实验测量中的表现。

Result: 研究发现，应变扰动空间的几何结构会在Kubo公式与弹性模量之间的对应关系中引入修正因子，从而解决了能量守恒的矛盾。通过广义f求和规则证明了接触项在实验测量中的可观测性。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架解决了Kubo线性响应理论在计算弹性模量时产生的理论矛盾，为解释更一般的线性响应函数提供了新的视角。研究结果对理解各向异性系统的弹性性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: Employing the Kubo linear response formalism to calculate the elasticity of anisotropic systems has been shown to yield odd elastic moduli. For Hamiltonian systems, this result seems to be contradictory as it would violate energy conservation. To resolve this discrepancy, we examine the predictions of quantum linear response in the context of our expectation from classical elasticity theory. Our framework reveals that the geometry of the space of strain perturbations introduces correction factors to the correspondence between the Kubo formula and the elastic moduli which resolves the contradiction. We use a two-dimensional gas of electrons in a magnetic field as a pedagogical example. We use generalized f-sum rules to demonstrate how contact terms may reveal themselves in experimental measurements. Finally, we discuss the implications of our results for interpreting more general linear response functions.

</details>


### [94] [Deep learning statistical defect models on magnetic material dynamic and static properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10182)
*C. Eagan,M. Copus,E. Iacocca*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种包含缺陷（特别是空位）的磁化动力学统计模型，结合深度学习技术预测缺陷阈值与物理可观测量之间的关系，为新材料发现和缺陷阈值确定提供基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实磁性材料的建模需要考虑缺陷的影响。基于伪谱Landau-Lifshitz磁化动力学描述，需要开发能够考虑缺陷（特别是空位）的统计模型，以预测缺陷阈值与相关物理可观测量之间的关联。

Method: 提出了一种统计模型，结合深度学习技术，包括卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network）和物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural network）与函数连接理论（theory of functional connections）相结合，预测给定缺陷参数和物理约束下的色散关系。开发了双分支卷积神经网络来预测依赖于缺陷阈值的畴壁宽度。

Result: 所提出的物理信息方法利用深度学习实现了以物理单位测量的统计预测。该方法能够预测缺陷参数下的色散关系，并分别考虑空间分布和畴壁宽度来预测依赖于缺陷阈值的畴壁宽度。

Conclusion: 这是迈向新材料发现和确定所需动力学、状态或拓扑纹理所需最小缺陷阈值的重要基石。该方法为材料设计和缺陷工程提供了有效的计算工具。

Abstract: The modeling of realistic magnetic materials requires the inclusion of defects. Based on the pseudospectral Landau-Lifshitz description of magnetisation dynamics, we propose a statistical model that takes into account defects, specifically vacancies. This statistical model can be integrated with deep learning techniques that correlate defect thresholds with relevant physical observables. We develop a convolutional neural network and a physics-informed neural network combined with theory of functional connections to predict the dispersion relation given defect parameters and physical constraints. A two-branch convolutional neural network is developed to predict domain-wall widths depending on defects threshold, taking into account the spatial profile and domain-wall width separately to achieve a prediction. The proposed physics-informed approaches leverage deep-learning and achieve statistical predictions measured in physical units. This is a stepping stone towards the discovery of new materials and the determination of minimal defect thresholds required for desired dynamics, states, or topological textures.

</details>


### [95] [Charge-tunable Cooper-pair diode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10193)
*Jon Ortuzar,Stefano Trivini,Leonard Edens,F. Sebastian Bergeret,Jose Ignacio Pascual*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了一种基于电子-电子相互作用（electron-electron interactions）的超导二极管（superconducting diode）效应，通过调控纳米尺度铅岛（lead islands）的静电环境实现无需外部磁场的门控可切换超导整流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管作为无耗散电子学的关键构建模块，现有实现方案依赖磁场、铁磁体或复杂异质结构，这限制了器件的集成度和可扩展性。因此需要开发无需外部磁场、结构简单的超导二极管实现方案。

Method: 研究采用纳米尺度超导铅岛，通过将其驱动至库仑阻塞（Coulomb blockade）区域，使库珀对（Cooper-pair）传输通过共振电荷态进行。通过调控岛的静电环境，可控地打破粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry），从而诱导非互易超电流（nonreciprocal supercurrents）。

Result: 该方法实现了无需任何外部磁场的门控可切换超导二极管，能够稳健地整流超导电流和微波光响应（microwave photoresponse）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种可扩展的策略，为超导逻辑器件的发展奠定了基础，通过纯电子-电子相互作用机制实现了超导二极管功能。

Abstract: Superconducting diodes, devices that allow Cooper-pair currents to flow more easily in one direction than the other, are set to become key building blocks for dissipationless electronics. Existing realizations, however, rely on magnetic fields, ferromagnets, or complex heterostructures that hinder integration and scalability. Here we demonstrate a diode effect for Cooper-pairs that arises solely from electron-electron interactions in nanoscale superconducting lead islands. When these islands are driven into the Coulomb blockade regime, Cooper-pair transport occurs through resonant charge states. By tuning the island's electrostatic environment, we controllably break particle-hole symmetry and induce nonreciprocal supercurrents, thereby achieving a gate-switchable superconducting diode without any external magnetic field. Our approach enables robust rectification of superconducting currents and microwave photoresponse, providing a scalable strategy to superconducting logic devices.

</details>


### [96] [Spin Inertia as a Driver of Chaotic and High-Speed Ferromagnetic Domain Walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10310)
*A. L. Bassant,Y. M. J. Ohlsen,M. Cherkasskii,P. B. He,R. A. Duine*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探索了铁磁体中自旋惯性效应对磁畴壁运动的影响，发现惯性效应导致畴壁呈现类质量动力学行为，在无阻尼条件下产生混沌运动，有阻尼条件下则能显著提升畴壁速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于近期实验发现的自旋动力学中的惯性效应，旨在探索该效应对磁畴壁（magnetic domain wall）运动的影响，这对赛道存储器（racetrack memory）等非易失性存储设备的发展具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法基于铁磁体中单个磁矩（magnetic moments）的惯性动力学，分析其对磁畴壁集体运动的影响。研究考察了磁场、自旋转移矩（spin-transfer torque）和自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque）三种驱动机制下的畴壁动力学。

Result: 研究发现磁矩的惯性动力学诱导了畴壁的类质量动力学（massive dynamics）。在无吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）条件下，畴壁运动呈现混沌行为，类似于二维晶体中的电子运动。有限阻尼条件下，类场驱动（field-like driving）能显著提升畴壁速度。低驱动极限下，畴壁宽度因自旋惯性而收缩。

Conclusion: 自旋惯性效应显著改变了磁畴壁的动力学特性，在无阻尼时导致混沌运动，有阻尼时则能提升畴壁速度，这为优化赛道存储器等非易失性存储设备的性能提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: Ferromagnetic domain walls -transitional regions between magnetic domains- are an essential ingredient for racetrack memory, a device concept that promises to deliver faster and more compact memory storage compared to other non-volatile memory devices. Motivated by recent experiments that have found inertial effects in spin dynamics, we explore its consequences on domain wall motion. We find that the inertial dynamics of the individual magnetic moments induce massive dynamics of the domain wall. We investigate these massive dynamics driven by a magnetic field, spin-transfer torque, and spin-orbit torque. We show that, in the absence of Gilbert damping, the domain wall dynamics become chaotic, resembling that of an electron in a two-dimensional crystal. For finite damping, field-like driving of the inertial domain wall significantly increases its velocity compared to conventional massless dynamics, potentially enabling faster racetrack operations. Additionally, in the limit of low driving, we observe that the domain wall width contracts due to the spin inertia of the ferromagnet.

</details>


### [97] [Symmetry Breaking and Transition to Robust Excitonic Topological Order in InAs/GaSb Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10363)
*Xinghao Wang,Wenfeng Zhang,Yujiang Dong,Weiliang Qiao,Peizhe Jia,Rui-Rui Du*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过栅控砷化铟-锑化镓双层结构，揭示了库仑相互作用在对称性破缺和拓扑相变中的关键作用，展示了量子自旋霍尔绝缘体与激子拓扑序之间的相变过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性（symmetry）和拓扑（topology）是物理学中的基本概念，但库仑相互作用在拓扑相变过程中的对称性破缺作用尚未被充分理解。本研究旨在探索电子-空穴双层系统中库仑相互作用如何影响对称性与拓扑之间的复杂相互作用。

Method: 研究采用栅控砷化铟-锑化镓（indium arsenide-gallium antimonide）双层结构，通过调节栅压将系统从高密度区进入稀薄区，增强层间库仑相互作用，并施加磁场驱动相变。

Result: 高密度区由量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（quantum spin Hall insulator, QSHI）主导，稀薄区增强的层间库仑相互作用导致出现具有自发时间反演对称性破缺的激子拓扑序（exciton topological order, ETO）。施加磁场驱动从QSHI到ETO的相变，伴随库仑诱导的自旋旋转对称性破缺，在最低朗道能级中选择三重态电子-空穴配对。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了电子-空穴双层系统中库仑相互作用下对称性与拓扑之间复杂的相互作用关系，为理解库仑相互作用在对称性破缺和拓扑相变中的关键作用提供了实验证据。

Abstract: Symmetry and topology are fundamental concepts deeply intertwined in various fields of physics, especially in the studies of quantum phases of matter. The critical role that Coulomb interactions play in symmetry breaking during topological transitions is a fundamental problem that has not been fully understood. Utilizing gated indium arsenide-gallium antimonide bilayers, we demonstrate that Coulomb interactions play a critical role in symmetry breaking and topological transitions. Whereas the quantum spin Hall insulator (QSHI) dominates the high-density regime, gating the system into the dilute regime enhances interlayer Coulomb interactions and leads to an emergent excitonic topological order (ETO) with spontaneous time-reversal-symmetry breaking. Moreover, applying a magnetic field drives a transition from the QSHI to the ETO accompanied by Coulomb-induced spin-rotation-symmetry breaking, which selects triplet electron-hole pairing in the lowest Landau levels. These results underscore an intricate interplay between symmetry and topology under Coulomb interactions in electron-hole bilayers.

</details>


### [98] [Do single-shot projective readouts necessarily estimate the $T_1$ lifetime ?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10447)
*Aparajita Modak,Sundeep Kapila,Bent Weber,Klaus Ensslin,Guido Burkard,Bhaskaran Muralidharan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了多能级系统中单次量子比特读取协议的理论T₁寿命计算与实验观测不符的根本原因，指出外在（extrinsic）布居动力学是导致这种差异的关键因素，并提出了改进的读取协议来准确估计谷量子比特的T₁寿命。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当单次量子比特读取协议（single-shot qubit readout protocols）应用于多能级系统时，理论T₁寿命计算往往无法准确反映实验观测的寿命趋势。这种理论与实验之间的差异需要被解释和解决，特别是在双层石墨烯自旋-谷态（spin-valley states in bilayer graphene）的近期测量中。

Method: 研究建立了一个综合理论（integrated theory）来分析外在布居动力学（extrinsic population dynamics）的影响。该方法不仅考虑了声子（phonon）和约翰逊噪声（Johnson noise）等内在因素，还系统性地纳入了外在因素，以解释实验观测到的寿命趋势。

Result: 研究确认声子和约翰逊噪声是主要的内在弛豫源，但发现外在因素的纳入对于匹配实验估计至关重要。外在因素还会导致广义马西森规则（generalized Mathiessen's rules）的违反。在某些工作区域，寿命估计可能与内在T₁时间截然不同。

Conclusion: 基于对设计空间（design space）的改进理解，研究提出了一个修订的读取协议来准确估计谷量子比特（valley qubit）的T₁寿命。该工作澄清了外在布居动力学在多能级系统寿命估计中的关键作用，为量子比特表征提供了更精确的理论框架。

Abstract: When single-shot qubit readout protocols are adapted for multilevel systems, theoretical $T_1$ lifetime calculations often fall short of capturing the experimental lifetime trends. We identify {\it extrinsic} population dynamics as the fundamental origin of this disparity, establishing that the lifetime estimates can, in certain operating regions, be distinct from the intrinsic $T_1$ time. We clarify these aspects with an integrated theory to address recent measurements [Nat. Nano, 20, 494, (2025)] on spin-valley states in bilayer graphene. While confirming that phonon and Johnson noise are the dominant intrinsic sources, we show that the inclusion of extrinsic factors provide the critical match to the experimental estimates. The extrinsic factors also effectuate violations of generalized Mathiessen's rules also. With an improved handle on the design space, a revised readout protocol to estimate the $T_1$ lifetime of the valley qubit is proposed.

</details>


### [99] [Topological heavy-tailed networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10467)
*Sunkyu Yu,Xianji Piao,Namkyoo Park*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过构建拓扑重尾网络（topological heavy-tailed networks），在阿波罗网络（Apollonian network）上实现了拓扑相，并计算了磁通依赖的能谱——阿波罗蝴蝶（Apollonian butterfly），揭示了复杂网络中的拓扑现象与控制性之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管二维周期结构一直是探索拓扑现象的主要平台，但近期研究已扩展到更复杂的非周期结构：准晶（quasicrystals）、分形（fractals）、非欧几里得晶格（non-Euclidean lattices）和无序材料。基于网络的视角不仅为分类这些多样化平台提供了统一框架，还揭示了复杂网络中未探索的拓扑现象区域。

Method: 研究实现了拓扑重尾网络作为展示拓扑相的高阶复杂网络示例。通过为阿波罗网络开发紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），并使用确定性算法为这种非周期几何分配非平凡规范场（nontrivial gauge fields），计算了磁通依赖的能谱。利用谱定位器（spectral localizers）来表征阿波罗蝴蝶的拓扑特征。

Result: 计算得到的阿波罗蝴蝶能谱显示出其拓扑特征的敏感性由低阶节点（lower-degree nodes）控制，类似于复杂网络的可控性。这一发现揭示了网络拓扑结构与物理拓扑现象之间的深刻联系。

Conclusion: 该框架桥接了拓扑物理和网络科学，引入了基于连接性驱动的拓扑波控制范式（connectivity-driven paradigm），为在复杂网络系统中探索和控制拓扑现象提供了新途径。

Abstract: Although two-dimensional periodic structures have functioned as the primary platform for exploring topological phenomena, recent advances have substantially expanded this research boundary to include more intricate, aperiodic structures: quasicrystals, fractals, non-Euclidean lattices, and disordered materials. A network-based perspective not only offers a unified framework for classifying these diverse platforms based on their network connectivity but also unveils unexplored regimes of topological phenomena in complex networks. Here, we implement topological heavy-tailed networks, as an example of high-degree complex networks exhibiting topological phases. By developing a tight-binding model for the Apollonian network and a deterministic algorithm to assign nontrivial gauge fields to this aperiodic geometry, we compute the magnetic-flux-dependent energy spectrum: the Apollonian butterfly. Using spectral localizers, we characterize the topological features of the Apollonian butterfly, whose sensitivity is governed by lower-degree nodes, analogous to the controllability of complex networks. Our framework bridges topological physics and network science, introducing a connectivity-driven paradigm for the control of topological waves.

</details>


### [100] [Parabolic-Cylinder Approach to Valley-Polarized Conductance in Tilted Anisotropic Dirac-Weyl Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10490)
*Can Yesilyurt*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种抛物线柱面（parabolic-cylinder）方法，用于分析倾斜各向异性狄拉克-外尔（Dirac-Weyl）系统中的谷极化电导，通过将平滑界面散射问题解析约化为韦伯方程（Weber equation），获得了角传输包络的闭式表达式，并阐明了倾斜分量的不同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究倾斜各向异性狄拉克-外尔系统中的谷极化电导，旨在理解界面隧穿如何产生净谷极化电导，并为候选材料如8-Pmmn硼烯（borophene）和WTe2提供实际工作窗口。

Method: 采用抛物线柱面（parabolic-cylinder）方法，将平滑界面散射问题解析约化为韦伯方程（Weber equation），该方程与量子谐振子属于同一微分方程类。结合固定器件坐标系与旋转势垒坐标系之间的非线性映射，建立了从谷依赖界面隧穿到净谷极化电导的直接路径。

Result: 获得了角传输包络的闭式表达式，阐明了倾斜分量的不同作用：垂直倾斜分量重整化隧穿包络宽度，而平行倾斜分量在相反谷中以不同方式移动法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Perot）共振结构。在研究的参数范围内，发现t=0.2附近存在稳健最优值，识别了从振荡到单调极化机制的交叉，并划定了候选材料的实际工作窗口。

Conclusion: 该解析方法为理解倾斜各向异性狄拉克-外尔系统中的谷极化电导提供了直接途径，揭示了倾斜分量的不同作用机制，并为8-Pmmn硼烯和WTe2等候选材料的实际应用划定了操作窗口。

Abstract: We develop a parabolic-cylinder approach to valley-polarized conductance in tilted anisotropic Dirac-Weyl systems, showing that the smooth-interface scattering problem can be reduced analytically to the Weber equation, which belongs to the same differential-equation class as the quantum harmonic oscillator. This reduction yields closed-form expressions for the angular transmission envelope and clarifies the distinct roles of the tilt components: the perpendicular tilt renormalizes the tunneling-envelope width, while the parallel tilt shifts the Fabry-Perot resonance structure differently in opposite valleys. Combined with the nonlinear mapping between the fixed device frame and the rotated barrier frame, this analytical structure provides a direct route from valley-dependent interface tunneling to net valley-polarized conductance. We apply the formalism to rotated electrostatic barriers and construct phase diagrams over barrier angle, tilt strength, width, height, and Fermi energy. The results reveal a robust optimum near t = 0.2 over the parameter range studied, identify the crossover from oscillatory to monotonic polarization regimes, and delineate practical operating windows for candidate materials including 8-Pmmn borophene and WTe2.

</details>


### [101] [Gauge transformation for pulse propagation and time ordered integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10659)
*Adel Abbout*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于逐步消除时间依赖在位势的规范变换，该变换将向内跃迁重整化为相位因子$e^{i φ(t)}$，向外跃迁重整化为$e^{-i φ(t)}$，简化了散射系统中脉冲传播的模拟和时间演化算符的时间序积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种规范变换方法，用于处理有限或无限系统中时间依赖在位势的逐步消除问题，旨在简化散射系统中脉冲传播的模拟和时间演化算符的计算复杂度。

Method: 该方法基于规范变换，通过逐步消除单个格点上的时间依赖在位势，实现对跃迁参数的重整化。具体而言，向内跃迁被重整化为相位因子$e^{i φ(t)}$，而向外跃迁被重整化为$e^{-i φ(t)}$。

Result: 分析结果表明，该规范变换能够有效简化散射系统中脉冲传播的模拟过程，同时显著简化时间依赖薛定谔方程中时间演化算符所涉及的时间序积分计算。

Conclusion: 该规范变换方法为处理时间依赖量子系统提供了一种有效的技术手段，特别是在散射系统的脉冲传播模拟和时间演化算符计算方面展现出显著的简化优势。

Abstract: We investigate a gauge transformation based on the successive elimination of time-dependent onsite potentials at individual sites in finite or infinite systems. Our analysis shows that this transformation renormalizes the inward hoppings by a phase factor $e^{i φ(t)}$ and the outward hoppings by $e^{-i φ(t)}$. We further demonstrate how this procedure facilitates the reduction and simulation of pulse propagation in scattering systems, while significantly simplifying the time-ordered integrals involved in the time evolution operator for time-dependent Schrodinger equation.

</details>


### [102] [Fast readout for large scale spin-based qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10696)
*X. Luo,B. Bertrand,H. Niebojewski,F. Martins,C. Smith,T. -Y. Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在采用工业兼容工艺制造的硅双量子点（DQD）中实现快速读取泡利自旋阻塞现象及调控点间耦合的能力，为大规模工业标准硅自旋量子比特阵列的可扩展快速读取奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于探索基于工业兼容工艺制造的硅双量子点（silicon double quantum dot, DQD）中快速读取泡利自旋阻塞（Pauli spin blockade）现象的方法，并实现对点间耦合（interdot coupling）的可调控性，以推动大规模硅自旋量子比特（spin qubit）阵列的可扩展制造。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）采用工业兼容工艺制造硅双量子点；2）使用第二层自对准栅极（second self-aligned gate layer）调控点间耦合；3）通过基于栅极的反射测量技术（gate-based reflectometry techniques）进行电荷传感（charge sensing）和自旋读取（spin readout）。

Result: 研究结果表明，成功实现了对硅双量子点中泡利自旋阻塞现象的快速读取，并展示了通过第二层自对准栅极有效调控点间耦合的能力，验证了基于栅极的反射测量技术在电荷传感和自旋读取中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究为大规模工业标准制造的硅自旋量子比特阵列的可扩展快速读取（scalable fast readout）铺平了道路，展示了工业兼容工艺在量子计算器件制造中的潜力。

Abstract: In this letter, we present fast readout of Pauli spin blockade phenomena and interdot coupling tunability in a silicon double quantum dot (DQD) fabricated using industry-compatible processes. The interdot couplings are tuned with a second self-aligned gate layer. The charge sensing and spin readout are performed by using gate-based reflectometry techniques. The results pave the way for scalable fast readout of large-scale industry-standard manufactured Si spin qubit arrays.

### [103] [Tuning correlated states of twisted mono-bilayer graphene with proximity-induced spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10914)
*Jeyong Park,Mingdi Luo,Louk Rademaker,Jurgen Smet,Mathias S. Scheurer,Laura Classen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过自洽哈特里-福克计算，分析了扭曲单双层石墨烯在有无自旋轨道耦合（SOC）下的关联基态，发现整数填充时保持莫尔平移对称性，半整数填充时则破坏对称性，且SOC类型显著影响自旋序构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解扭曲单双层石墨烯在有无过渡金属二硫化物诱导的自旋轨道耦合（SOC）下的关联基态特性，特别是在实验已报道的整数和半整数填充处观察到的关联拓扑态特征。

Method: 采用自洽哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）计算方法，允许变分空间包含多Q平移对称性破缺态，对所有整数和半整数填充的导带进行分析。

Result: 发现相互作用诱导的绝缘体在整数填充时保持莫尔（moiré）平移对称性，但在半整数填充时破坏该对称性。SOC类型显著影响自旋性质：伊辛（Ising）SOC有利于面外自旋极化和自旋-谷锁定，而拉什巴（Rashba）SOC有利于面内自旋序。

Conclusion: 平移对称性破缺源于半填充极化能带，SOC存在时亦然。SOC类型驱动自旋序转变：单一SOC类型时，从四面体反铁磁体转变为共面、非共面或共线自旋密度波态；两种SOC同时存在时，其竞争可在原本共线基态的参数范围内诱导手性非共面序。

Abstract: We study the correlated ground states of twisted mono-bilayer graphene with and without proximity-induced spin-orbit coupling (SOC) from a transition-metal dichalcogenide layer placed on top. We perform self-consistent Hartree-Fock calculations that allow the variational space to include multi-$Q$ translational symmetry broken states for all integer and half-integer fillings of the conduction bands, where signatures of correlated, topological states have been reported experimentally. We find interaction-induced insulators that retain moiré translational symmetry at integer fillings, but that break this symmetry at half-integer fillings. We argue that translational symmetry breaking arises from half-filled polarized bands, even when SOC is present. Yet, we find that small SOC can already crucially affect the spin nature of correlated states. Generally, Ising SOC favors out-of-plane spin polarization and spin-valley locking, while Rashba SOC favors in-plane spin order. If only one of these two terms is present, we find that, depending on the type of SOC, it drives a transition from a tetrahedal antiferromagnet to either a coplanar, non-coplanar, or collinear spin-density wave state for half-integer fillings. The frustration associated with the simultaneous presence of both types of SOC can induce chiral, non-coplanar order in parameter ranges where the ground state in the absence of SOC is collinear.

</details>


### [104] [Microscopic screening theory for excitons in two-dimensional materials: A bridge between effective models and ab initio descriptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10966)
*P. Ninhos,A. J. Uría-Álvarez,C. Tserkezis,N. A. Mortensen,J. J. Palacios*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）框架的二维材料激子计算方法，采用原子描述和点状轨道，通过量子屏蔽相互作用实现高效且准确的激子结合能计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前广泛使用的激子计算方法依赖于经典或有效相互作用模型（如Rytova-Keldysh模型），这些模型无法准确捕捉量子屏蔽效应。本文旨在开发一种既能保持计算效率又能准确描述二维材料中激子物理的计算方法。

Method: 该方法在Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）框架内采用原子描述和点状轨道（point-like orbitals），通过随机相位近似（random-phase approximation）水平上显式计算二维介电函数，从而纳入量子屏蔽相互作用（quantum screened interactions）。

Result: 该方法能够以可承受的计算成本准确估计激子结合能（exciton binding energies），其精度可与第一性原理方法相媲美。通过对各种收敛参数的详细分析，揭示了文献中使用第一性原理GW/BSE实现时报告的结合能大分散的可能原因。

Conclusion: 该工作为低维材料中的高效且可靠的介电屏蔽和激子计算提供了替代途径，超越了传统有效模型的局限性，同时保持了计算可行性。

Abstract: We present a computational approach for exciton calculations in two-dimensional (2D) materials within the Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE) framework, employing an atomistic description with point-like orbitals. Unlike widespread efficient calculations that rely on classical or effective interaction models, such as the Rytova-Keldysh model, our method incorporates quantum screened interactions. By explicitly computing the 2D dielectric function at the random-phase approximation level, we capture screening effects beyond such approximations with an accuracy akin to first-principles methods. Consequently, we can realistically estimate excitonic binding energies with a bearable computational cost. A detailed account of the various convergence parameters sheds light on a possible cause of the large dispersion of binding energies reported in the literature using first-principles GW/BSE implementations. This work thus provides an alternative pathway towards efficient and faithful dielectric screening and exciton computations in low-dimensional materials.

</details>

### [105] [A conformal lower bound of weighted Dirac eigenvalues on manifolds with boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10875)
*Mingwei Zhang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了紧致自旋流形上带权Dirac特征值问题，给出了特征值的下界估计，并证明了等号成立时流形必须是半球且特征函数为Killing旋量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究紧致自旋流形上带权Dirac特征值问题的下界估计，探索等号成立的条件及其几何意义。

Method: 使用相对Yamabe常数（relative Yamabe constant）作为工具，对带权Dirac特征值问题进行分析，并考虑手性边界条件（chiral boundary condition）。

Result: 首先证明了特征值的下界：λ² ≥ n/[4(n-1)] Y(M,∂M,[g])，然后证明了等号成立当且仅当（在共形变换下）M是半球且φ是Killing旋量（Killing spinor）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了带权Dirac特征值与相对Yamabe常数之间的精确关系，揭示了等号成立时的几何刚性条件，并进行了更广泛的推广研究。

Abstract: For the weighted Dirac eigenproblem on a compact spin manifold with the chiral boundary condition \begin{equation*}
  \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} D\varphi = λf\varphi & \text{in } M, \\ \mathbf{B}\varphi = 0 & \text{on } \partial M, \end{array} \right. \end{equation*} we first give a lower bound of the eigenvalue using the relative Yamabe constant
  \begin{equation*}
  λ^2 \geq \frac{n}{4(n-1)} Y(M,\partial M,[g]), \end{equation*} then prove that equality holds if and only if (up to a conformal transformation) $M$ is a hemisphere and $\varphi$ is a Killing spinor. More generalizations are studied.

</details>

### [106] [Spectral methods for wedge and corner flows: The Fourier-Kontorovich-Lebedev integral transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10942)
*Abdallah Daddi-Moussa-Ider*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文综述了低雷诺数流体力学中楔形几何问题的分析方法，重点关注点力（Stokeslet）和点扭矩（rotlet）的Stokes方程求解，为预测受限系统流体流动提供理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解楔形几何中的流体流动对于预测受限系统（如微流控设备和近角输运现象）中的流体动力学相互作用至关重要。本文旨在为楔形问题提供系统的分析方法。

Method: 基于Papkovich-Neuber表示法，使用四个调和函数表征流体流动。重点介绍了Fourier-Kontorovich-Lebedev（FKL）变换方法，概述了其关键性质和求解步骤。

Result: 建立了求解点力（Stokeslet）和点扭矩（rotlet）在楔形几何中Stokes方程的通用框架。该框架能够预测楔形约束中的粒子动力学。

Conclusion: 所提出的分析方法为预测楔形约束中的粒子动力学和设计具有角几何的微流控系统提供了通用框架，在受限系统流体动力学研究中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Understanding fluid flow in wedge-shaped geometries is essential for predicting hydrodynamic interactions in confined systems, such as microfluidic devices and near-corner transport phenomena. This article reviews analytical methods and techniques for addressing wedge problems in low-Reynolds-number hydrodynamics, focusing on solutions of the Stokes equations for a point force (Stokeslet) and a point torque (rotlet). The formulation is based on the Papkovich-Neuber representation, which uses four harmonic functions to characterize the fluid flow. A concise overview of the Fourier-Kontorovich-Lebedev (FKL) transform method is provided, highlighting key properties and steps employed in deriving these solutions. This offers a versatile framework for predicting particle dynamics in wedge confinements and for designing microfluidic systems with corner geometries.

Method: 通过建立量子细胞自动机与粗同调理论的对应关系，证明QCA自然地构成粗同调理论的零度部分，并利用粗同调理论的形式性质推导相关结果。

Result: 证明了量子细胞自动机形成粗同调理论的零度部分，且Ji和Yang关于QCA空间形成Ω-谱（Omega-spectrum）的结果是粗同调理论形式性质的直接推论。

Abstract: We show that quantum cellular automata naturally form the degree-zero part of a coarse homology theory. The recent result of Ji and Yang that the space of QCA forms an Omega-spectrum in the sense of algebraic topology is a direct consequence of the formal properties of coarse homology theories.

### [108] [Symmetric localization of $ν_{\text{tot}}=4/3$ fractional topological insulator edges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10103)
*Yang-Zhi Chou,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于扭曲MoTe₂实验，研究了ν_tot=4/3分数量子拓扑绝缘体的无序相互作用边缘理论，揭示了边缘输运不足以识别此类拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于最近的扭曲MoTe₂实验[arXiv:2601.18508]，旨在理解由两个时间反演共轭ν=2/3分数量子霍尔态组成的ν_tot=4/3分数量子拓扑绝缘体的边缘行为。

Method: 开发了无序相互作用边缘理论（disordered interacting edge theory），在Sz守恒边缘条件下分析不同相，并考虑Sz改变微扰（如Rashba自旋轨道耦合）的影响。进一步提供了与非相互作用费米子理论（noninteracting fermionic theory）的精确映射。

Result: 在Sz守恒边缘中发现了三个不同相，每个边缘在长边缘极限下具有两种可能的电导值：2/3 e²/h和4/3 e²/h。在Sz改变微扰下，相互作用可诱导出绝缘边缘态而不破坏时间反演或电荷守恒对称性，对应拓扑保护边缘态的缺失。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，ν_tot=4/3分数量子拓扑绝缘体的两端输运测量不足以识别其拓扑相，为实验相关系统提供了明确示例。

Abstract: Motivated by the recent twisted MoTe$_2$ experiment [arXiv:2601.18508], we develop a disordered interacting edge theory of a fractional topological insulator at $ν_{\text{tot}}=4/3$, consisting of two time-reversal-conjugated $ν=2/3$ fractional quantum Hall states. For an $S_z$-conserving edge, we uncover three distinct phases with two possible conductance values per edge in the long-edge limit: $\frac{2}{3}\frac{e^2}{h}$ and $\frac{4}{3}\frac{e^2}{h}$. In the presence of $S_z$-changing perturbations (e.g., Rashba spin-orbit coupling), an interaction-induced insulating edge state can emerge without breaking time-reversal or charge-conservation symmetry, corresponding to the absence of a topologically protected edge state. We further provide an exact mapping to a noninteracting fermionic theory exhibiting Anderson localization. Our results showcase an explicit, experimentally relevant example that the edge-state two-terminal transport is insufficient to identify the $ν_{\text{tot}}=4/3$ fractional topological insulators.

</details>


### [109] [Classical Kitaev model in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10112)
*Paul A. McClarty,Roderich Moessner,Karlo Penc,Jeffrey G. Rau*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了磁场中经典Kitaev蜂窝模型的物理性质，揭示了自旋液体（spin liquid）在有限磁场窗口内的存在，并探讨了其热容、磁化率等低温行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对具有Kitaev交换的自旋轨道耦合磁体在磁场中实验现象的探索，旨在理解经典Kitaev蜂窝模型在磁场存在下的物理行为。

Method: 采用对经典Kitaev蜂窝模型在磁场存在下的理论分析，通过揭示基态自旋需满足的约束条件，构建粗粒化理论（coarse-grained theory）来描述有效电荷自由度的涨落。

Result: 研究发现存在从零场到有限阈值内的自旋液体（spin liquid）区域，之后才转变为极化顺磁体（polarized paramagnet）。在有限磁场下，两点自旋关联和四极关联（quadrupolar correlations）均为短程，与零场情况形成对比。

Conclusion: 研究确定了自旋液体区域内热容和磁化率随磁场变化的精确零温极限行为，并发现弱位点稀释（site-dilution）不会改变自旋液体内的磁化强度，表现出一种"完美"的补偿效应。

Abstract: Motivated by experiments on spin-orbit coupled magnets with Kitaev exchange in magnetic fields, we present an analysis of the classical Kitaev honeycomb model in the presence of a magnetic field. We show that there is a spin liquid regime that exists within a finite window of fields from zero up to a finite threshold before transitioning into the polarized paramagnet. We uncover constraints that spins need to satisfy in the ground state and show that they determine the exact limiting zero temperature behavior of the heat capacity and magnetic susceptibility within the spin liquid as a function of field. When the field is finite, both the two-point spin and the quadrupolar correlations are short-ranged, in contrast to the zero-field case. We rationalize an effective mass for the quadrupolar correlations in terms of a coarse-grained theory with fluctuating effective charge degrees of freedom. Finally, we show that weak site-dilution does not change the magnetization within the spin liquid -- a kind of "perfect" compensation of the site dilution.

</details>


### [110] [Disorder-induced localisation in the Mott-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10238)
*Ričards Kristers Knipšis,Friedemann Queisser,Jesumony Jayabalan,Gael Reecht,Manuel Gruber,Uwe Bovensiepen,Ralf Schützhold*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究采用关联层次方法分析Mott绝缘体相中Fermi-Hubbard模型的doublon和holon准粒子激发在无序系统中的行为，比较了电荷无序和自旋无序对局域化特性的不同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索Mott绝缘体相中Fermi-Hubbard模型的准粒子激发在无序环境下的行为，特别是理解电荷无序和自旋无序对doublon和holon准粒子局域化特性的不同影响机制。

Method: 采用关联层次方法（hierarchy of correlations）研究无序系统中的准粒子激发，分析两种无序类型：电荷无序（charge disorder，表现为在位势随机性）和自旋无序（spin disorder，表现为固定的随机背景自旋排列）。通过分析准粒子本征谱并量化相应本征态的局域化程度来研究系统特性。

Result: 研究发现电荷无序导致局域态和扩展态在能量和空间上的分离，而自旋无序则使准粒子能带中的态全部局域化。研究还通过强耦合微扰理论（strong-coupling perturbation theory）重复计算，并将两种方法的结果进行了比较。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了电荷无序和自旋无序对Fermi-Hubbard模型Mott绝缘体相中准粒子激发的不同局域化效应，电荷无序产生局域态与扩展态的分离，而自旋无序导致全面的局域化，为理解无序强关联系统的输运性质提供了重要见解。

Abstract: For the Fermi-Hubbard model in the Mott insulator phase, we employ the hierarchy of correlations to study how doublon and holon quasi-particle excitations are affected by adding disorder to the system. We study two types of disorder: charge disorder, in the form of on-site potential randomness; and spin disorder, in the form of a fixed, randomly generated background spin arrangement. By analysing the quasi-particle eigen-spectra and quantifying the degree to which the corresponding eigen-states localise, we find both an energetic and spatial separation between localised and delocalised states in the charge disorder. In contrast, the spin disorder results in localised states throughout the quasi-particle bands. Finally, we repeat our calculations using strong-coupling perturbation theory, and compare the results obtained from both methods.

</details>


### [111] [Long-range magnetic order with disordered spin orientations in a high-entropy antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10412)
*Yao Shen,Guangkai Zhang,Qinghua Zhang,Xuejuan Gui,Yu Zhang,Heemin Lee,Cheng-Tai Kuo,Jun-Sik Lee,Ronny Sutarto,Feng Ye,Zhao Pan,Xiaomei Qin,Jinchen Wang,Tianping Ying,Youwen Long*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过中子衍射和共振软X射线散射技术，揭示了高熵范德华材料(Mn1/4Fe1/4Co1/4Ni1/4)PS3中一种新型长程磁有序：尽管存在显著原子无序，所有四种过渡金属元素共同参与统一的锯齿形反铁磁相变，但各元素的自旋取向因单离子各向异性和交换相互作用的竞争而呈现差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性系统中的无序通常抑制长程有序，促进自旋玻璃和磁团簇等短程态。在高熵材料中，尽管存在局部磁实体和交换相互作用的随机分布，但长程磁有序在少数例外情况下仍能持续存在，其微观特征和潜在机制尚不明确，特别是各元素的磁行为。

Method: 结合中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和共振软X射线散射（resonant soft x-ray scattering）技术，对高熵蜂窝晶格范德华材料(Mn1/4Fe1/4Co1/4Ni1/4)PS3进行了元素特异性磁有序研究。

Result: 尽管存在显著原子无序，在72 K以下观察到长程锯齿形反铁磁有序（zigzag antiferromagnetic order），所有四种过渡金属元素均参与统一的相变。然而，不同元素的自旋取向存在差异，这归因于单离子各向异性（single-ion anisotropies）和交换相互作用之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 研究发现了一种具有无序自旋取向的新型长程磁有序，该有序由高熵磁体中不同的磁性元素协同稳定，为理解复杂磁性系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Disorder in magnetic systems typically suppresses long-range order, promoting short-range states such as spin glasses and magnetic clusters. This is particularly prominent in high-entropy materials, characterized by the random distributions of local magnetic entities and exchange interactions. However, in rare exceptions, long-range magnetic order can persist in high-entropy systems, while the microscopic characters and underlying mechanisms remain elusive, especially the magnetic behaviors of individual elements. Here, combining neutron diffraction and resonant soft x-ray scattering, we have conducted an element-specific investigation into the magnetic order of a high-entropy honeycomb-lattice van der Waals material (Mn1/4Fe1/4Co1/4Ni1/4)PS3. Despite significant atomic disorder, long-range zigzag antiferromagnetic order is observed below 72 K, with all four transition-metal elements participating in a unified phase transition. However, the spin orientations of various elements are distinct, attributed to the competition between single-ion anisotropies and exchange interactions. Our findings showcase a novel form of long-range magnetic order with disordered spin orientations, which is synergically stabilized by distinct magnetic elements in a high entropy magnet, offering a new paradigm for understanding complex magnetic systems.

</details>


### [112] [Ab initio quantum embedding description of magic angle twisted bilayer graphene at even-integer fillings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10433)
*Raehyun Kim,Woochang Kim,Kevin D. Stubbs,Steven G. Louie,Lin Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究开发了从第一性原理出发的量子嵌入工作流，用于推导魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）中的相互作用平带哈密顿量，揭示了电荷中性点和电子掺杂时的绝缘KIVC态，以及在空穴掺杂侧发现的脆弱半金属态，展示了显著的粒子-空穴不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）具有meV量级的窄莫尔能带，其关联相态对材料参数和低能下折叠的建模选择高度敏感。需要建立从第一性原理出发的可靠方法，以连接微观电子结构、屏蔽相互作用和实验观测特征。

Method: 开发了基于第一性原理的量子嵌入工作流，从弛豫无应变结构的Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（KS-DFT）出发，结合约束随机相位近似（cRPA）屏蔽、受控的双计数扣除，以及基于密度矩阵选定列（SCDM）的自动规范固定程序。使用Hartree-Fock（HF）和耦合簇单双激发（CCSD）方法求解所得模型。

Result: 在电荷中性点（ν=0）和电子掺杂（ν=+2）时恢复了稳健的绝缘Kramers谷间相干（KIVC）态。在空穴掺杂侧（ν=-2）观察到具有弱√3×√3 Kekulé调制的脆弱半金属态，并在傅里叶变换局域态密度中显示出增强的谷间散射峰。尽管基础KS-DFT能带结构近乎粒子-空穴对称，但有效相互作用哈密顿量在ν=±2时表现出显著的粒子-空穴不对称性。

Conclusion: 该工作为连接MATBG中的微观电子结构、屏蔽相互作用、扣除选择与扫描隧道显微特征提供了第一性原理路径，揭示了由与KS-DFT填充一致的参考密度构建的扣除项产生的动量依赖单粒子重整化效应。

Abstract: Magic angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) hosts narrow moiré bands with meV-scale energy splittings, making its correlated phases sensitive to both material parameters and modeling choices in low-energy downfolding. We develop an ab initio quantum-embedding workflow that derives interacting flat-band Hamiltonians from Kohn-Sham density functional theory (KS-DFT) of a relaxed, unstrained structure. Our model combines constrained random phase approximation (cRPA) screening, controlled double-counting subtraction, and an automated gauge-fixing procedure based on the selected columns of the density matrix (SCDM) that is compatible with symmetry-resolved many-body calculations. Solving the resulting models using Hartree-Fock (HF) and coupled cluster singles and doubles (CCSD), we recover robust insulating Kramers intervalley coherent (KIVC) states at charge neutrality ($ν=0$) and at electron doping ($ν=+2$). The main new physical effect appears on the hole-doped side: at $ν=-2$ we observe a fragile semimetal with a weak $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ Kekulé modulation and enhanced intervalley-scattering peaks in the Fourier-transformed local density of states. Although the underlying KS-DFT band structure is nearly particle-hole symmetric, the effective interacting Hamiltonian exhibits a pronounced particle-hole asymmetry at $ν=\pm 2$ that we trace to momentum-dependent single-particle renormalizations generated by subtraction terms constructed from reference densities consistent with the KS-DFT filling. Our work provides a first-principles route for connecting microscopic electronic structure, screened interactions, subtraction choices, and scanning tunneling microscopy signatures in MATBG.

</details>


### [113] [Observation of Kondo hybridization wave in UTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10552)
*Xin Yu,Shuikang Yu,Zheyu Wu,Alexander G. Eaton,Andrej Cabala,Michal Vališka,Jun Li,Rui Zhou,Yi-feng Yang,Zhenyu Wang,Peijie Sun,Rui Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 首次在自旋三重态重费米子超导体UTe2表面观测到Kondo杂化波（KHW）的平移对称性破缺有序相，表现为周期性调制的Fano晶格，伴随电荷密度波（CDW）和费米能级附近的能隙打开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kondo晶格作为强关联电子系统的原型，通常表现为杂化过程的宽交叉而非相变，此前从未观测到有序的杂化相。研究旨在探索Kondo物理中是否存在有序杂化状态。

Method: 使用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）技术，在自旋三重态重费米子超导体UTe2表面进行观测，识别Kondo杂化波（KHW）的平移对称性破缺有序相。

Result: 首次观测到KHW有序相，表现为周期性调制的Fano晶格，伴随共存的电荷密度波（CDW）和费米能级附近的显著能隙。KHW形成的CDW具有重f电荷与传导电荷互补占据的实空间纹理，构成Kondo超晶格。

Conclusion: KHW有序相与UTe2的超导性共存，为理解其争议的自旋三重态配对对称性和潜在机制提供新视角。这一首次实验证据为Kondo晶格系统的强关联物理开辟了新研究方向。

Abstract: Condensed matter systems with strong electronic correlations often manifest a variety of intertwined ordered phases of charge, spin, orbital and other degrees of freedom. As a prototypical strongly correlated electronic system, the Kondo lattice provides fertile soil for many fascinating quantum states, including quantum criticality, unconventional superconductivity, hidden order and topological Kondo insulator/semimetal. The foundation of Kondo physics lies in the hybridization between localized moments and itinerant electrons. Generally, the evolution of Kondo hybridization is characterized as a broad crossover rather than a phase transition. Thus far, an ordered hybridization phase has not been observed. Here, we use scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) to identify a translational-symmetry-breaking order of Kondo hybridization wave(KHW) for the first time on the surface of the spin-triplet heavy-fermion superconductor UTe2. The unprecedented phase of KHW manifests as a periodically modulated Fano lattice, accompanied by a commensurate charge density wave (CDW) and a pronounced energy gap opening near the Fermi level. This KHW-imprinted CDW has an intriguing real-space texture of complementary occupation of the heavy f and conduction charges, thereby forming a Kondo superlattice. The KHW is coexistent with superconductivity in UTe2, which may provide valuable insight into its controversial spin-triplet pairing symmetry and the underlying mechanism. Our first experimental evidence for an ordered hybridization state potentially sheds new light on the strong correlation physics of Kondo lattice system.

</details>


### [114] [Formulation of intrinsic nonlinear thermal conductivity for bosonic systems using quantum kinetic equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10605)
*Aoi Kuwabara,Joji Nasu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文建立了玻色子系统中非线性热传导的理论框架，揭示了量子几何量（量子度规和热贝里联络极化率）对非线性热输运的关键作用，并通过量子自旋模型展示了热贝里联络极化率项在非线性热霍尔效应中的主导地位。

Method: 采用量子动力学方程方法（quantum kinetic equation approach）构建玻色子系统的本征非线性热导率理论框架，避免了Luttinger引力势方法的困难，并自然包含了能量磁化的贡献。将非线性热导率分解为三个独立贡献：两个基于量子几何量（量子度规和热贝里联络极化率），一个仅由能带色散决定。

Conclusion: 研究结果为玻色子系统的本征非线性热响应建立了普适理论框架，揭示了超越线性响应理论的热输运量子几何机制，特别是热贝里联络极化率在非线性热霍尔效应中的关键作用。

Abstract: Nonlinear responses in transport phenomena have attracted significant attention because they can arise even when linear responses are forbidden by symmetry, with the quantum geometry of Bloch wave functions playing an essential role. While such effects have been extensively studied in electric transport, similar quantum-geometric mechanisms are also expected to govern nonlinear thermal transport. In particular, thermal responses are crucial in bosonic systems such as magnons and phonons, which are charge-neutral quasiparticles. However, a consistent theoretical description of nonlinear thermal transport remains challenging because of the difficulty in the treatment of energy magnetization in higher-order responses with Luttinger's gravitational potential method. Here, we formulate the intrinsic nonlinear thermal conductivity of bosonic systems using a quantum kinetic equation approach that avoids Luttinger's method and naturally incorporates contributions from energy magnetization. We identify three distinct contributions to the nonlinear thermal conductivity: two expressed in terms of quantum-geometric quantities, namely the quantum metric and the thermal Berry-connection polarizability (TBCP), and a third determined solely by the band dispersions. Applying our formalism to a specific quantum spin model within linear spin-wave theory, we show that the TBCP term dominates the nonlinear thermal Hall effect in the absence of threefold symmetry. Our results differ quantitatively from those obtained using semiclassical theory, thereby highlighting the importance of quantum corrections beyond the semiclassical picture. These findings establish a general framework for intrinsic nonlinear thermal responses in bosonic systems and reveal quantum-geometric mechanisms underlying thermal transport beyond linear response theory.

Abstract: One-body multipole operators are defined as irreducible representations of rotational symmetry together with spatial-inversion and time-reversal symmetries, providing a systematic framework for classifying electronic internal degrees of freedom and for describing a wide variety of composite order parameters. While this formalism has been successfully established for the one-body operator space, a systematic classification of the many-body operator space, especially in interacting systems, remains an open challenge. In this paper, we extend the multipole formalism in the one-body operator space to the many-body operator space. By formulating fermionic creation and annihilation operators as spherical tensors and employing Clebsch-Gordan coupling combined with the exterior (Grassmann) algebra, we construct an irreducible decomposition of many-body operators that fully incorporates fermionic antisymmetrization.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文引入范式转变，用广义约化密度矩阵（generalized reduced density matrix, GRDM）替代配分函数作为模拟对象。这种重新表述从源头上消除了测量瓶颈，并将约化描述的维度缩减优势从静态量扩展到动力学可观测量。

Result: 该框架允许定向循环算法（directed-loop algorithm）同时测量等时和虚时非对角可观测量，后者可直接获取动力学谱。此外，还能测量用于诊断混合态中强-弱对称性破缺的Rényi-1关联子（Rényi-1 correlators）。

Conclusion: 这项工作为量子蒙特卡罗内的全息表征（holographic characterization）建立了一个统一框架，显著扩展了从模拟中提取信息的能力。

Abstract: In quantum Monte Carlo (QMC), what can be measured efficiently is largely determined by what is sampled. When the sampled object is the partition function, a broad class of observables, including general off-diagonal operators, is typically unavailable as direct estimators. In this article, we introduce a paradigm shift by replacing the partition function with a generalized reduced density matrix (GRDM) as the simulated object. This reformulation removes the measurement bottleneck at its source and extends the dimensional-reduction advantage of reduced descriptions from static quantities to dynamical observables, thereby enabling much richer information extraction. As substantial demonstrations, the framework allows the directed-loop algorithm to measure both equal-time and imaginary-time off-diagonal observables, with the latter giving direct access to dynamical spectra. It also enables measurements of Rényi-1 correlators that diagnose strong-to-weak symmetry breaking in mixed states. This work establishes a unified framework for holographic characterization within QMC.

### [120] [Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya-driven instabilities in square-kagome quantum antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10998)

Abstract: Decorated square-kagome quantum antiferromagnets provide a natural setting in which strong frustration, lattice decoration, and spin-orbit-induced anisotropy compete on comparable energy scales. As a benchmark, the isotropic square-kagome Heisenberg model exhibits four competing low-energy saddle points distinguished by their Wilson-loop fluxes and by characteristic static and dynamical structure-factor fingerprints. A minimal DM perturbation does not qualitatively reshape this competing landscape, but already enhances the tendency towards order. For the realistic decorated Hamiltonian, finite-size scaling of $Δ_{\mathrm{spinon}}$ together with momentum-resolved structure factors identifies $J_{10}$ (exchange with decorating Cu) as the control parameter of the gapped regime and shows that the full symmetry-allowed DM pattern shifts the system further toward condensation. ### [121] [Two-Body Solution and Instabilities along Streda Lines in Moire Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11007)
*Guopeng Xu,Chunli Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了外磁场对莫尔（moire）扭曲双层半导体中拓扑态的影响，发现沿Streda线的不可压缩态在强磁场下变得不稳定，并发展了适用于不等磁场情况下的赝势理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔微带（moire minibands）在适当近似下可建模为一对具有相反陈数（Chern numbers）的朗道能级（Landau levels），这为在时间反演对称哈密顿量中寻找新拓扑态提供了最小模型。本研究旨在探究外磁场对此模型的影响。

Method: 采用哈特里-福克近似（Hartree-Fock approximation）研究密度-磁场（n-B）平面上沿dn/dB = ±1/Φ0 Streda线的多体基态。使用含时平均场理论分析自旋翻转激发（spin-flip excitations），并引入电荷中心基（center-of-charge basis）精确求解不等磁场下的两体问题。

Result: 远离电荷中性点时，陈绝缘体（不可压缩）态非常稳定；而靠近电荷中性点时，随着相互作用强度κ减小，系统从不可压缩相转变为可压缩相。强磁场下，沿Streda线靠近电荷中性点的不可压缩态变得不稳定。不等磁场情况下的赝势（pseudopotentials）显示出一系列能级交叉，呈现出普通朗道能级系统中不存在的非单调结构。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为研究莫尔平带（moire flat bands）中的弱场物理提供了有用起点，其中由于基组尺寸过大，磁布洛赫态基（magnetic Bloch-state basis）在计算上变得不可行。电荷中心基的引入将哈尔丹赝势（Haldane pseudopotentials）推广到不等磁场情形。

Abstract: Moire minibands in twisted homobilayer semiconductors can, under suitable approximations, be modeled as a pair of Landau levels with opposite Chern numbers. This provides a minimal model for searching novel topological states in a time-reversal-symmetric Hamiltonian. In this work, we investigate the effects of an external magnetic field in this model. We study the many-body ground state in the density-magnetic-field (n-B) plane along the dn/dB = \pm1/Phi0 Streda line with Hartree-Fock approximation. Away from charge neutrality, we find the Chern-insulating (incompressible) state is very robust while towards charge neutrality, we find a transition from incompressible phase to compressible phase as the interaction strength kappa decreases. Using time-dependent mean-field theory, we further analyze spin-flip excitations and find that the incompressible state along Streda line toward charge neutrality becomes unstable even at large kappa when magnetic field is sufficiently large. Finally, we solve the two-body problem in a given Landau level exactly where the two particles experience unequal magnetic fields using a new basis called center-of-charge basis. This basis allows any isotropic interaction to be parameterized by a single quantum number, the relative angular momentum, thereby extending the Haldane pseudopotentials to the unequal-magnetic-fields case. As the difference of the two magnetic fields varies, these pseudopotentials show a sequence of level crossings, leading to non-monotonic structure of pseudopotentials that is absent in ordinary Landau level systems. Our formulation provides a useful starting point for studying weak-field physics in moire flat bands, where magnetic Bloch-state basis becomes computationally impossible due to the large basis sizes.

</details>


<div id='nlin.SI'></div>

# nlin.SI [[Back]](#toc)

### [122] [Invariant Reduction for Partial Differential Equations. IV: Symmetries that Rescale Geometric Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10131)
*Kostya Druzhkov,Alexei Cheviakov*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了偏微分方程对称约化框架，处理对称性作用下被重新标度（rescaled）而非不变的几何结构，建立了"平移规则（shift rule）"，并应用于获得具有足够对称性和守恒律系统的精确解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对称约化框架主要处理不变几何结构，但许多重要几何结构在对称性作用下仅被重新标度而非保持不变。需要扩展该框架以处理这类被重新标度的结构，并理解约化过程中不变性的获得与丧失现象。

Method: 扩展对称约化机制至被对称性重新标度的几何结构，建立平移规则：若X为约化对称性，X_s满足[X_s,X]=aX，且李导数$\mathcal{L}_{X_s}$在Vinogradov $\mathcal{C}$-谱序列上作用为乘以b，则限制对称性$X_s|_{\mathcal{E}_X}$在对应约化上作用为乘以a+b。

Result: 平移规则导致两个现象：不变性的获得（emergence of invariance）和不变性的丧失（loss of invariance）。应用该框架描述了一类具有足够对称性和守恒律系统的精确解，这些解在对称性对下不变，由显式构造的常数函数完全确定。

Conclusion: 该框架成功处理了对称性作用下被重新标度的几何结构，为获得精确解提供了几何描述方法，无需Lax对等可积性结构。通过Lin-Reissner-Tsien方程和势Boussinesq系统两个实例验证了理论的有效性。

Abstract: For a system of partial differential equations admitting point, contact, or higher symmetries, the framework of invariant reduction systematically computes how invariant geometric structures, such as conservation laws, presymplectic structures, variational principles, and Poisson brackets, are inherited by the systems governing symmetry-invariant solutions. We extend this mechanism to geometric structures that are not invariant but are $\textit{rescaled}$ by a symmetry. Specifically, if $X$ is the symmetry used for reduction, $X_s$ is a symmetry satisfying $[X_s,X]=aX$, and the Lie derivative $\mathcal{L}_{X_s}$ acts on an $X$-invariant element of the Vinogradov $\mathcal{C}$-spectral sequence as multiplication by $b$, then the restricted symmetry $X_s|_{\mathcal{E}_X}$ acts on the corresponding reduction as multiplication by $a+b$. This shift rule gives rise to two phenomena: the $\textit{emergence of invariance}$, where reductions acquire an invariance that was not present at the level of the original structure, and the $\textit{loss of invariance}$, where reductions of invariant structures are no longer invariant. As an application, we describe a class of exact solutions to systems possessing sufficiently many symmetries and conservation laws subject to certain compatibility conditions. These solutions are invariant under pairs of symmetries and are completely determined by explicitly constructed functions that are constant on them; the description is geometric and does not require any integrability-related structures such as Lax pairs. The framework is illustrated by two examples: the Lin--Reissner--Tsien equation of potential nonstationary transonic gas flows, for which closed-form exact solutions are obtained and validated numerically, and the potential Boussinesq system, for which the inherited Poisson bracket is employed to describe solutions determined by algebraic equations.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [123] [A brief history of Timing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10762)
*N. Cartiglia*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了粒子物理实验中精密计时技术的发展历程，从1990年代闪烁体和光电倍增管的大规模应用，到未来对撞机皮秒级精度探测器，识别了四个技术代际。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统梳理粒子物理实验中精密计时技术的演进脉络，为理解当前技术状态和未来发展方向提供历史视角。通过识别不同技术代际的特征，帮助研究者把握技术发展趋势。

Method: 采用历史回顾和代际划分的方法，将精密计时技术发展分为四个阶段：离散电子学与PMT时代、硅探测器革命、向四维追踪的过渡、以及面向未来设施的进一步突破。

Result: 识别出四个明确的技术代际：1）离散电子学（NIM、CAMAC、VME）和PMT时代，确立了时间测量的三个经典用途；2）硅光电倍增管（SiPMs）、低增益雪崩二极管（LGADs）和专用集成电路（ASICs）带来的硅革命；3）当前向四维（4D）追踪的过渡；4）面向未来设施的10皮秒级精度需求。

Conclusion: 精密计时技术已从百万通道规模的30-50皮秒硅计时成熟系统，发展到面向未来对撞机（如μ子对撞机和FCC）的10皮秒级精度需求，这为未来十年的探测器研发设定了议程。

Abstract: This review traces the evolution of precision timing in particle physics experiments, from the first large-scale applications of scintillator and photomultiplier tube (PMT) systems in the 1990s to the picosecond-precision detectors of future colliders. Four technological generations are identified: (i) the era of discrete electronics (NIM, CAMAC, VME) and PMTs, which established the three canonical uses of timing -- particle identification via time-of-flight, background and pile-up rejection, and directionality triggering; (ii) the silicon revolution enabled by Silicon Photomultipliers (SiPMs), Low-Gain Avalanche Diodes (LGADs), and Application-Specific Integrated Circuits (ASICs); (iii) the current transition to ubiquitous four-dimensional (4D) tracking, in which time is a coordinate measured at every point along a particle trajectory. Under-construction systems at the HL-LHC (CMS MTD, ATLAS HGTD, CMS HGCAL) demonstrate the maturity of 30--50\,ps silicon timing at the million-channel scale. The EIC, LHCb VELO Upgrade~II, and ALICE~3 push this technology into new regimes of radiation hardness, material budget, and granularity. (iv) The Far-future facilities such as the Muon Collider and FCC require a further leap to $\sim$10\,ps, setting the agenda for the next decade of detector R\&D.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在搜索底夸克偶素χ_{bJ}(1P)衰变中的带电轻子味破坏（charged-lepton-flavor violation）过程，这是标准模型（Standard Model）中严格禁戒的过程，其观测将暗示新物理（new physics）的存在。

Method: 利用Belle探测器在KEKB对撞机（KEKB collider）的e⁺e⁻对撞中收集的1.58亿个Υ(2S)衰变事件，搜索χ_{bJ}(1P)到e⁺μ⁻、e⁺τ⁻或μ⁺τ⁻等带电轻子对（charged leptons）的衰变信号。

Result: 未观察到显著的信号，为χ_{bJ}(1P)到e⁺μ⁻的衰变设定了约10⁻⁶量级的分支比上限，到e⁺τ⁻或μ⁺τ⁻的衰变设定了约10⁻⁵量级的上限。对χ_{b0}(1P)衰变的限制被转化为对介导带电轻子味破坏的标量算符（scalar operators）相应威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）的约束。

Conclusion: 研究为χ_{bJ}(1P)衰变中的带电轻子味破坏过程设定了迄今为止最严格的实验上限，这些结果对超出标准模型的新物理模型，特别是那些包含标量算符的模型，构成了重要的约束。

Abstract: We report the first searches for charged-lepton-flavor violation in decays of $χ_{bJ}(1P)$ ($J=0, 1,$ and $2$) to a pair of charged leptons using 158 million $Υ(2S)$ decays collected with the Belle detector in $e^+e^-$ collisions at the KEKB collider. No significant signal is observed, and we set upper limits on the branching fractions for $χ_{bJ}(1P)$ decays to $e^\pmμ^\mp$ at the level of $10^{-6}$ and to $e^\pmτ^\mp$ or $μ^\pmτ^\mp$ at the level of $10^{-5}$. Limits on $χ_{b0}(1P)$ decays are translated into bounds on the corresponding Wilson coefficients of scalar operators that mediate charged-lepton-flavor violation.

### [125] [Why (and How) LGADs Work: Ionization, Space Charge, and Gain Saturation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10841)
*N. Cartiglia,A. R. Altamura,R. Arcidiacono,M. Durando,S. Galletto,M. Ferrero,L. Lanteri,A. Losana,L. Massaccesi,L. Menzio,F. Siviero,V. Sola,R. White*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过引入空间电荷效应和增益饱和两种物理机制，修正了传统模拟对LGAD探测器时间分辨率的过高估计，建立了更精确的Landau噪声模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低增益雪崩探测器（Low-Gain Avalanche Detectors, LGADs）的时间分辨率受电子噪声和Landau噪声共同影响。传统模拟仅考虑初始电离会显著高估实测的Landau噪声，需要更精确的物理模型来解释实验数据。

Method: 研究引入了两种关键物理机制：电子/空穴漂移过程中的空间电荷效应（space charge effects）和平滑初始电荷分布，以及倍增过程中的增益饱和（gain saturation）抑制大振幅涨落。所有步骤均在快速模拟程序Weightfield2（WF2）中实现。

Result: 模型通过多个独立实验观测得到验证：包括测量电荷分布随增益的演化、Landau尾端事件的时间分辨率，以及时间性能的厚度依赖性。研究还讨论了基于增益饱和的数据驱动增益测量方法及其对增益层设计的启示。

Conclusion: 空间电荷效应和增益饱和机制对于准确模拟LGAD探测器的Landau噪声至关重要。该模型成功解释了实验观测，并为增益层优化设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The temporal resolution of Low-Gain Avalanche Detectors (LGADs), also known as Ultra-Fast Silicon Detectors (UFSDs), is governed by two contributions: jitter, arising from electronic noise and signal slew rate, and the Landau noise term, arising from the non-uniform energy deposition of minimum ionizing particles (MIPs). We show that a correct simulation of the initial ionization alone significantly overestimates the measured Landau noise. Two additional physical mechanisms are necessary to reproduce the data: space charge effects during electron/hole drift, which smooth the granularity of the initial charge distribution, and gain saturation during multiplication, which preferentially suppresses large-amplitude fluctuations. All steps of the model have been implemented in the fast simulation program Weightfield2 (WF2). The model is validated against several independent experimental observations: the evolution of the measured charge distribution with gain, the temporal resolution of events in the Landau tail, and the thickness dependence of timing performance. We also discuss a data-driven gain measurement method based on gain saturation, and implications for gain layer design.

</details>

Witek,L. Witola,T. Wolf,E. Wood,G. Wormser,S. A. Wotton,H. Wu,J. Wu,X. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,R. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: LHCb实验测量了B_s^0→D_s^-π^+衰变中的未标记CP不对称性，结果为(-1.4±5.9±1.1)×10^{-3，与标准模型预期一致，为树级b强子衰变中的新物理提供了直接约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在测量B_s^0→D_s^-π^+衰变中的未标记CP不对称性（untagged CP asymmetry），以检验标准模型（Standard Model）预期并为树级b强子衰变（tree-level b-hadron decays）中的新物理（new physics）提供直接约束。

Method: 使用LHCb实验在2016-2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，中心质心能量为13 TeV，总积分亮度为5.4 fb^{-1}。在两种D_s^-介子衰变模式（D_s^-→K^-K^+π^-和D_s^-→π^-π^+π^-）中测量CP不对称性。

Result: 测量得到的未标记CP不对称性为⟨A^s_untagged⟩ = (-1.4±5.9(统计)±1.1(系统))×10^{-3}。该结果与标准模型预期一致，为树级b强子衰变中的新物理提供了直接约束。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型预期相符，未发现显著CP破坏（CP violation）证据。该测量为树级b强子衰变中的新物理提供了重要的实验约束，支持标准模型在此类衰变中的有效性。

Abstract: A measurement of the flavour-untagged decay-time-integrated ${C\!P}$ asymmetry in the flavour-specific decay ${B_s^0 \to D_s^-π^+}$, ${\langle A^s_{\rm untagged}\rangle}$, is performed using proton-proton collision data collected by the LHCb experiment between 2016 and 2018 at a center-of-mass energy of ${13\,{\rm TeV}}$, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of ${5.4\,{\rm fb}^{-1}}$. The ${C\!P}$ asymmetry is measured in two $D_s^-$ meson decay modes, ${D_s^- \to K^-K^+π^-}$ and ${D_s^- \to π^-π^+π^-}$. The combined result, $\langle A^s_{\rm untagged}\rangle = ( -1.4 \pm 5.9\,\rm{(stat)} \pm 1.1\,\rm{(syst)}) \times 10^{-3}$, is consistent with the Standard Model expectation and provides a direct constraint on new physics in tree-level $b$-hadron decays.

</details>


### [127] [First Axion Search Results of the SUPAX Prototype Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10943)
*Tim Schneemann,Hendrik Bekker,Dmitry Budker,Kristof Schmieden,Matthias Schott,Malavika Unni,Arne Wickenbrock*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: SUPerconduction AXion search experiment (Supax) 原型实验使用铜腔在2K温度和12T磁场下探测约34μeV质量的轴子，排除了轴子-光子耦合常数大于1.6×10⁻¹³ GeV⁻¹的可能性，同时排除了相同质量范围内动力学混合参数大于1.4×10⁻¹²的暗光子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Supax实验旨在探测轴子类粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs），这些粒子是暗物质候选者，并能解决强CP问题（strong-CP problem）。原型实验的目标是验证实验方案，为未来在8-30μeV质量范围内的正式实验做准备。

Method: 采用haloscope型探测器原型，使用铜腔（copper cavity）冷却至2K温度，并在12T磁场中运行。通过分析实验数据来探测约34μeV质量范围内的轴子和暗光子。

Result: 在约34μeV质量处，排除了轴子-光子耦合常数（axion-photon coupling）|g_{aγγ}| > 1.6×10⁻¹³ GeV⁻¹的可能性。同时排除了相同质量范围内暗光子（dark photons）的动力学混合参数（kinetic mixing parameter）χ > 1.4×10⁻¹²。

Conclusion: 原型实验成功验证了Supax实验方案，为未来在8-30μeV质量范围内探测轴子类粒子的正式实验奠定了基础。论文总结了实验装置和分析策略的详细信息。

Abstract: The SUPerconduction AXion search experiment (Supax) is a future haloscope-type detector designed to probe axion-like particles (ALPs) as candidates for dark matter and solutions to the strong-CP problem in the mass range between $8\,μ$eV and $30\,μ$eV. In the course of the preparation of Supax, a prototype experiment was built and operated. Using a copper cavity, cooled down to a temperature of 2 K and operated in a magnetic field of 12 T, we probe axion masses around $34\,μ$eV and exclude axion-photon couplings down to $|g_{aγγ}|> 1.6\cdot 10^{-13}$GeV$^{-1}$. The data was also used to exclude dark photons in the same mass range with a kinetic mixing parameter of $χ> 1.4\cdot 10^{-12}$. Details of the experimental setup and the analysis strategy are summarized in this paper.

</details>


### [128] [Search for Z' bosons decaying into charginos in final states with two oppositely charged leptons and missing transverse momentum in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11035)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文使用CMS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中收集的138 fb⁻¹数据，搜索衰变为一对chargino（带电荷超对称粒子）的大质量轻子不敏感Z'玻色子。通过参数化神经网络进行信号提取，结果与标准模型预期一致，并设置了Z'玻色子产生截面的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是搜索超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model）的新物理，特别是通过寻找源自额外U(1)'规范对称性扩展至最小超对称标准模型（Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model）的大质量轻子不敏感（leptophobic）Z'玻色子。这些Z'玻色子衰变为一对chargino，为探索超对称（supersymmetry）和额外规范玻色子提供了重要途径。

Method: 方法基于CMS实验在2016-2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量为13 TeV，总积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。最终态包含两个带相反电荷的轻子和缺失横向动量（missing transverse momentum）。信号提取采用参数化神经网络（parametrized neural network）进行分析。

Result: 测量结果与标准模型（Standard Model）预期一致，未发现显著超出。研究设置了Z'玻色子产生截面作为Z'和chargino质量函数的上限。对于Z'玻色子专有衰变为chargino（charginos随后衰变为W玻色子和neutralino）的特定情况，分析排除了质量高达约3.5 TeV的Z'玻色子。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在138 fb⁻¹的LHC数据中未观测到轻子不敏感Z'玻色子衰变为chargino的信号。研究为Z'玻色子产生截面设置了严格的实验上限，并排除了特定衰变模式下质量高达3.5 TeV的Z'玻色子存在，为超对称和额外规范玻色子模型提供了重要约束。

Abstract: Massive leptophobic Z' bosons decaying to a pair of charginos are searched for in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, using data samples collected by the CMS experiment in 2016, 2017, and 2018, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The Z' bosons originate from an additional U(1)' gauge symmetry extended to the minimal supersymmetric standard model. The final state consists of two oppositely charged leptons and missing transverse momentum. The signal extraction is performed with a parametrized neural network. The measurements are found to be consistent with the standard model expectations. Upper limits are set on the Z' boson production cross sections as a function of the Z' and chargino masses. The analysis excludes Z' boson masses up to about 3.5 TeV for the specific case of Z' bosons decaying exclusively to charginos, with the charginos decaying to W bosons and neutralinos.

</details>

### [129] [Fast Programming of In-Plane Hyperbolic Phonon Polariton Optics Through van der Waals Crystals using the Phase-Change Material In3SbTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10900)
*Lina Jäckering,Umberto Saldarelli,Aaron Moos,Lukas Conrads,Enrique Terán-García,Christian Lanza,Aitana Tarazaga Martín-Luengo,Gonzalo Álvarez-Pérez,Pablo Alonso-González,Matthias Wuttig,Thomas Taubner*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于光学编程的方法，在α-MoO3/In3SbTe2异质结构中可重构双曲声子极化激元（HPhPs）的激发与限制结构，实现了对高度定向极化激元传播的快速、灵活调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双曲声子极化激元（hyperbolic phonon polaritons, HPhPs）具有高度定向性，为纳米尺度能量路由提供了新途径。然而，传统纳米加工方法制备高效且精确对准的极化激元激发结构耗时且昂贵，限制了其应用灵活性。

Method: 研究采用光学编程方法，在沉积于In3SbTe2上的α-MoO3薄片中编程多种激发和限制纳米结构。关键创新在于薄片沉积后的光学编程，使激发条纹能够与薄片的[001]轴精确对准，从而控制定向极化激元传播。

Result: 展示了两种结构能力：1）光学编程的圆盘结构，显示出与金盘聚焦相似的调谐范围和限制能力；2）通过将单圆盘重构为双圆盘结构，创建了面内HPhPs腔体，仅通过重新编程圆盘间距即可定制限制效果。

Conclusion: 该制造方案提供了快速周转时间、灵活对准和结构重构能力，是一种快速、高效且多功能的按需定制高度定向极化激元传播和限制的方法。

Abstract: The high directionality of hyperbolic phonon polaritons (HPhPs) has opened radically new ways to route and steer the flow of energy at the nanoscale. However, launching HPhPs requires fabricating efficient and precisely aligned polariton launching structures, which remains time-consuming and expensive with conventional nanofabrication approaches. Recently, using optical laser pulses, polariton launching structures have been programmed into the plasmonic phase-change material In3SbTe2. Here, we leverage this approach to reconfigure HPhPs by programming a variety of launching and confining nanostructures through α-MoO3 flakes deposited onto In3SbTe2. Importantly, optical programming after flake deposition enables alignment of launching stripes to the [001]-axis of the flake, essential to control the directional polariton propagation. We showcase these capabilities in a variety of structures: i) an optically programmed disk, showing similar tuning ranges and confinement as focusing by gold disks; and ii) a cavity for in-plane HPhPs created by reconfiguring the single disk to a double disk structure, tailoring the confinement by simply reprogramming the disk distance. Our fabrication scheme offers fast turn-around times, flexible alignment and the opportunity to reconfigure the structures. Thus, it is a fast, efficient and versatile way to tailor propagation and confinement of highly directional polaritons on demand.

### [130] [Topological Tunneling Magnetoresistance Driven by Type-II Weyl-Like States in the Room-Temperature Half-Metal Mn2PC Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10615)
*Wei Ma,Yu-Ting Wang,Wen-Bo Sun,Zhiheng Lv,Shuai Shi,Jian-Hong Rong,Tie-Lei Song,Zhi-Feng Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究预测Mn2PC单层是一种室温铁磁半金属（half-metal），居里温度达554K，具有II型外尔（Weyl-like）能带交叉和拓扑边缘态，在磁性隧道结中可实现拓扑隧穿磁阻效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索具有室温稳定性和拓扑特性的二维材料，为自旋电子学（spintronic）器件提供新的平台。当前需要寻找同时具备铁磁有序、半金属性和拓扑非平庸特性的材料体系。

Method: 研究采用第一性原理计算预测Mn2PC单层的电子结构，通过紧束缚模型（tight-binding calculations）验证拓扑边缘态，并分析自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）对能带的影响。

Result: Mn2PC单层显示为室温铁磁半金属，自旋向上通道在费米能级处具有II型外尔能带交叉，自旋向下通道为宽禁带半导体。自旋轨道耦合在交叉点打开11.2 meV的小能隙，产生显著的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和异常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）。

Conclusion: Mn2PC单层是一种有前景的室温拓扑自旋电子学平台，其拓扑隧穿磁阻效应和并发异常霍尔效应为实验探测拓扑载流子提供了可观测特征，有望应用于高性能自旋电子器件。

Abstract: We predict the tetragonal Mn2PC monolayer to be a room-temperature ferromagnetic half-metal with a Curie temperature of 554 K. The spin-up channel hosts type-II Weyl-like crossings at the Fermi level with highly anisotropic band dispersion, whereas the spin-down channel is a wide-gap semiconductor. Topological edge states obtained from tight-binding calculations confirm the non-trivial bulk topology. Spin-orbit coupling opens a small gap of 11.2 meV at the Weyl-like crossings, generating pronounced Berry curvature and a sizable anomalous Hall conductivity near the Fermi level. Based on these properties, we propose topological tunneling magnetoresistance in a Mn2PC-based magnetic tunnel junction: the parallel configuration conducts through fully spin-polarized Weyl-like carriers, while the antiparallel configuration is suppressed by the half-metallic gap, yielding a giant magnetoresistance ratio. The concurrent anomalous Hall effect in the conducting state provides an experimentally accessible signature of the topological carriers. These results identify the Mn2PC monolayer as a promising platform for room-temperature topological spintronic devices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高精度热容测量技术，在低于1K的温度下对吸附在高度结晶石墨表面的亚单层$^3$He进行实验观测，分析其热容行为与密度变化的关系。

Result: 实验发现了两个条纹畴壁相：$α_1$相具有可变的畴壁间距，其线性温度热容源于沿畴壁的一维声子激发；$α_2$相具有固定的畴壁间距。$α_2$相在临界密度下通过二阶相变熔化为$α_1$相，$α_1$相表现出量子向列态（quantum nematic/quantum liquid-crystal）特性。

Conclusion: 研究证实了$α_1$相中的量子向列态存在，成功调和了热力学数据与先前核磁共振数据之间的矛盾，为理解低维量子系统的相变机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: We report high-precision heat-capacity measurements of submonolayer $^3$He adsorbed on highly crystalline graphite, revealing new aspects of the commensurate$-$incommensurate transition. Below 1K, two possible striped domain-wall phases emerge: $α_1$ with variable wall spacing and $α_2$ with fixed spacing. The $T$-linear heat capacity in $α_1$ arises from one-dimensional phonons along the walls. $α_2$ melts into $α_1$ at a critical density via a second-order transition, consistent with a quantum nematic (quantum liquid-crystal) state in $α_1$, and reconciling thermodynamic and prior nuclear-magnetic data.

### [132] [Neural Field Thermal Tomography: A Differentiable Physics Framework for Non-Destructive Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11045)
*Tao Zhong,Yixun Hu,Dongzhe Zheng,Aditya Sood,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NeFTY（Neural Field Thermal Tomography）提出了一种基于可微分物理框架的三维材料特性重建方法，通过瞬态表面温度测量实现高精度亚表面缺陷定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热成像方法依赖像素级一维近似，忽略了横向扩散效应；而基于软约束的物理信息神经网络（PINNs）在瞬态扩散场景中因梯度刚性（gradient stiffness）常失效。需要一种能精确重建三维材料特性的新方法。

Method: NeFTY将三维扩散率场（diffusivity field）参数化为连续神经场（continuous neural field），通过严格数值求解器进行优化。采用可微分物理求解器（differentiable physics solver）将热力学定律作为硬约束（hard constraints）强制执行，同时保持高分辨率三维层析所需的内存效率。

Result: 在合成数据上的实验验证表明，NeFTY在亚表面缺陷定位（subsurface defect localization）精度上显著优于基线方法。其离散化后优化范式（discretize-then-optimize paradigm）有效缓解了逆热传导问题固有的谱偏差（spectral bias）和不适定性（ill-posedness）。

Conclusion: NeFTY框架能够恢复任意尺度的亚表面缺陷，为三维材料特性定量重建提供了有效的可微分物理解决方案。

Abstract: We propose Neural Field Thermal Tomography (NeFTY), a differentiable physics framework for the quantitative 3D reconstruction of material properties from transient surface temperature measurements. While traditional thermography relies on pixel-wise 1D approximations that neglect lateral diffusion, and soft-constrained Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) often fail in transient diffusion scenarios due to gradient stiffness, NeFTY parameterizes the 3D diffusivity field as a continuous neural field optimized through a rigorous numerical solver. By leveraging a differentiable physics solver, our approach enforces thermodynamic laws as hard constraints while maintaining the memory efficiency required for high-resolution 3D tomography. Our discretize-then-optimize paradigm effectively mitigates the spectral bias and ill-posedness inherent in inverse heat conduction, enabling the recovery of subsurface defects at arbitrary scales. Experimental validation on synthetic data demonstrates that NeFTY significantly improves the accuracy of subsurface defect localization over baselines. Additional details at https://cab-lab-princeton.github.io/nefty/

</details>
