### [133] [Bridge Scaling in Conditioned Henyey-Greenstein Random Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10147)
*Claude Zeller*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛模拟研究三维随机游走的固定长度桥路径（bridge paths），发现其与经典布朗运动理论存在四个异常：超扩散平均振幅、异常扩散系数标度、瑞利分布的中点深度分布，以及桥条件平均方向余弦收敛于-2/3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三维随机游走中固定长度桥路径的结构特性，特别是当散射角度遵循Henyey-Greenstein分布且步长呈指数分布时的行为。关注这些路径与经典布朗运动理论预测的偏差。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法，研究不对称参数g从0到0.95、路径长度从4到200步的三维随机游走。关键结构特征是游走在二维马尔可夫状态空间（深度，方向余弦）上演化，而非仅标量深度坐标。

Result: 发现了四个相对于经典布朗运动理论的异常：1）平均振幅呈超扩散标度，各向同性散射时幂指数为0.57-0.58；2）扩散系数标度为输运平均自由程的0.415次方；3）中点深度分布为瑞利分布而非半正态分布；4）桥条件平均方向余弦在最后一步收敛于-2/3。

Conclusion: 所有异常均归因于二维状态空间结构。两个异常指数之和约为1，表明共同的几何起源。主要未解问题是这构成永久普适类转变还是异常缓慢的布朗运动交叉行为。

Abstract: We study fixed-length bridge paths -- half-space excursions that start and end at a planar boundary -- for three-dimensional random walks with Henyey-Greenstein scattering angles and exponentially distributed step lengths, using Monte Carlo simulation over asymmetry parameter g from 0 to 0.95 and path lengths from 4 to 200 steps. The key structural feature is that the walk evolves on a two-dimensional Markovian state space (depth, direction cosine) rather than the scalar depth coordinate alone.
  Four anomalies with respect to classical Brownian-excursion theory are reported. The mean amplitude scales super-diffusively, as path length to a power of 0.57--0.58 for isotropic scattering, nine standard deviations above the Brownian prediction of 0.5, with no sign of convergence out to 200 steps. The diffusion coefficient scales as the transport mean free path to the power 0.415 rather than the predicted 1.0. The midpoint depth distribution is Rayleigh rather than half-normal, consistent with a two-dimensional Bessel process. The bridge-conditioned mean direction cosine converges to minus two-thirds at the final step, independently of the asymmetry parameter and initial direction -- the classical Milne result anchored by the H-function moment identity.
  All anomalies are attributed to the two-dimensional state-space structure. The two anomalous exponents sum to approximately unity, suggesting a common geometric origin. Whether this constitutes a permanent universality-class shift or an anomalously slow crossover to Brownian-excursion behaviour remains the primary open question.

</details>


### [134] [Integrability-breaking-induced Mpemba effect in spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10164)
*Adam J. McRoberts*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了弱破坏可积性的自旋链中存在两种不同的对称性恢复姆潘巴效应机制：早期高温系统因相空间更大而恢复更快，后期低温系统因超扩散自旋流体动力学寿命更长而恢复更快，且仅出现在非可积模型中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索弱破坏可积性的自旋链中对称性恢复姆潘巴效应的不同机制，特别是在各向同性自旋链淬火失衡后，温度差异如何影响各向同性恢复的动态过程。

Method: 研究方法基于分析各向同性自旋链通过抑制z分量而淬火失衡的系统，不诱导任何净磁化，比较可积与非可积模型中温度对对称性恢复动力学的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示存在两种不同的对称性恢复机制：早期高温系统因相空间更大而恢复更快，后期低温系统因超扩散自旋流体动力学（superdiffusive spin hydrodynamics）寿命参数化更大而恢复更快，但后者仅出现在非可积模型中。

Conclusion: 结论表明，根据温度和初始对称性破坏程度的具体细节，各向同性恢复曲线可能在早期、晚期、两者皆无或两者皆有交叉点，这揭示了弱破坏可积性系统中对称性恢复动力学的复杂行为。

Abstract: We show that there are two distinct mechanisms that can cause the symmetry-restoration Mpemba effect in spin chains with \textit{weakly broken} integrability, such that the asymptotic equilibration is diffusive, but the lifetime of anomalously fast spin hydrodynamics at low temperature is parametrically large. In particular, we consider isotropic spin chains quenched out of equilibrium by suppressing the $z$-components, without inducing any net magnetisation. Initially, the restoration of isotropy is faster in hotter systems -- because they have more phase space available to scramble their initial conditions -- which may cause the equilibration curves to cross at early times in both integrable and non-integrable systems. At later times, however, the equilibration is effectively hydrodynamic, and the \textit{colder} systems start to equilibrate faster as the lifetime over which they evince superdiffusive spin hydrodynamics is parametrically larger -- but only in \textit{non}-integrable models. Depending on the details of the temperatures and the extent of the initial symmetry-breaking, two isotropy-restoration curves may have a crossing at early time, late time, neither, or both.

</details>


### [135] [Violating the All-or-Nothing Picture of Local Charges in Non-Hermitian Bosonic Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10972)
*Mizuki Yamaguchi,Naoto Shiraishi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文通过构造具体反例，挑战了局部对易荷（local commuting charges）普遍存在的"全有或全无"经验预期，展示了在特定玻色子链模型中存在部分k-局部荷而非全部的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在挑战关于局部对易荷（local commuting charges）普遍存在的"全有或全无"（all-or-nothing）经验预期，这种预期在相关研究领域中被广泛接受但缺乏严格证明。

Method: 在具有对称最近邻跳跃（symmetric nearest-neighbor hopping）和任意在位项（包括非厄米项）的玻色子链模型类中，作者构造了具体的反例系统，并给出了k-局部荷（k-local charges）存在的充分必要条件。

Result: 研究构造了具有3-局部荷但无其他非平凡局部荷的非厄米模型，以及除k=4外所有k值都存在k-局部荷的模型。这些结果表明基于3-局部荷的Grabowski-Mathieu可积性检验并非普遍适用。

Conclusion: 论文通过提供明确反例推翻了关于局部对易荷的"全有或全无"经验预期，建立了该类模型中k-局部荷存在的完整分类，并发现了新的可积模型（integrable models）。

Abstract: We present explicit counterexamples to a widespread empirical expectation that local commuting charges display all-or-nothing behavior. In the class of bosonic chains with symmetric nearest-neighbor hopping and arbitrary on-site terms (including non-Hermitian terms), we exhibit systems that possess k-local charges for some but not all k. Concretely, we construct non-Hermitian models with a 3-local charge but no other nontrivial local charges and models with k-local charges for all k except k = 4. These results show that the Grabowski--Mathieu integrability test based on 3-local charges is not universally applicable. We further give necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of k-local charges in this class, yielding an exhaustive classification and uncovering additional integrable models.

</details>


### [136] [Directional information transfer between interacting Brownian particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10475)
*Tenta Tani*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论分析两个相互作用的布朗粒子，揭示了质量不对称性如何导致信息流的定向传输，从较重粒子流向较轻粒子，且净信息流与质量比呈对数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解定向信息流（directional information flow）的物理机制对于推进信息热力学（information thermodynamics）和随机计算（stochastic computing）至关重要。然而，机械运动与因果信息传递（causal information transfer）之间的基本联系仍然不明确。

Method: 研究考察了限制在一维势（one-dimensional potential）中的两个相互作用的布朗粒子（Brownian particles）。通过模拟其朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics），使用转移熵（transfer entropy）量化因果信息交换。

Result: 质量不对称性（mass asymmetry）本质上打破了信息流的对称性，诱导了从较重粒子到较轻粒子的净定向传输。较重粒子具有更大的惯性和更高的主动信息存储（active information storage），能更长时间地抵抗热涨落（thermal fluctuations）而保留其轨迹记忆，从而作为信息源。净传输受记忆容量差异和粒子轨迹可预测性之间的竞争支配。

Conclusion: 净信息流与质量比呈对数关系（scales logarithmically with the mass ratio）。这些发现为转移熵的物理意义和一般物理系统中信息流的本质提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate how information flows when two particles interact with each other. Understanding the physical mechanisms of directional information flow is crucial for advancing information thermodynamics and stochastic computing. However, the fundamental connection between mechanical motion and causal information transfer remains elusive. To focus only on essential effects of physical dynamics, we examine two interacting Brownian particles confined in a one-dimensional potential. By simulating their Langevin dynamics, we quantify the causal information exchange using transfer entropy. We demonstrate that a mass asymmetry inherently breaks the symmetry of information flow, inducing a net directional transfer from the heavier to the lighter particle. Physically, the heavier particle, possessing larger inertia and higher active information storage, retains the memory of its trajectory longer against thermal fluctuations, thereby acting as a source of information. We analytically clarify that this net transfer is governed by a competition between the difference in memory capacity and the predictability of the particle trajectories. Furthermore, we reveal that the net information flow scales logarithmically with the mass ratio. These findings provide essential insights into the physical significance of transfer entropy and the nature of information flow in general physical systems.

</details>


### [137] [Dissipation- versus Chaos-Induced Relaxation in Non-Markovian Quantum Many-Body Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10815)
*Gabriel Almeida,Pedro Ribeiro,Masudul Haque,Lucas Sá*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在相互作用的量子多体系统中，弛豫向平衡反映了内部混沌动力学与环境耗散之间的竞争。传统马尔可夫浴通常产生指数衰减，而非马尔可夫耗散可能导致更复杂的行为，包括代数弛豫。

Method: 研究采用开放Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型与赝能隙（pseudogapped）费米子浴耦合，利用Keldysh形式在大N极限下计算稳态关联函数。

Result: 结果揭示了一个丰富的动力学相图，包括浴驱动的幂律弛豫（power-law relaxation）、混沌驱动的指数衰减（exponential decay），以及一个中间预弛豫相（pre-relaxation phase），其中指数衰减过渡到代数衰减。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明，非马尔可夫环境能够定性重塑强关联量子多体系统中的弛豫机制，揭示了复杂弛豫行为的物理起源。

Abstract: In interacting quantum many-body systems, relaxation toward equilibrium reflects a competition between internal chaotic dynamics and environmental dissipation. While conventional Markovian baths typically produce exponential decay, non-Markovian dissipation can give rise to more intricate behavior, including algebraic relaxation. We study an open Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model coupled to a pseudogapped fermionic bath, using the Keldysh formalism to compute steady-state correlations in the large-$N$ limit. Our results uncover a rich dynamical phase diagram, with regimes of bath-driven power-law relaxation, chaos-driven exponential decay, and an intermediate pre-relaxation phase where exponential decay crosses over to algebraic decay. These findings demonstrate that non-Markovian environments can qualitatively reshape relaxation mechanisms in strongly correlated quantum many-body systems.

### [138] [Complexity and Operator Growth in Holographic 6d SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10106)
*Ali Fatemiabhari,Carlos Nunez,Ricardo T. Santamaria*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了六维超共形场论中的Krylov复杂度，通过全息对偶分析大质量测地探针在相应几何中的动力学，揭示了算子增长与内部对称性及quiver结构的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索高维全息共形理论中的Krylov复杂度，特别是六维${\cal N}=(1,0)$超共形场论，这些理论具有大质量IIA型超重力中的全息对偶。研究旨在理解算子增长如何探测强耦合共形场论中的内部对称性和quiver结构。

Method: 方法基于全息对偶，将Krylov复杂度增长与下落粒子的固有动量相关联。分析了大质量测地探针在相应几何中的动力学，允许粒子沿三个方向运动：径向AdS坐标、与$SU(2)_R$对称性相关的内部$S^2$、以及参数化quiver的坐标。对代表性quiver配置进行了解析和数值分析。

Result: 沿quiver方向的运动在早期通常被阻尼和局域化，而晚期行为由径向AdS运动主导。广义固有动量在晚期线性增长，与共形理论中Krylov复杂度的预期一致。角动量（$SU(2)_R$荷）的引入对允许运动施加了额外约束，并修改了早期动力学，但未改变渐近行为。

Conclusion: 这些结果首次探索了高维全息共形理论中的Krylov复杂度，揭示了算子增长如何探测强耦合共形场论中的内部对称性和quiver结构。研究为理解全息对偶框架下的算子动力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study Krylov (spread) complexity in strongly coupled six-dimensional ${\cal N}=(1,0)$ superconformal field theories with holographic duals in massive type IIA supergravity. Extending recent holographic proposals relating Krylov complexity growth to the proper momentum of an infalling particle, we analyse the dynamics of massive geodesic probes in these geometries. In our setup, the bulk particle is allowed to move along three directions: the radial AdS coordinate, the internal $S^2$ associated with the $SU(2)_R$ symmetry, and the coordinate parametrising the quiver. In the dual field theory these motions encode, respectively, operator growth, the presence of R-symmetry charges, and spreading across different nodes of the quiver. We analyse the geodesic motion both analytically and numerically for representative quiver configurations. The motion along the quiver direction is typically damped and localised at early times, while the late-time behaviour is dominated by the radial AdS motion. As a consequence, the generalised proper momentum grows linearly at late times, consistent with expectations for Krylov complexity in conformal theories. The inclusion of angular momentum ($SU(2)_R$ charge) introduces additional constraints on the allowed motion and modifies the early-time dynamics while leaving the asymptotic behaviour unchanged. These results provide a first exploration of Krylov complexity in higher-dimensional holographic conformal theories and reveal how operator growth can probe both internal symmetries and quiver structure in strongly coupled conformal field theories.

</details>


### [139] [Entanglement and Renormalization Group Irreversibility of Quantum Field Theory in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10117)
*Nicolás Abate,Ignacio Salazar,Gonzalo Torroba*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究利用量子信息论方法，在刚性反德西特（anti de Sitter, AdS）时空中探索量子场论（quantum field theory, QFT）的非微扰方面，证明了重整化群（renormalization group, RG）在AdS时空中的不可逆性，并发展了计算纠缠熵和RG荷（RG charges）的数值方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重整化群（renormalization group, RG）流的不可逆性在平直时空中已得到确立，但在负曲率且具有渐近类时边界的AdS时空中是否依然成立尚不明确。研究旨在探究AdS时空中的红外动力学如何影响RG不可逆性，并发展适用于该几何结构的量子信息论方法。

Method: 利用强次可加性（strong subadditivity）和AdS不变性，推导了量子场论真空纠缠熵（vacuum entanglement entropy）与其紫外固定点（ultraviolet fixed point）之间差异的熵二阶微分不等式。针对AdS中的自由标量场和费米子理论，开发了适应几何结构的格点（lattice）表述，并计算了纠缠熵和RG荷。

Result: 通过熵不等式定义了测量相关自由度数量的RG荷，并在2、3、4维时空中证明了RG的不可逆性。在AdS₂中，获得了大质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermion）的解析结果，并与数值格点计算进行了比较，阐明了共形理论（conformal theories）与大质量理论在AdS中的区别。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了AdS时空中重整化群流的不可逆性，并发展了结合量子信息论和几何适应方法的分析框架。研究结果为理解负曲率时空中的量子场论非微扰特性提供了新视角，同时展示了纠缠熵在探测RG流中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study nonperturbative aspects of quantum field theory (QFT) in rigid anti de Sitter (AdS) spacetime using quantum information theoretic methods. While irreversibility of renormalization group (RG) flows is well established in flat space, it is not obvious whether it persists in AdS, where negative curvature and an asymptotic timelike boundary significantly modify infrared dynamics. Using strong subadditivity and AdS invariance, we derive an entropic second-order differential inequality for the difference between the vacuum entanglement entropy of a QFT and that of its ultraviolet fixed point, evaluated for spherical bulk regions. This inequality allows us to define RG charges that measure the relevant number of degrees of freedom, and we prove the irreversibility of the RG in $2,\,3,$ and $4$ spacetime dimensions. We further analyze free scalar and fermion theories in AdS, developing lattice formulations adapted to the geometry and computing entanglement entropies and RG charges. In AdS$_2$, we obtain analytic results for a massive Dirac fermion and compare them with numerical lattice calculations. These examples illustrate the general irreversibility theorem and clarify the distinction between conformal and massive theories in AdS.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用泛函重整化群（functional renormalisation group）方法计算了类空间动量（spacelike momenta）下标量-引力子三点散射顶点的完整动量依赖性，并讨论了向闵可夫斯基分支（Minkowski branch）的解析延拓及其角依赖性。

Result: 成功重建了顶点的时间分量（timelike part），并用于计算散射振幅和截面，结果显示截面在小能量下还原为广义相对论结果，且在紫外区域满足幺正性。

Conclusion: 渐近安全量子引力理论能够自洽地描述引力介导的散射过程，其预测在低能极限下与广义相对论一致，同时在紫外区域保持幺正性，为该理论的物理自洽性提供了重要支持。

Abstract: We compute the graviton-mediated two-to-two scattering amplitude and cross section for scalar particles in asymptotically safe quantum gravity. Specifically, we compute the full momentum dependence of the scalar-graviton three-point scattering vertex for spacelike momenta with the functional renormalisation group. We also discuss the analytic continuation to the Minkowski branch, and in particular its angular dependence. Then, the timelike part of the vertex is reconstructed and used to compute the scattering amplitude and cross-section. We show that the cross-section reduces to that in General Relativity at small energies, and it respects unitarity in the UV.

### [141] [States of 2D Yang-Mills and Large-Volume Entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10171)
*Dmitry Melnikov,Jefferson T. Oliveira,Valmir Peixoto,Marcia Tenser*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了二维杨-米尔斯理论（2D Yang-Mills theory）中的纠缠特性，将其视为涌现空间（emergent space）的准拓扑模型。研究发现，由黎曼面（Riemann surfaces）上欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path integrals）定义的态具有热场双重结构（thermofield double structure），其纠缠随总面积和拓扑缺陷（topological defects）数量增加而减少，在无限面积极限下可分离。相反，威尔逊线（Wilson lines）和威尔逊圈（Wilson loops）则产生丰富非单调的纠缠熵行为，某些离散构型甚至在无限面积下仍保持有限纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将二维杨-米尔斯理论视为涌现空间的准拓扑模型，探索其中的纠缠特性。该工作旨在理解不同状态类别（特别是由黎曼面上欧几里得路径积分定义的态与由威尔逊线/圈生成的态）在纠缠行为上的根本差异。

Method: 研究方法基于二维杨-米尔斯理论框架，分析了两类不同状态：一类是通过黎曼面上的欧几里得路径积分定义的态；另一类是由威尔逊线和威尔逊圈生成的态。通过计算这些态的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）并研究其随系统参数（如总面积、拓扑缺陷数量）的变化行为。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）黎曼面路径积分定义的二分态具有热场双重结构，其纠缠熵随总面积和拓扑缺陷数量增加而一致减少，在无限面积极限下变为可分离态；2）威尔逊线和威尔逊圈产生丰富非单调的纠缠熵行为；3）对于特定离散构型，纠缠在无限面积下仍保持有限，约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrices）表现为有限维投影算符，作用在非平凡真空扇区（vacuum sectors）上。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，二维杨-米尔斯理论中的纠缠行为高度依赖于状态类型。特别地，威尔逊线/圈构型能在无限体积极限下维持有限纠缠，其约化密度矩阵具有有限维投影结构。此外，大体积效应（large-volume effects）对禁闭（confinement）有重要启示，特定渐近构型与禁闭力（confining force）的相变相关。

Abstract: We study entanglement in two-dimensional Yang-Mills theory, viewed as a quasi-topological model of emergent space. The most familiar class of states in this theory are states defined by Euclidean path integrals over Riemann surfaces. Bipartite states of this class have thermofield double structure, with entanglement consistently reducing with total area and the number of topological defects, turning separable in the infinite-area limit. In contrast, Wilson lines and loops generate rich non-monotonic behavior of the entanglement entropy. Most notably, we find that for a certain discrete set of configurations, entanglement remains finite at infinite area. The reduced density matrices, in such configurations, take the form of finite-dimensional projectors onto non-trivial vacuum sectors. We also discuss the implications of the large-volume effects for confinement and find that special asymptotic configurations are related to transitions in the confining force.

</details>

Method: 方法包括计算边界内外区域的正频Wightman函数，并利用这些函数推导玻色子电流真空期望值的解析表达式。研究假设圆形边界与磁通量同心，且标量量子场满足Robin边界条件。

In order to develop this analysis, we calculate the positive frequency Wightman functions for both regions, inside and outside the boundary. Using these functions, we obtain analytical expressions for the vacuum expectation bosonic currents. As we will see, these functions are presented in the form of the sum of boundary-free and boundary-induced parts. Abstract: We study large-spin operators in conformal field theories (CFTs) in spacetime dimensions $d>2$ by placing the theory on appropriate pp-wave backgrounds. We show that these geometries admit Heisenberg-group symmetries, and that these symmetries, combined with locality of quantum fields on such spacetimes, impose strong constraints on the asymptotic spectrum in the large-spin limit. The pp-wave backgrounds probe both the small-twist regime, corresponding to the Regge or light-cone bootstrap, and a strongly coupled regime of large twist. Finally, we demonstrate that causality (or the requirement that the energy be bounded from below) leads to a new unitarity bound in $3+1$ dimensions.

### [144] [Non-Lorentzian Supergravity from Matrix Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10278)
*Dawid Maskalaniec,Ziqi Yan,Utku Zorba*

Result: 在大N极限下，D-粒子的反作用将非洛伦兹超引力形变为洛伦兹IIA理论，为BFSS矩阵理论提供了全息描述。在中等大N情况下，非洛伦兹超引力全息映射到弱耦合体引力（bulk gravity）的领头阶贡献，这一近似非洛伦兹区域与十一维超引力的零维约化相关。

At a moderately large N such that the D-particles decouple at the leading order, this non-Lorentzian supergravity maps holographically to the leading-order contribution of weakly coupled bulk gravity. This approximately non-Lorentzian regime is related to the null reduction of eleven-dimensional supergravity. Within the non-Lorentzian supergravity, non-trivial dynamics arises from the backreaction of extended brane objects that form BPS states with the D-particles. Finally, we generalize these results to other D-brane and string soliton holographic constructions.

### [145] [Efficient Conformal Block Evaluation with GoBlocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10627)
*James Chryssanthacopoulos,Vasilis Niarchos,Constantinos Papageorgakis,Alexander G. Stapleton*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文介绍了GoBlocks：一个用Go语言实现的新型共形块生成器，用于在共形自举中实现快速、并行计算。该工具通过递归关系支持多点与导数基自举方法，并在计算速度与中等精度要求场景下相比scalar_blocks有显著性能提升。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在奇数时空维度中，共形块（conformal blocks）缺乏封闭解析形式，这限制了共形自举（conformal bootstrap）中的高效计算。因此需要开发能够快速进行并行评估的工具来促进相关研究。

Method: 作者开发了GoBlocks——一个基于Go编程语言的新型共形块生成器，利用递归关系（recursive relations）实现快速、实时的并行评估。该软件包支持多点（multi-point）和基于导数（derivative-based）的自举方法，并允许灵活控制精度与性能平衡。

Result: 与scalar_blocks软件包相比，GoBlocks在计算速度和中等精度要求的关键应用中显示出显著的速度提升，特别是在不需要超高精度的场景下。作为示例，作者将GoBlocks应用于三维Ising模型的混合关联子自举（mixed-correlator bootstrap），将其表述为适当截断方案中的非凸优化问题，并同时优化外部标度维度（external scaling dimensions）和OPE CFT数据。

Conclusion: GoBlocks为奇数维度共形自举计算提供了高效工具，在计算速度与精度平衡方面具有优势。该方法可扩展至更一般的O(N)矢量模型（vector models）中增加混合关联子数量的情况，展示了其在更广泛场景下的应用潜力。

Abstract: Conformal blocks in odd spacetime dimensions are not known in closed analytic form. To facilitate efficient computations in the conformal bootstrap, we introduce $\texttt{GoBlocks}$: a novel conformal-block generator implemented in the Go programming language, designed for rapid, on-the-fly, parallel evaluation using recursive relations. The package supports both multi-point and derivative-based bootstrap approaches and allows flexible control over accuracy and performance. We benchmark $\texttt{GoBlocks}$ against the $\texttt{scalar_blocks}$ package, finding significant speed improvements in applications where computational speed and moderate accuracy are critical, but ultra-high precision is not essential. As an illustration, we apply $\texttt{GoBlocks}$ to the mixed-correlator bootstrap of the three-dimensional Ising model, formulated as a non-convex optimisation problem in a suitable truncation scheme. We simultaneously optimise over external scaling dimensions and OPE CFT data. In addition, we discuss how the approach scales as we increase the number of mixed correlators in more general $O(N)$ vector models.

</details>


### [146] [Generalised Complex and Spinor Relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10819)
*Thomas C. De Fraja,Vincenzo Emilio Marotta,Richard J. Szabo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究Courant代数胚关系在Dirac结构、旋量、广义复结构和广义Kähler结构中的应用，特别关注T-对偶关系及其在超对称sigma模型和II型超引力方程中的兼容性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立Courant代数胚关系（Courant algebroid relations）在不同几何结构间的系统性联系，特别是探索这些关系如何统一描述Dirac结构、旋量以及广义复结构之间的对应关系。研究重点在于理解T-对偶（T-duality）如何通过这些关系实现不同几何结构间的转换。

Method: 采用Courant代数胚关系作为基本工具，定义了Dirac结构与旋量之间的关系概念。通过分析旋量关系在何种条件下给出Courant代数胚关系，并研究其如何下降为Dirac结构间的关系。特别地，证明了T-对偶关系可诱导连接T-对偶Courant代数胚的Dirac生成算子的旋量关系。

Result: 证明了T-对偶关系诱导的旋量关系推广了拓扑T-对偶相关的扭曲上同构（twisted cohomology）。引入了广义复结构（generalised complex structures）和广义Kähler结构（generalised Kähler structures）的关系概念，并将其用双Hermitian结构（bi-Hermitian structures）重新表述。这些结构诱导了$\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$超对称sigma模型的T-对偶关系。

Conclusion: 研究证明了T-对偶结构的存在性结果，并展示了T-对偶关系与II型超引力方程（Type II supergravity equations）的兼容性。这些结果为理解不同几何结构通过Courant代数胚关系和T-对偶建立的系统性联系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Courant algebroid relations are used to define notions of relations between Dirac structures and spinors. It is shown under which circumstances a spinor relation gives a Courant algebroid relation and how it descends to a relation between Dirac structures. A converse to this result is proved: a T-duality relation induces a spinor relation that links the Dirac generating operators defining T-dual Courant algebroids, generalising the isomorphism of twisted cohomology associated with topological T-duality. We introduce the notion of relation between generalised complex structures and characterise their reduction. We also define relations between generalised Kähler structures, and rephrase them in terms of bi-Hermitian structures which induce T-duality relations between $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ supersymmetric sigma-models. We prove existence results for T-dual structures, and demonstrate compatibility of T-duality relations with Type II supergravity equations.

### [147] [Nucleating an Inflationary Universe: Euclidean Wormholes and their No-Boundary Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11003)
*George Lavrelashvili,Jean-Luc Lehners*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文揭示无边界瞬子（no-boundary instantons）与欧几里得"酒杯"虫洞（Euclidean "wineglass" wormholes）属于同一类欧几里得解族，在零电荷极限下虫洞喉部收缩形成无边界瞬子，从而统一了两种宇宙初始条件理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无边界瞬子和欧几里得"酒杯"虫洞都被提出作为当前宇宙膨胀相的合适初始条件，特别是为暴胀阶段提供有利条件。这两种有限作用量解通常被视为互不相关，分别对应"从无创生时空"和"从欧几里得反德西特真空向上隧穿"的不同场景。

Method: 通过研究轴子（axionic）和磁（magnetic）酒杯虫洞的显式解，分析在零电荷极限下虫洞喉部的行为变化，探讨两种解之间的数学联系。

Result: 在零电荷极限下，虫洞喉部收缩（pinches off），形成与渐近反德西特区域断开连接的无边界瞬子，表明虫洞和无边界瞬子属于共同的欧几里得解族。同时解决了酒杯虫洞作用量可能为负的长期难题，并发现小电荷虫洞比大电荷解导致更长的暴胀阶段。

Conclusion: 虫洞和无边界瞬子构成统一的欧几里得解族，无边界瞬子在概率分布中占主导地位。这一发现将两种看似不同的宇宙初始条件理论联系起来，为理解宇宙早期演化提供了更完整的理论框架。

Abstract: No-boundary instantons and Euclidean "wineglass" wormholes have both been proposed as providing suitable initial conditions for the current expanding phase of our universe, and in particular for providing conditions that are favorable to an inflationary phase. These finite action solutions have generally been regarded as unrelated, and enacting different scenarios - in one case the creation of spacetime from nothing, and in the other up-tunneling from a Euclidean Anti-de Sitter vacuum. By studying explicit solutions of both axionic and magnetic wineglass wormholes, we find that in the zero-charge limit the throat of the wormholes pinches off, leaving a no-boundary instanton that disconnects from the asymptotic Anti-de Sitter region. Thus wormholes and no-boundary instantons are part of a common family of Euclidean solutions. Along the way, we resolve the long-known puzzle that the action of wineglass wormholes can become negative. Moreover, small-charge wormholes lead to a longer inflationary phase than large-charge solutions, while no-boundary instantons dominate the probability distribution overall.

### [148] [Bouncing singularities and thermal correlators on line defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11012)
*Simone Giombi,Yue-Zhou Li,Jieru Shan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究详细分析了全息共形场论中热关联函数的"反弹奇点（bouncing singularities）"，确认了这些奇点存在于体标量场和威尔逊线位移算符的推迟两点函数中，并揭示了两种独立计算方法的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全息共形场论中的热关联函数在复时间上表现出被称为"反弹奇点"的奇异性，这些奇点被认为与探测黑洞内部的体测地线相关。研究旨在详细重新计算这些关联函数，并探索不同计算方法之间的一致性。

Method: 采用两种独立方法：1）大频率WKB分析，在视界处施加流入边界条件；2）渐近算子乘积展开（OPE）分析，仅依赖近边界展开，无需黑洞内部直接信息。将计算扩展到有限温度规范理论中威尔逊线上位移算符的推迟两点函数。

Result: 确认体标量场和缺陷关联函数都表现出反弹奇点，且WKB分析与渐近OPE分析之间完全一致。这种一致性表明反弹奇点和相应的OPE数据编码了推迟关联函数的普适高频率结构。

Conclusion: 反弹奇点和相应OPE数据编码了推迟关联函数的普适高频率结构，研究者提出了一个因子化公式来编码偏离这种普适性的偏差。两种独立方法的一致性表明这些奇点具有深刻的物理意义。

Abstract: Thermal correlators in holographic conformal field theories are known to exhibit singularities in complex time, sometimes referred to as ``bouncing singularities", which are believed to be related to bulk geodesics probing the black hole interior. These singularities correspond to exponentially suppressed contributions in the high-frequency limit of the thermal correlators. We revisit in detail the calculation of retarded two-point functions of local operators dual to bulk scalar fields in the planar AdS black hole background. We confirm that these correlators develop bouncing singularities, and highlight the agreement of two independent methods: a large frequency WKB analysis with infalling boundary conditions at the horizon; and an asymptotic OPE analysis that relies only on the near-boundary expansion, without any direct input from the black hole interior. We then extend these calculations to the case of the retarded two-point function of displacement operators on a Wilson line in the finite temperature gauge theory. This is computed holographically by solving the wave equation for the transverse fluctuations of the dual string worldsheet in the planar AdS black hole background. We find that these defect correlators also exhibit bouncing singularities, and again observe exact agreement between the WKB analysis sensitive to the black hole interior and the asymptotic OPE analysis. This agreement suggests that the bouncing singularities and the corresponding OPE data encode a universal high-frequency structure of the retarded correlators, and we propose a factorization formula that encodes the deviations from this universality.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究通过两种新颖的构造性证明，确立了路径积分与随机量子化方法在标量欧几里得量子场论中的等价性，为量子场论的基础理论提供了重要支持。

Abstract: We give two novel proofs that the path integral and stochastic quantizations of generic scalar Euclidean quantum field theories are equivalent. The second one works at the level of the path integral and avoids the full expansion of the Feynman perturbation series.

Method: 基于先前为平坦环面和二维球面开发的Zeitlin模型，该模型是与底层几何结构一致的磁流体动力学矩阵近似。本文推导了三维球面上轴对称磁流体动力学的简化模型，并给出了其哈密顿表述。

Indeed, they admit a geodesic formulation in the sense of Arnold, as a Lie--Poisson flow on the dual of an infinite-dimensional Lie algebra. Zeitlin's model, previously developed for MHD on the flat torus and the two-sphere, is a matrix approximation of MHD consistent with the underlying geometric structures. In this paper, we derive the reduced model of axially symmetric magnetohydrodynamics on the three-sphere and give its Hamiltonian formulation. We further extend finite dimensional Zeitlin's matrix model for MHD from 2D to axially symmetric 3D flows of magnetized fluids, yielding the first discrete model for 3D magnetohydrodynamics compatible with the underlying Lie--Poisson structure.

### [152] [Thermal enhancement of inflationary magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10157)
*Arjun Berera,Suddhasattwa Brahma,Zizang Qiu,Rudnei O. Ramos*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新的原初磁场生成机制，通过在暴胀期间将规范场置于热态而非标准的邦奇-戴维斯真空态，利用温度引入的物理尺度打破共形不变性，从而显著增强现今的磁场强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统暴胀磁生成模型面临共形不变性的阻碍，导致磁场能量密度随宇宙尺度因子按a^{-4}衰减，难以解释观测到的星系尺度磁场。本研究旨在探索通过热初始条件来缓解这一障碍的新途径。

Method: 假设规范场在暴胀期间处于热态（thermal state）而非标准的邦奇-戴维斯真空态（Bunch-Davies vacuum），利用温度T引入的物理尺度在态层面打破共形不变性，同时保持标准的麦克斯韦作用量不变。

Result: 热修正产生了一种"耗散增强（dissipative boost）"效应，将磁场能量密度标度从a^{-4}改变为a^{-3}，使现今磁场强度B_0在星系尺度上可能增强约10^8到10^16倍。虽然该玩具模型单独不能满足观测下限，但证明了热初始条件能显著缓解共形障碍。

Conclusion: 将这一机制嵌入完全动态的暖暴胀框架中，通过耗散持续维持热浴，为实现无需非最小耦合、反常背景动力学或非线性电动力学扩展的最小暴胀磁生成模型提供了极具前景的路径。

Abstract: We investigate primordial magnetogenesis by assuming the gauge field is prepared in a thermal state during inflation rather than the standard Bunch-Davies vacuum. The temperature $\mathcal{T}$ introduces a physical scale that breaks conformal invariance at the level of the state while preserving the standard Maxwell action. This modification results in a {\it dissipative boost} that alters the magnetic energy density scaling from $a^{-4}$ to $a^{-3}$, resulting in a present-day magnetic field $B_0$ enhancement that can potentially range from about $10^{8}$ to $10^{16}$ on galactic scales. While this toy model alone does not satisfy observational lower bounds, it demonstrates that thermal initial conditions can significantly mitigate the conformal obstruction. Our results suggest that embedding this mechanism within a fully dynamical warm inflation framework, where dissipation continuously maintains the thermal bath, provides a highly promising path towards successfully realizing a minimal model of inflationary magnetogenesis without the need to invoke non-minimal couplings, anomalous background dynamics or nonlinear extensions of electrodynamics.

### [153] [Interacting dark sector from intrinsic entropy couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10622)
*Erik Jensko,Elsa M. Teixeira,Vivian Poulin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新的相互作用暗区模型，将暗物质的内在熵（intrinsic entropy）与标量场暗能量耦合。该框架在保持背景宇宙学与ΛCDM一致的同时，在线性扰动层面产生尺度依赖的结构增长修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建一个理论自洽且观测可行的标准宇宙学模型扩展，探索暗区（dark sector）中新型相互作用。通过耦合暗物质内在熵与暗能量，为研究暗区相互作用开辟新方向。

Method: 采用相对论性完美流体（relativistic perfect fluids）的拉格朗日表述，构建了包含代数耦合和导数耦合（algebraic and derivative entropy couplings）的协变作用量。该框架保持背景宇宙学不变，仅在线性扰动层面引入修正。

Result: 熵耦合在暗物质欧拉方程（Euler equation）中产生尺度依赖修正，而连续性方程在线性阶保持不变。这种相互作用对应暗区内的纯动量交换（pure-momentum exchange）。内在熵扰动可携带原初尺度依赖性，非最小耦合导致结构增长的尺度依赖抑制或增强。

Conclusion: 该模型与当前宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background）观测兼容，同时在大尺度结构中产生独特信号。该框架为探索暗区相互作用提供了理论动机充分且观测可行的新途径。

Abstract: We introduce a new class of interacting dark sector models that couple the intrinsic entropy of dark matter to scalar field dark energy. Using the Lagrangian formulation for relativistic perfect fluids, we construct consistent covariant actions that incorporate algebraic and derivative entropy couplings. These interactions leave the expansion history unchanged, rendering the background cosmology indistinguishable from $Λ$CDM or uncoupled quintessence. At the level of cosmological perturbations, the entropy couplings generate scale-dependent modifications to the dark matter Euler equation, while the continuity equation remains unaltered at linear order. The resulting interactions correspond to a pure-momentum exchange within the dark sector. We show that intrinsic entropy perturbations can carry primordial scale dependence, and non-minimal couplings can lead to a scale-dependent suppression or enhancement of structure growth. Finally, we demonstrate that these models are generically compatible with current Cosmic Microwave Background observations, while inducing distinctive signatures in large-scale structure. The framework provides a theoretically well-motivated and observationally viable extension to the standard cosmological model, opening new directions to explore novel interactions in the dark sector.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期高精度宇宙学数据的发布，特别是ACT的小尺度宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）测量和DESI的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）数据，为探测中微子质量开辟了新前景。研究旨在利用这些最新数据集更新对中微子总质量及其质量层级的约束。

Method: 研究在ΛCDM、wCDM、全息暗能量（holographic dark energy, HDE）和w₀wₐCDM四种宇宙学模型框架下，使用最新的ACT DR6、DESI DR2和DESY5数据集进行分析，以约束中微子总质量∑m_ν及其质量层级。

Result: 研究发现∑m_ν的上限受暗能量状态方程演化行为的决定性影响：具有早期精质（early-time quintessence）特征的模型（如HDE）给出最严格的约束，而允许早期幻影（early-time phantom）行为的模型（如w₀wₐCDM）则给出显著宽松的界限。所有场景下均观察到稳健的质量层级依赖性，其中反转层级（inverted hierarchy）约束最弱，简并层级（degenerate hierarchy）约束最紧。

Conclusion: 分析表明，来自ACT的改进小尺度CMB信息与高精度BAO数据相结合，系统性地收紧了对∑m_ν的限制，为未来的中微子质量测量提供了重要基准。暗能量演化行为对中微子质量约束具有关键影响。

Abstract: The recent release of high-precision cosmological data, particularly the small-scale cosmic microwave background (CMB) measurements from ACT and baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data from DESI, has opened a new landscape for probing the neutrino mass. In this work, we present updated constraints on the total neutrino mass, $\sum m_ν$, and its hierarchy within the $Λ$CDM, $w$CDM, holographic dark energy (HDE), and $w_0w_a$CDM models, using the latest ACT DR6, DESI DR2, and DESY5 datasets. We find that the upper limits on $\sum m_ν$ are critically governed by the evolutionary behavior of the dark energy equation of state. Specifically, models exhibiting early-time quintessence features (e.g., HDE) yield the most stringent constraints, whereas those allowing for early-time phantom behavior (e.g., $w_0w_a$CDM) result in significantly looser bounds. Despite these model-dependent variations, we observe a robust hierarchy dependence across all scenarios, where the inverted hierarchy consistently yields weaker constraints and the degenerate hierarchy consistently yields tightest constraints. Our analysis demonstrates that the improved small-scale CMB information from ACT, combined with high-precision BAO data, systematically tightens the limits on $\sum m_ν$, providing a crucial benchmark for future neutrino mass measurement.

</details>


<div id='cs.CE'></div>

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [155] [An Atlas of Extreme Properties in Cubic Symmetric Metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10934)
*Sahar Choukir,Nirosh Manohara,Chandra Veer Singh*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一个基于36种立方空间群的大规模对称性引导框架，用于生成和分析三维超材料，构建了约195万个周期性单胞数据库，并开发了三维卷积神经网络代理模型来预测力学性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前三维超材料研究主要集中于传统的杆、板、壳基晶格设计，这些设计虽具优势但存在固有局限性，限制了其在某些应用中的性能，因此需要探索替代的结构拓扑。

Method: 采用基于体素（voxel-based）的表示方法，构建了涵盖36种立方空间群的周期性单胞数据库，包含约195万个设计，覆盖广泛的相对密度和拓扑复杂度。同时开发了三维卷积神经网络（3D convolutional neural network）代理模型，在全数据库上进行训练和评估。

Result: 数据库揭示了由晶体学对称性塑造的丰富弹性性能景观，包括具有高体剪切比（$K/G \approx 166$）的罕见五模（pentamode）设计、泊松比低至$ν=-0.76$的各向同性拉胀（isotropic-auxetic）结构，以及达到Hashin-Shtrikman刚度上限93%的结构。代理模型能够预测单轴、剪切和静水压力加载下的应变能密度值。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了立方对称超材料的全面图集，并提供了预训练模型，用于加速发现和设计具有极端力学性能的三维架构材料。

Abstract: Current research on three-dimensional metamaterial has largely focused on conventional strut, plate, and shell-based lattice designs. Although these designs offer several advantages, they possess inherent limitations that can restrict their performance in certain applications, motivating the exploration of alternative structural topologies. Here, we present a large-scale, symmetry guided framework for the generation and analysis of architected metamaterials based on all 36 cubic space groups. Using a voxel-based representation, we construct a database of approximately 1.95 million periodic unit cells spanning a broad range of relative densities and topological complexity. This dataset reveals a rich elastic property landscape shaped by crystallographic symmetry, including rare pentamode designs with high bulk to shear ratios such as $K/G \approx 166$ , isotropic-auxetic architectures with Poisson's ratio as low as $ν=-0.76$, and structures achieving up to 93% of the Hashin-Shtrikman upper bound on stiffness. Complementing the dataset, we develop a three-dimensional convolutional neural network surrogate model trained and evaluated on the full database to predict strain-energy density values under uniaxial, shear, and hydrostatic loading. Together, this work establishes a comprehensive atlas of cubic symmetric metamaterials and provides a pre-trained model for the accelerated discovery and design of 3D architected materials with extreme mechanical properties.

</details>
